#### 5.5.4.1.3 Code domain allocation (Cyclic Shifts)

**5.5.4.1.3.0-1**  (ID: `11461030`)

Code domain allocation (Cyclic Shifts)
The supported SRS cyclic shift are listed per baseband technology.

It indicates the allowed values for CyclicShift and BmCyclicShifts.

Additional constraints for simultaneous usage are explicitly indicated.

Note (\*):

1. Subband Beamforming only supported for Loki HW under CB009459. for Loki and Thor under CB008322
2. Precise Positioning is only supported in Thor, FR1-TDD-eCPRI-7-2a.

---

##### 5.5.4.1.3.1 Loner

**5.5.4.1.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `11461043`)

Loner
Loner HW

For Loner, cyclic shift is indicated by IE cyclicShift of srsSuMimoStruct in 5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (message UlData\_SrsReceiveReq).

Aperiodic SRS:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Frequency range | TDD | FDD |
| FR1 | [0..7] | [0..7] |
| FR2 | [0..7] |  |

Note: to avoid inter-UE interference, allocation of cyclic shifts only from subset {0,2,4,6} or from subset {1,3,5,7} shall be configured by higher layers, i.e., separation greater or equal than 2 between active cyclic shifts.

---

##### 5.5.4.1.3.2 Loki

**5.5.4.1.3.2.0-2**  (ID: `11461063`)

Loki
Loki HW

For Loki, cyclic shift is indicated by IE cyclicShift of srsSuMimo structure in 5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (message UlData\_SrsReceiveReq) for SU-MIMO. Also indicated by IE BmCyclicShifts of srsBmStruct in 5G\_L1\_IF\_250\_replaced([11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (message UlData\_SrsReceiveReq) for BM.

[CB008322-A] Also indicated by IE cyclicShift of srsBwv structure in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14860\_replaced([11514427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PbfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (message UlData\_SrsReceiveReq) for Subband Beamforming. [End CB008322-A]

[CB008322-D] cyclic shift is extended to support SRS comb4 configuration. [End CB008322-D]

Aperiodic and Periodic SRS:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Frequency range | TDD | FDD |
| FR1 | [0..7] [CB008322-D]  [0..11] [End CB008322-D] | [0..7] |
| FR2 | [0..7] |  |

Note: to avoid inter-UE interference, allocation of cyclic shifts only from subset {0,2,4,6} or from subset {1,3,5,7} for comb2, [CB008322-D] and from subset {0,3,6,9} or from subset {1,4,7,10} or from subset {2,5,8,11} for comb4 [End CB008322-D] shall be configured by higher layers, i.e., separation greater or equal than 2 for comb2 [CB008322-D]  and 3 for comb4 [End CB008322-D] between active cyclic shifts.

Due to limitations in algorithm performance: For comb2, when subband size is configured to 4 PRB, only up to 2 cyclic shifts can be allocated. Other cyclic shifts can not be used by any other UEs. if pure SRS BM UEs in the comb, up to 4 cyclic shifts can be used. [CB008322-D] For comb4, min subband size is 8 PRBs and up to 4 cyclic shifts can be allocated.  [End CB008322-D]

---

##### 5.5.4.1.3.3 Thor

**5.5.4.1.3.3.0-4**  (ID: `11461095`)

Thor
**Thor HW**

For Thor, cyclic shift is indicated by IE *cyclicShift of* srsSuMimoStruct in 5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (message UlData\_SrsReceiveReq) for SU-MIMO. Also indicated by IE *BmCyclicShifts of* srsBmStruct in 5G\_L1\_IF\_250\_replaced([11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (message UlData\_SrsReceiveReq) for BM.\*\*\*\*

Also indicated by IE *cyclicShift of* srsBwv structure in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14860\_replaced([11514427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PbfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (message UlData\_SrsReceiveReq) for Subband Beamforming.\*\*

**[CB010332-B] When SRS is used for Precise Positioning (Thor (BB), FR1-TDD-eCPRI-7-2a), that is, when *srsPosAct ([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) is True, 5G-L1-UL shall use *cyclicShift*of *srsPosReportRequest  per UE, (in* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message) for all the processes required for TOE, TOC, and Pilot Separation pertaining to each requested UE. \*\*[End CB010332-B]*****\***\*

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Frequency range | TDD | FDD |
| FR1 | [0..7] [0..11] | [0..7] |
| FR2 | [0..7] | - |

To avoid inter-UE interference, allocation of cyclic shifts only from

* subset {0,2,4, 6} or {1,3,5,7} for comb2
* subset {0,3,6,9} or {1,4,7,10}, or {2,5,8,11} for comb4

**[Before CNI-130313] [CB011117-B] - subset {0,2,4,6,8,10} or {1,3,5,7,9, 11} for comb4** [End CB011117-B] [End CNI-130313]\*\*\*\*

shall be configured by higher layers, i.e., separation greater or equal than **2 for comb2,** and 3 **[Before CNI-130313]**[CB011117-B] or 2 **[End CB011117-B] [End CNI-130313]  for comb4 between active cyclic shifts.*****\****\*

Due to limitations in algorithm performance: when the subband size is configured to 4 PRB, if there is any SRS SuMimo UE allocated in the comb, only up to 2 cyclic shifts can be allocated, other cyclic shifts can not be used by any other UEs. If pure SRS BM UEs in the comb, up to 4 cyclic shifts can be used. For comb4, min subband size is 8 PRBs and up to 4 **[Before CNI-130313] [CB011117-B] or 6** [End CB011117-B] [End***\*CNI-130313]  cyclic shifts can be allocated.*****\***

**Note:**

1. Configurationwise, some RRM functionality is dependent on FH technology, *cyclicShift>7 is currently restricted to eCPRI FH.*

**[Before CNI-130313] [CB011117-B] 2.** For comb4, 6 cyclic shifts per combId is controlled by ***rdEnable6CsForComb4* \*(5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_14085) and it is only for pSRS. 5G-L1-UL shall support both 4 or 6 CS per combId.*****\****

1. 6 CS per combId reduces the CS interval and it may degrade the SRS channel estimation performance especially when channel delay spread is large. Simulation shows that such degradation is obvious in high SINR region. Refer to below link.

<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:p:/r/sites/ATFL1Spec/_layouts/15/Doc.aspx?sourcedoc=%7B173E06D6--BCB0-D0C89ECB9D2C%7D&file=SRS%20comb4%206CS%20measurement.pptx&action=edit&mobileredirect=true>

**[End CB011117-B]** [End CNI-130313]\*\*\*\*

---

### 5.5.4.2 SRS modes

### 5.5.4.3 SRS messages

##### 5.5.4.3.1 SRS messages to/from L2-PS

###### 5.5.4.3.1.1 Receive Request for SU-MIMO

###### 5.5.4.3.1.1.1 Loner

###### 5.5.4.3.1.1.1.0-3 Loner L1-SW shall configure L1-FPGA of L1Low-RAU-CPRI to store the SRS SU-MIMO processing related data of a subcell in FPGA DDR if bufferedUlConfig indicates NRT for that subcell. See BTSC_L1_Req_369. L1-SW shall configure L1-FPGA of L1Low-RAU-CPRI and also L1-FPGA of L1High-RAU-CPRI to process the SRS SU-MIMO data at the SFN and Slot provided by bufferedUlConfig, i.e., rx_conf storage area of DDR corresponding to SFN and Slot provided by bufferedUlConfig shall be programmed to process the data in NRT at given SFN and Slot. See BTSC_L1_Req_369. (ID: 11461224)

###### 5.5.4.3.1.1.2 Loki-Thor

**5.5.4.3.1.1.2.0-3**  (ID: `13240176`)

Loki-Thor
For ulSubcellType=15 (A8):

* 5G-L1-UL(BB) shall process suSplitpanelMode in srsSuMimo structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message ([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) as follows:

For i=0..3

if suSplitpanelMode[i] is not in range {0,9,10,11,12} then UlData\_SrsReceiveReq is not valid and shall be dropped.

end For.

* Additional entries of suSplitpanelMode, suSplitpanelMode[j], j=4,...,7,  shall be ignored.

End case A8.

---

###### 5.5.4.3.1.2 Response to L2-PS for SU-MIMO for Loner

###### 5.5.4.3.1.2.1 Response message to L2-PS

**5.5.4.3.1.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11461261`)

Response message to L2-PS
L1-SW shall send a single UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message per subcell (no bundle) to 5G-L2-PS containing, for all subcells receiving SRS in the slot, in the IE bufferedUlResp, 3 new IEs,

bufferedUlResp.processInRealTime which is of type Bool, where True indicates SRS process was done in RT (i.e., same as air interface time given by SFN and Slot IEs), and False indicates SRS process was done in NRT;

bufferedUlResp.sfnForProcessing which is of type u16 [0..1023], which indicates the SFN at which SRS processing was done;

bufferedUlResp.slotForProcessing which is of type u8 [0..79], which indicates the Slot at which SRS processing was done.

SubcellId parameter shall support any value 0 through 7. subcellId is defined by 5G\_UP\_1851.

---

###### 5.5.4.3.1.2.2 T2min

###### 5.5.4.3.1.2.2.1 Below 6 GHz

###### 5.5.4.3.1.2.2.1.0-1 Below 6 GHz 5G-L1-UL below 6GHz shall increase T2min by 1 slot, the earliest UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs messages can be sent, and shall increase T2max by 3 slots, the latest UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs messages can be sent, for the subcells processed in NRT. There is no impact to the timing related to subcells which are processed in RT. (ID: 11461280)

###### 5.5.4.3.1.2.2.2 Above 6 GHz

###### 5.5.4.3.1.2.2.2.0-1 Above 6 GHz 5G-L1-UL above 6GHz shall increase T2min by 1 slot, the earliest UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs messages can be sent, and shall increase T2max by 3 slots, the latest UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs messages can be sent, for the subcells processed in NRT. There is no impact to the timing related to subcells which are processed in RT. (ID: 11461292)

###### 5.5.4.3.1.3 Response to L2-PS for Short-Term Beamforming (SRS_SBF)

###### 5.5.4.3.1.3.1 BWV calculation result report

**5.5.4.3.1.3.1.0-2**  (ID: `11461315`)

BWV calculation result report
5G-L1-UL shall send response to L2 after normalization of the beamweight vectors has finished.

The result IE in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBwvPs is filled as:

If all SRS ports (numSrsPorts) are NOT validated

then result = 1 "Failure".

Else

then result = 0 "Ok".

The numSrsPorts IE is in srsBwv structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message. Refer to 5G\_L1\_10070\_replaced([11506726](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fFbmAPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SRS port validation.

---

###### 5.5.4.3.1.3.2 Fronthaul-RU transmission delay report

###### 5.5.4.3.1.3.2.0-1 Fronthaul-RU transmission delay report 5G-L1-UL shall report Fronthaul-RU transmission delay for BWV delivery at RU in unit of slot number via fhTransDelay in 5G_L1_IF_14858_replaced( 11514505 ). Default value is 5. (ID: 11461327)

###### 5.5.4.3.1.3.3 Number of BWV(s) report

###### 5.5.4.3.1.3.3.0-1 Number of BWV(s) report 5G-L1-UL shall report the selected number of BWVs per subband to 5G-L2-PS via numBwvPerSubband in 5G_L1_IF_14858_replaced( 11514505 ), which is the output of SRS port validation. (ID: 11461337)

###### 5.5.4.3.1.3.4 EIRP report

**5.5.4.3.1.3.4.0-1**  (ID: `11461349`)

EIRP report
The computed DFT expansion coefficients for EIRP computation is reported to 5G-L2-PS via eirpCoefficients in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14858\_replaced([11514505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32ePvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in the following order:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | DFT beam index | polarization | DFT beam 0 | DFT beam 1 | … | DFT beam N-2 | DFT beam N-1 |
| numBwvPerSubband | BWV beam 0 | - | eirpCoefficients[0] | eirpCoefficients[1] | … | eirpCoefficients[N-2] | eirpCoefficients[N-1] |
| + | eirpCoefficients[N] | eirpCoefficients[N+1] |  | eirpCoefficients[2N-2] | eirpCoefficients[2N-1] |  |  |
| BWV beam 1 | - | eirpCoefficients[2N] | eirpCoefficients[2N+1] | … | eirpCoefficients[3N-2] | eirpCoefficients[3N-1] |  |
| + | eirpCoefficients[3N] | eirpCoefficients[3N+1] | … | eirpCoefficients[4N-2] | eirpCoefficients[4N-1] |  |  |
| … | … | … | … | … | … | … |  |
| BWV beam M-1 | - | eirpCoefficients[2(M-1)N] | eirpCoefficients[2(M-1)N+1] | … | eirpCoefficients[(2M-1)N-2] | eirpCoefficients[(2M-1)N-1] |  |
| + | eirpCoefficients[(2M-1)N] | eirpCoefficients[(2M-1)N+1] | … | eirpCoefficients[2MN-2] | eirpCoefficients[2MN-1] |  |  |

where M is numBwvPerSubband in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14860\_replaced([11514427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PbfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and N = numOfRowTRX  x numOfColumnTRX in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14077\_replaced([11513492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) which denotes the number of 2-D DFT beams.

---

###### 5.5.4.3.1.3.5 Port power report

**5.5.4.3.1.3.5.0-1**  (ID: `11461363`)

Port power report
5G-L1-UL shall report portPower and sinr in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14858\_replaced([11514505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32ePvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to 5G-L2-PS. The portPower IE is always filled regardless of result IE.

When srsSinrThreshold = -400 (-40 dB), since simplified sinr computation is not activated, 5G-L1-UL shall fill sinr as invalid value (-255dB).

When srsSinrThreshold > -400 (-40 dB), 5G-L1-UL shall report the computed sinr.

Also, port power of the selected SRS subband for UE-specific CSI RS beams computation is reported to 5G-L2-PS via portPowerCsiRsSubband in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14858\_replaced([11514505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32ePvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Unit is dBm and invalid value is -140dBm.

---

###### 5.5.4.3.1.3.6 TOE/TOC report

###### 5.5.4.3.1.3.6.0-1 TOE/TOC report 5G-L1-UL shall report the TOE/TOC result via timeOffset in 5G_L1_IF_14858_replaced( 11514505 ) to 5G-L2-PS. (ID: 11461376)

#### 5.5.4.3.2 SRS messages from L1-BB to L1-Radio and from L1-Radio to L1-BB

##### 5.5.4.3.2.1 SU-MIMO (SRS_SU)

###### 5.5.4.3.2.1.1 multiUeMode

###### 5.5.4.3.2.1.1-1 multiUeMode

###### 5.5.4.3.2.1.1-1.0-1 multiUeMode From L1-BB to L1-Radio (Receive Request Message) (ID: 11461419)

**5.5.4.3.2.1.1-1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12780803`)

multiUeMode
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall support the generation and fragmentation of message *UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveReq (see [11517212](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSJjSPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) from message* UlData\_SrsReceiveReq ([11514379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), when *srsSuMimoEnable=*true, using the rules described in [11517249](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSKKUfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).\*\*\*\*

Once generation and fragmentation of *UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveReq is completed, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall send the one or more fragments of* UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveReq  to 5G-L1-UL (Radio) via C-plane fronthaul interface.\*\*

[CB012115-SR-GA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW.

Note: Testing under CB012115-SR-GA only requires single fragment case.

[End CB012115-SR-GA]

---

###### 5.5.4.3.2.1.1-1.0-2 multiUeMode From L1-Radio to L1-BB (Receive Response Message) (ID: 11461438)

**5.5.4.3.2.1.1-1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12782191`)

multiUeMode
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall support the reception of one fragment, in the case of single fragment reception,  or several fragments, in the case of multi-fragment reception,  from message *UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs ([11517282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSKKWfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and creation of response message* UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs ([11514446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PcfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*

Generation of *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs from one or more fragments is as follows:*

-The common IEs in *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs are retrieved from any of the* UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs fragments common IEs*.*\*\*

-The UE dedicated IEs in *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs  are retrieved from each fragment's* srsSuMimoRuResp*structure (5G\_L1\_IF\_14988\_replaced([11517301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSKKXvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*\*\*

Once creation of *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs from* UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs is completed, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall send message to 5G-L2-PS.\*\*

[CB012115-SR-GA]

Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW.

Note: Testing under CB012115-SR-GA only requires single fragment case.

**[End CB012115-SR-GA]**

---

###### 5.5.4.3.2.1.1-2 multiUeMode

**5.5.4.3.2.1.1-2.0-2**  (ID: `12782215`)

multiUeMode
Any fragment of *UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs not reaching 5G-L1-UL (BB) within the reception window defined in ([11590319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BR5NW_wGEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is considered lost.*

For the generation of *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs response to L2, 5G-L1-UL (BB) only includes fragments (one in the case of single fragment reception or several in the case of multi-fragment reception) of* UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs message reaching 5G-L1-UL (BB) within the reception window defined in ([11590319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BR5NW_wGEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), that is, fragments not considered lost.\*\*

If all fragments are lost, 5G-L1-UL (BB) takes no action and no *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message is sent to L2-PS.*

[CB012115-SR-GA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-GA]

---

###### 5.5.4.3.2.1.1.0-2 multiUeMode [Draft for CB009527-F] MultiUeMode = mono UE, 4Cs and 6CS (ID: 11461408)

##### 5.5.4.3.2.2 Beamforming (SRS_BM)

###### 5.5.4.3.2.2.0-1 Beamforming (SRS_BM) Message Fragmentation (ID: 11461475)

**5.5.4.3.2.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11461480`)

Beamforming (SRS\_BM)
From L1-BB to L1-Radio (Receive Request Message)

---

**5.5.4.3.2.2.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11461486`)

Beamforming (SRS\_BM)
General

---

**5.5.4.3.2.2.0-1.0-1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12782245`)

Beamforming (SRS\_BM)
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall support the generation and fragmentation of *UlDataFH\_SrsBmReceiveReq message (see ([11517354](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSKxZ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) from message* UlData\_SrsReceiveReq ([11514379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), when *srsBmEnable=true, using the rules described in ([11517385](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSKxbvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*\*\*

Once generation and fragmentation of *UlDataFH\_SrsBmReceiveReq message is completed, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall send each fragment of* UlDataFH\_SrsBmReceiveReq message to 5G-L1-UL (Radio) via C-plane fronthaul interface.\*\*

**[CB012115-SR-GA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW.**[End CB012115-SR-GA]\*\*\*\*

---

**5.5.4.3.2.2.0-1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11461506`)

Beamforming (SRS\_BM)
Interworking with SRS\_RTBF

---

**5.5.4.3.2.2.0-1.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11461513`)

Beamforming (SRS\_BM)
When srsBmSubbandIdLtCoMa in srsRtBf structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq (5G\_L1\_IF\_15277\_replaced([11514438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3Pb_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is valid, 5G\_L1\_UL (BB) shall support the generation and fragmentation of message UlDataFH\_SrsBmReceiveReq (5G\_L1\_IF\_15077\_replaced([11517357](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSKxaPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to 5G\_L1\_15684\_replaced([11461480](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBBAFfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and the process of UlDataFH\_SrsBmReceiveRespPs (5G\_L1\_IF\_15083\_replaced([11517407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSLYcPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  fragment loss according to 5G\_L1\_15351\_replaced([11461536](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBBAHvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Rationale: In case of SRS\_RtBf coexists with SRS\_BM for the same UE (5G\_L1\_15526\_replaced([11507308](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fFgehfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the configurations are merged together in the same srsRtBf structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq.

---

**5.5.4.3.2.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11461519`)

Beamforming (SRS\_BM)
From L1-Radio to L1-BB (Receive Response Message)

---

**5.5.4.3.2.2.0-1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12782251`)

Beamforming (SRS\_BM)
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall support the reception of fragments from message *UlDataFH\_SrsBmReceiveRespPs ([11517404](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSKxdPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and creation of response message* UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs **([11514467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**\*\*

Generation of *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs* *message from the different fragments is as follows:*\*\*

-The common IEs in *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs are retrieved from any of the* UlDataFH\_SrsBmReceiveReq fragments common IEs*.*\*\*

-The SRS\_BM resource dedicated IEs in *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs are retrieved from each fragment's* srsBmRuResp structure ([11517429](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSLYdPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*

Once creation of *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs* *from* UlDataFH\_SrsBmReceiveRespPs is completed*, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall send message to 5G-L2-PS.*\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-SR-GA] Shall be supported in Odin L1 HW.**[End CB012115-SR-GA]\*\*\*\*

---

###### 5.5.4.3.2.2.0-2 Beamforming (SRS_BM) Fragment Loss (ID: 11461536)

**5.5.4.3.2.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12782261`)

Beamforming (SRS\_BM)
Any fragment of *UlDataFH\_SrsBmReceiveRespPs not reaching 5G-L1-UL (BB) within the reception window defined in ([11590319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BR5NW_wGEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is considered lost.*

For the generation of *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs response to L2, 5G-L1-UL (BB) only includes fragments of* UlDataFH\_SrsBmReceiveRespPs message reaching 5G-L1-UL (BB) within the reception window defined in ([11590319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BR5NW_wGEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), that is, fragments not considered lost.\*\*

If all fragments are lost, 5G-L1-UL (BB) takes no action and no *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs message is sent to L2-PS.*

**[CB012115-SR-GA] Shall be supported in Odin L1 HW.**[End CB012115-SR-GA]\*\*\*\*

---

##### 5.5.4.3.2.3 Real-Time Beamforming (SRS_RTBF)

###### 5.5.4.3.2.3.0-1 Real-Time Beamforming (SRS_RTBF) Message Fragmentation (ID: 11461556)

**5.5.4.3.2.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11461562`)

Real-Time Beamforming (SRS\_RTBF)
From L1-BB to L1-Radio (Receive Request Message)

---

**5.5.4.3.2.3.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11461569`)

Real-Time Beamforming (SRS\_RTBF)
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall support the generation and fragmentation of message UlDataFH\_SrsRtBfReceiveReq (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15281\_replaced([11517454](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSLYe_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) from message UlData\_SrsReceiveReq (5G\_L1\_IF\_241\_replaced([11514379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), when srsRtBfEnable=true, using the rules described in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15288\_replaced([11517484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSLYgvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

After generation and fragmentation of UlDataFH\_SrsRtBfReceiveReq is completed, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall send each fragment of UlDataFH\_SrsRtBfReceiveReq to 5G-L1-UL (Radio) via C-plane fronthaul interface.

Note: Under the current system constraints of CB009527(the maximum number of requests fits in a single fragment), only single fragment reception is required. Check 5G\_L1\_15672\_replaced([11507322](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fFgeifvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_IF\_15288\_replaced([11517484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSLYgvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Consequently, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall bypass fragmentation procedure and send single fragment.

---

**5.5.4.3.2.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11461575`)

Real-Time Beamforming (SRS\_RTBF)
From L1-Radio to L1-BB (Receive Response Message)

---

**5.5.4.3.2.3.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11461580`)

Real-Time Beamforming (SRS\_RTBF)
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall support the reception of one fragment, in the case of single fragment reception,  or several fragments, in the case of multi-fragment reception,  from message UlDataFH\_SrsRtBfReceiveRespPs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15282\_replaced([11517500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSL_gvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and creation of response message UlData\_SrsReceiveRespRtBfPs (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15279\_replaced([11514515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32evvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Generation of UlData\_SrsReceiveRespRtBfPs from one or more fragments is as follows:

-The common IEs in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespRtBfPs are retrieved from any of the UlDataFH\_SrsRtBfReceiveRespPs fragments common IEs.

-The UE dedicated IEs in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespRtBfPs  are retrieved from each fragment's srsRtBfRuResp structure (5G\_L1\_IF\_15295\_replaced([11517522](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSL_ivvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Once creation of UlData\_SrsReceiveRespRtBfPs from UlDataFH\_SrsRtBfReceiveRespPs is completed, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall send message to 5G-L2-PS.

---

###### 5.5.4.3.2.3.0-2 Real-Time Beamforming (SRS_RTBF) Fragment Loss (ID: 11461586)

**5.5.4.3.2.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11461592`)

Real-Time Beamforming (SRS\_RTBF)
Any fragment of UlDataFH\_SrsRtBfReceiveRespPs not reaching 5G-L1-UL (BB) within the reception window defined in BTSC\_L1\_Req\_10882\_replaced([11590316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BR5NWvwGEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is considered lost.

For the generation of UlData\_SrsReceiveRespRtBfPs response to L2, 5G-L1-UL (BB) only includes fragments of UlDataFH\_SrsRtBfReceiveRespPs message reaching 5G-L1-UL (BB) within the reception window defined in BTSC\_L1\_Req\_10882\_replaced([11590316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BR5NWvwGEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), that is, fragments not considered lost.

If all fragments are lost, 5G-L1-UL (BB) takes no action and no UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs message is sent to L2-PS.

---

###### 5.5.4.3.2.3.1 Response validation

#### 5.5.4.3.3 SRS messages validation

##### 5.5.4.3.3.1 UlData_SrsReceiveReq message validation

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.1 transmissionComb validation

**5.5.4.3.3.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `12730677`)

transmissionComb validation
~~5G-L1-DL (BB) shall validate that any *transmissionComb is equal to 2 or 4 and consistent across  any SRS type (srsSuMimo, srsBm, srsBwv) that is currently enabled in UlData\_SrsReceiveReq.*~~

~~In case *transmissionComb  is not equal to 2 or 4, or  differ for any  SRS type, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.*~~

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514383: UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message content:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_T6-DQPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.2 cyclicShift validation

**5.5.4.3.3.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `12730747`)

cyclicShift validation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that any cyclicShift  is not in range [8 .. 11] for SRS SU MIMO, if transmissionComb is equal to 2.

In case cyclicShift  is in range [8 .. 11], 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514431: srsBwv structure content:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Ucs3UPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and [11514394: Structure content reorganized and modified. Support for NDM SRS is introduced. The new design targets backward compatibility with previous platform with minimal changes.](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_UCyigPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.3 numRbgPerSubband validation

**5.5.4.3.3.1.3.0-1**  (ID: `12730753`)

numRbgPerSubband validation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that any numRbgPerSubband is not higher than floor(ulBandwidth / 4), where ulBandwidth is received in UlCell\_SetupReq

In case numRbgPerSubband higher than floor(ulBandwidth / 4), 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514394: Structure content reorganized and modified. Support for NDM SRS is introduced. The new design targets backward compatibility with previous platform with minimal changes.](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_UCyigPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.4 startPrb validation

**5.5.4.3.3.1.4.0-1**  (ID: `12730759`)

startPrb validation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that any startPrb is not higher than (ulBandwidth - 4 \* numPrbPerSubband ), where:

* ulBandwidth is received in UlCell\_SetupReq and
* numPrbPerSubband received in pSRSConfig of UlCell\_SetupReq message.

In case startPrb higher than (ulBandwidth - 4 \* numRbgPerSubband), 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514394: Structure content reorganized and modified. Support for NDM SRS is introduced. The new design targets backward compatibility with previous platform with minimal changes.](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_UCyigPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and [11514420: srsBm structure content:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_UWhW0PvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.5 transmissionCombId validation

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.5.1 Checker 1

**5.5.4.3.3.1.5.1.0-1**  (ID: `12730757`)

Checker 1
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that transmissionCombId in **srsSuMimo is not equal to 2 or 3, if transmissionComb from UlCell\_SetupReq is 2**

In case transmissionCombId is equal to 2 or 3, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514394: Structure content reorganized and modified. Support for NDM SRS is introduced. The new design targets backward compatibility with previous platform with minimal changes.](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_UCyigPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.5.2 Checker 2

**5.5.4.3.3.1.5.2.0-1**  (ID: `12733433`)

Checker 2
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that transmissionCombId in srsBwv struct is not equal to 2 or 3 , if transmissionComb from UlCell\_SetupReq is 2

In case transmissionCombId in srsBwv struct is greater than 2, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514431: srsBwv structure content:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Ucs3UPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.6 ueType validation

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.6.1 Checker 1

**5.5.4.3.3.1.6.1.0-1**  (ID: `12730756`)

Checker 1
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that ueType is not equal to 1 or 3, if UlData\_SrsReceiveReq was received for subcell with:

* *pSrsact  = false*
* *pSrsBwvAct = false*
* fronthaulMode not equal to 7-2e eCPRI

In case ueType is equal to 1 or 3 in such configuration, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514394: Structure content reorganized and modified. Support for NDM SRS is introduced. The new design targets backward compatibility with previous platform with minimal changes.](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_UCyigPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.6.2 Checker 2

**5.5.4.3.3.1.6.2.0-1**  (ID: `12730998`)

Checker 2
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that ueType is not equal to 3, if UlData\_SrsReceiveReq was received for subcell with:

* *pSrsBwvAct = false*
* fronthaulMode not equal to 7-2e eCPRI

In case ueType is equal to 3 in such configuration, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514394: Structure content reorganized and modified. Support for NDM SRS is introduced. The new design targets backward compatibility with previous platform with minimal changes.](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_UCyigPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.6.3 Checker 3

**5.5.4.3.3.1.6.3.0-1**  (ID: `12731000`)

Checker 3
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate *ueType field LSB+1 is not set, if* ueType field LSB='0'\*\*

Invalid ueType 0b10 mean short-term Beamforming SRS with aperiodic SRS and this configuration is not supported.

In case *ueType field LSB-1 is set in such configuration, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.*

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514394: Structure content reorganized and modified. Support for NDM SRS is introduced. The new design targets backward compatibility with previous platform with minimal changes.](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_UCyigPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.7 patternId validation

**5.5.4.3.3.1.7.0-1**  (ID: `12731011`)

patternId validation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that any element of patternId is not equal to 0x0000 (invalid), if ueReceiverSize is 16 (16Rx)

In case any patternId *field is equal to 0x0000 in such configuration, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.*

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514394: Structure content reorganized and modified. Support for NDM SRS is introduced. The new design targets backward compatibility with previous platform with minimal changes.](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_UCyigPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.8 ueReceiverSize validation

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.8.1 Checker 1

**5.5.4.3.3.1.8.1.0-1**  (ID: `12733082`)

Checker 1
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that ueReceiverSize is equal to 16 (16Rx) only when UlData\_SRSReceiveReq was received for for subcell in subpool that was set up with:

* fronthaulMode = 6 (eCPRI\_7\_2e)

Only eCPRI 7-2e supports 16Rx SRS SU MIMO

In case any ueReceiverSize equal to 16 (16Rx) will be received in different FH configuration, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514394: Structure content reorganized and modified. Support for NDM SRS is introduced. The new design targets backward compatibility with previous platform with minimal changes.](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_UCyigPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.8.2 Checker 2

**5.5.4.3.3.1.8.2.0-1**  (ID: `12733167`)

Checker 2
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that ueReceiverSize is not equal to 4 when UlData\_SRSReceiveReq was received for for subcell with:

* ulSubcellType = C8\_2/C8\_4/C8\_8

In case ueReceiverSize is equal to 4 for such configuration, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514394: Structure content reorganized and modified. Support for NDM SRS is introduced. The new design targets backward compatibility with previous platform with minimal changes.](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_UCyigPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.9 tranmissionCombId validation

**5.5.4.3.3.1.9.0-1**  (ID: `12733374`)

tranmissionCombId validation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that any *transmissionCombId is not greater than 1, when UlData\_SRSReceiveReq was received for for subcell with:*

* transmissionComb = 2

In case *transmissionCombId is greater than 1 for such configuration, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.*

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514420: srsBm structure content:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_UWhW0PvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.5.4.3.3.1.10 BmCyclicShift validation

**5.5.4.3.3.1.10.0-1**  (ID: `12733387`)

BmCyclicShift validation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that BmCyclicShift *is not in range [8..11], when UlData\_SRSReceiveReq was received for for subcell with:*

* transmissionComb = 2

In case BmCyclicShift *is in range [8..11] for such configuration, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.*

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514420: srsBm structure content:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_UWhW0PvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

##### 5.5.4.3.3.2 UlData_SrsReceiveRespRtBfPs validation

###### 5.5.4.3.3.2.1 rtBfCorrUeIndex validation

###### 5.5.4.3.3.2.1.1 Checker 1

**5.5.4.3.3.2.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `12733445`)

Checker 1
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that not all MSB bits 0~3 from rtBfCorrUeIndex are set to 0, when UlData\_SRSReceiveRespRtBfPs is prepared for send for subcell with:

* numOfUeCorrelation > 0

In case all MSB bits 0~3 from rtBfCorrUeIndex are set to 0 for such configuration, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the response and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514519: UlData\_SrsReceiveRespRtBfPs message content:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_VX7wgPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

###### 5.5.4.3.3.2.1.1.1 Checker 2

**5.5.4.3.3.2.1.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `12744489`)

Checker 2
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that rtBfCorrUeIndex is not equal to rtBfUeIndex, when UlData\_SRSReceiveReq was received for for subcell with:

* numOfUeCorrelation > 0

In case all rtBfCorrUeIndex is equalt to rtBfUeIndex for such configuration, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

Note: this requirement is derived form interface definition [11514519: UlData\_SrsReceiveRespRtBfPs message content:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_VX7wgPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

## 5.5.5 SRS processing

### 5.5.5.1 SRS generation

#### 5.5.5.1.1 SRS generation for Precise Positioning (SRS_POS)

**5.5.5.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `11461625`)

SRS generation for Precise Positioning (SRS\_POS)
Upon reception of UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq, 5G-L1-UL shall generate all the base sequences corresponding to unique triplets of {sequenceId, transmissionComb, numPrb} in the srsPosReportRequests array.

Rationale: The base sequence which UE is originally configured with may differ from the base sequence of the cell which is performing the Precise Positioning.

[Before CB007880-A]

Note: Only 1 attached UE shall be tested in CB010332-B, for which only 1 unique base sequence is needed. The restriction will be lifted by another feature in the same release.

[End CB007880-A]

---

### 5.5.5.2 SRS mode selection

#### 5.5.5.2.1 General

##### 5.5.5.2.1.0-2 General The following behaviour is expected for the cases of IE flags of UlData_SrsReceiveReq (see 5G_L1_IF_241_replaced( 11514379 )): srsBwvEnable=true. 5G-L1-UL shall compute Beamweight vectors per each of the subband and UE indicated in the srsBwv structure (5G_L1_IF_14860_replaced( 11514427 ))  of UlData_SrsReceiveReq  and the configuration in the pSRSBwvConfig (5G_L1_IF_14862_replaced( 11513497 )) structure of UlCell_SetupReq message. The flag can only be activated for periodic SRS when pSRSact=true. (ID: 11461649)

#### 5.5.5.2.2 SRS_BM interwork with SRS_SU and SRS_SBM

**5.5.5.2.2.0-2**  (ID: `11461669`)

SRS\_BM interwork with SRS\_SU and SRS\_SBM
The following behaviour is expected based on the following IE flags of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_241\_replaced([11514379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

- srsSuMimoEnable=true. 5G-L1-UL shall compute SU-MIMO measurements. The flag is used for both aperiodic and periodic SRS. Within a slot, either aperiodic or periodic SRS may be enabled, but not both.

- srsBmEnable=true. 5G-L1-UL shall compute and report a covariance matrix for each of the cyclic shifts, combs and subbands indicated in the Ul\_DataSrsReceiveReq message, [CB013710-A] except for the ones excluded by ignoreBm flag in srsBm structure, for which beam management process is not required, yet dummy covariance matrices shall be reported to L2PS as described in 5G\_L1\_IF\_257\_replaced([11514467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB013710-A] The flag can only be activated for periodic SRS.

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

This requirement is applicable to Thor BB.

Note: This requirement is applicable to the Loki-based board ABIN.

---

#### 5.5.5.2.3 SRS_SBF interwork with SRS_BM and SRS_BWV

**5.5.5.2.3.0-2**  (ID: `12443953`)

SRS\_SBF interwork with SRS\_BM and SRS\_BWV
5G-L1-UL supports the computation of Long Term (LT) Covariance Matrix (CoMa) for wideband beamforming via wideband TAS SRS resources configured for subband beamforming. The PRB group (as a subband) used for LT CoMa calculations is indicated by *srsBmSubbandIdLtCoMa,* startPrbLtCoMa and *numRbgLtCoMa in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14860\_replaced([11514427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PbfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*\*\*

Note:

1. In this case, 5G-L1-UL shall ingore the configurations in srsBmStrucuture in UlData\_SrsReceiveReq for current UE. The precombination beams are defined in *pSRSConfig in UlCell\_SetupReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_14077\_replaced([11513492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB014005-SR-A] or online updated in UlCell\_BeamConfigUpdateReq message ([11513613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxv3PvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_CqlKNu3yEe-rL47x_rCCmw)) [End CB014005-SR-A].* srsBmEnable = True and *srsBwvEnable = True (If only UEs with wideband TAS SRS resource are configured, then* srsBmEnable = False and *srsBwvEnable = True).*\*\*\*\*

2. UE with wideband TAS SRS resource and UE with subband SRS resouce cannot coexist in the same slot with same comb.

*numRbgLtCoMa is replaced by* numPrbPerSubband in UlCell\_SetupReq message. Refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_14077\_replaced([11513492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*

---

#### 5.5.5.2.4 SRS_SBF interwork with SRS_SU, SRS_BM and SRS_BWV

##### 5.5.5.2.4.1 Overview

**5.5.5.2.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `11461708`)

Overview
[Before CB008322-B, Before CB008322-C]

The following cases are possible when subband beamforming is activated (pSrsBwvAct=true, 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

* When IE slot in UlData\_SrsReceiveReq is a special slot:

-  srsBwvEnable=true

- srsSuMimoEnable=false.

- srsBmEnable=false.

[CB008322-B, CB008322-C]

The Subband Beamforming usage of SRS can be mixed with other SRS usages (SU-MIMO and BM) within the same slot. The following configurations are all allowed.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| srsSuMimoEnable | srsBmEnable | srsBwvEnable | First Feature |
| True | True | True | CB008322 |
| True | True | False | 5GC001086 |
| True | False | True | CB008322 |
| True | False | False | 5GC000532 |
| False | True | True | CB008322 |
| False | True | False | 5GC001086 |
| False | False | True | CB009459 |

[End CB008322-B, CB008322-C]

---

PRB(s) configuration
11461726:
PRB(s) configuration
11461726:
PRB(s) configuration
11461726:
PRB(s) configuration
11461726:
PRB(s) configuration
5G-L1-UL supports the computation of RI/PMI (SRS for SU MIMO usage) via wideband TAS SRS resources configured for subband beamforming. The PRB group (as a subband) used for SU-MIMO calculations is indicated by startPrb and numRbgPerSubband in 5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is used.

Note:

* In this case, srsSuMimoEnbale = True, srsBwvEnable = True, ueType = 3, SRSBandwidth, SRSBandwidthConfig, freqDomainPosition, and freqDomainShift are used to indicate SRS sequence for UE, startPrb andnumRbgPerSubband  are used to decide the computation size for SU MIMO measurements.
* In below example, SRSBandwidth = 0 and SRSBandwidthConfig = 63 determine the SRS pilot sequence length. freqDomainPosition = 0 and freqDomainShift =0. startPrb = 8 and numPbgPerSubband = 2 (In RBG granularity) indicates the number of PRBs that are used for SuMimo measurements. Both are needed for RI/PMI measurement via wideband TAS SS resources configured for subband beamforming.

[CB008322-G] numRbgPerSubband (in RBG granularity) is replaced by numPrbPerSubband  (in PRB granularity) in UlCell\_SetupReq message as a subcell-level configuration parameter. Refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_14077\_replaced([11513492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008322-G]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a screenshot of a spreadsheet with some annotations. The spreadsheet appears to be related to wireless communication parameters, specifically for a "periodic BWV UE" (likely a User Equipment for Bandwidth Verification).

### 5.5.5.3 SRS_BM Long-Term Beamforming: Parameter estimation in Antenna (AxC) domain

#### 5.5.5.3.1 General

**5.5.5.3.1.0-2**  (ID: `11461749`)

General
This section describes the SRS reception and Measurements when SRS is used for Beam Management (SRS\_BM) purposes. SRS for Beam Management is activated when IE pSRSact is set to true (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UlCell\_SetupReq message). SRS for Beamforming is only supported with periodic SRS. [CB013710-A] The BM processing shall be performed only for SRS BM Resources for which ignoreBm flag is False (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_250\_replaced([11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for srsBm structure). The goal is to reduce the processing load of periodic SRS in L2. The reason the request message still includes those UE's for which BM shall be ignored is that SU MIMO processing chain needs the configuration information that is only available in srsBm structure. (see 5G\_L1\_5337\_replaced([11480541](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fDXJdvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB013710-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

This requirement is applicable to Thor BB.

This requirement is ported to the Loki-based board ABIN.

---

A new SRS\_BM block is introduced for beamManagement. This block is separated from the block that carries RI and PMI computations for SU MIMO.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating two parallel processes within "L1HIGH": "SRS for BM" and "SRS for SU-MIMO". Both processes originate from an "RFU" (Radio Front-end Unit) and lead to an output labeled "L2-PS" (Layer 2 - Physical Signaling).
The "SRS for BM" process starts with "SRS spatial streams precombination per direction". This block receives input labeled "Parpolarization" and also receives "Precombinationset for horizontal direction" and "Precombinationset for vertical direction" (with a note "(SG000523 or SG00200. bee rret)"). The output of this block goes to "SRS Channel estimation". This "SRS Channel estimation" block receives input labeled "Foroydir shibcnnb-subband of horizontaldinuccion" and "Foroydir shibcranbeachhang.of". The output of "SRS Channel estimation" then feeds into "Covariance Matrix (CoMa) calculation". The output of "Covariance Matrix (CoMa) calculation" is labeled "Foroydir shibcnnb-subband of horizontaldinuccion" and "Foroydir shibcranbeachhang.of" and leads to the "L2-PS" output.
The "SRS for SU-MIMO" process starts with "UE specific SRS spatial streams precombination". This block receives input from the "RFU" and also receives "UE specific precombinationset". The output of this block goes to "SRS Channel estimation". The output of this "SRS Channel estimation" block then feeds into "SU-MIMO measurements PMI/RI". The output of "SU-MIMO measurements PMI/RI" leads to the "L2-PS" output.
The overall diagram uses blue rounded rectangles for process blocks and green arrows for data flow. The text is in a sans-serif font.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7102.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[5GC001086-A]

SRS reception for beamforming management is using the messages UlData\_SrsReceiveReq.

5G-L1-UL receives SRS signal from 64 [5GC001086-C], 32 and 16 [End 5GC001086-C] TRX via eCPRI fronthaul.

Reception of SRS signal from RU is deferred to the next DL slot in the frame in a non-delay managed fashion.

The 64 [5GC001086-C], 32 and 16 [End 5GC001086-C] spatial streams are associated with the principal subcell (C2/C4 and future subcell types) of active cell.

For the supported number of symbols, transmissionComb, cyclic shift, number of subbands, please see 5G\_L1\_3103\_replaced([11461803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBC1SvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 5GC001086-A]

[Before-CNI-122313]

[CB009444-U] This requirement is also applicable to RINLINE1 HW. [End CB009444-U]

[CNI-122313]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313]

[CB008325-5G-CA] This requirement is applicable to Thor BB [End CB008325-5G-CA]

[CB007134-B] Note:  This requirement is ported to the Loki-based board ABIN [End CB007134-B]

##### 5.5.5.3.2.3 SRS BM block overview

**5.5.5.3.2.3.0-2**  (ID: `11461810`)

SRS BM block overview
SRS\_BM block  shall support reception of:

* SRS signal from 1, 2, or 4 antenna port transmission.
* Subband SRS signal.

 [Before CB008322-G] The number of subbands is given by numSrsBmSubbands in UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message (srsBm Struct): Values [1..68] are supported. [CB008322-G] The max number of SRS BM subbands is still 68, but each SRS BM subband resource is determined by the combination of subband/comb/cyclic shift directly. No need to loop per subband per comb per cyclic shift sequentially. [End CB008322-G]

* SRS signal sent on up to 4 CS per comb. To reduce interference from different user, only one of the following CS sets shall be configured: {0, 2, 4, 6} or {1, 3, 5, 7} for comb2 [CB008322-D] {0,3,6,9}, or {1,4,7,10} or {2,5,8,11} for comb4 [End CB008322-D].
* SRS signal sent on up to [Before CB008322-D] 2 [CB008322-D] 4 [End CB008322-D] combs. Note: though comb4 is supported, but only up to 2 combs per subcell shall be configured until L1 benchmarks are ready in CB008322-G.
* 1 SRS symbol transmission (see IE srsSymbolPosition in srsBm Struct 5G\_L1\_IF\_250\_replaced([11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

SRS\_BM calculation for a given special slot is requested by setting srsBmEnable flag in UlData\_SrsReceiveReq (5G\_L1\_IF\_241\_replaced([11514379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Supported values of srsBmEnable are:

TDD:

* In FR1, {true, false} are supported. Value true is only supported in special slots.
* In FR2, only false is supported.

FDD:

* Only false is supported.
* SRS\_BM block enables CE (Channel Estimate) sub-block as described in 5G\_L1\_3100\_replaced([11461774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBC1RvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* The output of the CE sub-block is conveyed to covariance matrix sub-block as described in 5G\_L1\_3135\_replaced([11462112](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBEqevvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* 5G-L1-UL shall set the IE data for covariance matrix

---

64 TRX precombining
The SRS spatial streams received at the fronthaul of 5G-L1-UL are firstly combined using the precombining vectors, indicated in *pSRSConfig struct of UlCell\_SetupReq message [CB014005-SR-A] or online updated in UlCell\_BeamConfigUpdateReq message ([11513613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxv3PvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_CqlKNu3yEe-rL47x_rCCmw)) [End CB014005-SR-A]. The reasoning behind precombination is to reduce complexity of the following processing steps.*

Precombination in 5G-L1-UL is done separately per direction (horizontal and vertical) and polarization (-45° and +45°).

The section below, bordered in blue, contains the remaining rows of 'X' formations.
The numbers within the grid range from 0 to 63. The arrangement suggests a permutation or switching network where data inputs are routed through these diagonal connections.
Here is the data represented in a table format:

| Precombiner\_row | Column 0 | Column 1 | Column 2 | Column 3 | Column 4 | Column 5 | Column 6 | Column 7 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Precombiner\_column[3]** | 56 (red), 24 (green) | 57 (red), 25 (green) | 58 (red), 26 (green) | 59 (red), 27 (green) | 60 (red), 28 (green) | 61 (red), 29 (green) | 62 (red), 30 (green) | 63 (red), 31 (green) |
| **Precombiner\_column[2]** | 48 (red), 16 (green) | 49 (red), 17 (green) | 50 (red), 18 (green) | 51 (red), 19 (green) | 52 (red), 20 (green) | 53 (red), 21 (green) | 54 (red), 22 (green) | 55 (red), 23 (green) |
| **Precombiner\_column[1]** | 40 (red), 8 (green) | 41 (red), 9 (green) | 42 (red), 10 (green) | 43 (red), 11 (green) | 44 (red), 12 (green) | 45 (red), 13 (green) | 46 (red), 14 (green) | 47 (red), 15 (green) |
| **Precombiner\_column[0]** | 32 (red), 0 (green) | 33 (red), 1 (green) | 34 (red), 2 (green) | 35 (red), 3 (green) | 36 (red), 4 (green) | 37 (red), 5 (green) | 38 (red), 6 (green) | 39 (red), 7 (green) |

1.Horizontal precombining:

Per polarization:

Per column:

Complex-valued vector *Precombiner\_column=(*RealPartofPrecombinerColumns+j**ImagPartofPrecombinerColumns) combines SRS spatial streams in the column direction.**\*

Input: *numOfRowTRX SRS complex-valued spatial streams. Each stream contains up to 272 PRBs.*

Output: one complex-valued spatial stream containing up to 272 PRBs.

*Precombiner\_column is independently applied to all the* NumOfColumnTRX column.\*\*

1. Vertical precombining:

Per polarization:

Per row:

Complex-valued vector *Precombiner\_row=(*RealPartofPrecombinerRows+j**ImagPartofPrecombinerRows) combines SRS spatial streams in the vertical direction.**\*

Input: *numOfColumnTRX SRS complex-valued spatial streams. Each stream contains up to 272 PRBs.*

Output: one complex-valued spatial stream containing up to 272 PRBs.

*Precombiner\_row is independently applied to all the* NumOfRowTRX rows.\*\*

The following values are supported:

*numOfColumnTRX =8*

*numOfRowTRX= 4*

After precombination, there are *numOfColumnTRX spatial streams in the horizontal direction and* numOfRowTRX in the vertical direction, for a total of *numOfRowTRX+numOfColumnTRX spatial streams per polarization.*\*\*

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

---

---

##### 5.5.5.3.3.4 eAxC configuration for RFU sharing case

**5.5.5.3.3.4.0-1**  (ID: `11461893`)

eAxC configuration for RFU sharing case
In the case of RFU sharing, the mapping from eAxC ID (RRU\_Port\_ID) to localCeAxCIndex is such that localCeAxCIndex ranges from 0 to numOfColumnTRX*numOfRowTRX*2-1 following the same order as an equivalent full panel of size numOfColumnTRX*numOfRowTRX*2, i.e., elements are numebered using the left-to-right element, lowest-to-highest row, and minus45-to-plus45 polarization order, starting from lowest row and leftmost TRX of -45 polarization.

[Before-CNI-122313]

[CB009444-U] This requirement is also applicable to RINLINE1 HW. [End CB009444-U]

[CNI-122313]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313]

[CB008325-5G-CA] This requirement is applicable to Thor BB [End CB008325-5G-CA]

[CB007134-B]Note:  This requirement is ported to the Loki-based board ABIN [End CB007134-B]

---

##### 5.5.5.3.3.5 Normalization

**5.5.5.3.3.5.0-2**  (ID: `12443367`)

Normalization
After beamforming with (column vector) precombiner  **w of size *NumOfColumnTRX*NumOfRowTRX, the result must be normalised with factor: 1/sqrt(**w^H*\*w).***\*\*\*\*

Equivalently, during cell setup [CB014005-SR-A] or online updated in UlCell\_BeamConfigUpdateReq message ([11513613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxv3PvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_CqlKNu3yEe-rL47x_rCCmw)) [End CB014005-SR-A], each beam weight vector component must be divided by 1/sqrt(**w^H**w).\*\*\*\*

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

---

#### 5.5.5.3.4 Channel estimation

##### 5.5.5.3.4.1 Algorithm

**5.5.5.3.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `11461929`)

Algorithm
The channel estimation algorithm is described in the "Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification" document:

Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification.doc- <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:w:/r/sites/5gmax/_layouts/15/Doc.aspx?sourcedoc=%7BC7D041A7-9D30-43D5-9233-3FE4F70347B7%7D&file=Massive%20MIMO%20Algorithm%20Specification.docx&action=default&mobileredirect=true>

The algorithm outline is the following:

1.   5G-L1-UL shall generate SRS signal according to 3GPP document 38.211. Necessary information for signal generation is included in message

[Before CB008322-G] UlData\_SrsReceiveReq, structure srsBm: parameters sequenceId, srsBmSubbandId, transmissionCombId and BmCyclicShifts.

[CB008322-G] sequenceId and transmissionComb are moved to UlCell\_SetupReq message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15025\_replaced([11513501](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIx_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), also numPrbPerSubband that gives the size of SRS subband configuration (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14077\_replaced([11513492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB008322-G]

2. 5G-L1-UL shall compute Raw Channel Estimate for each SRS spatial stream after precombination, i.e., a total NumOfColumnTRX  x NumOfRowTRX x 2 polarizations.

3. For each SRS spatial stream, Raw Channel Estimate yields 1 channel estimate per PRB per cyclic shift/comb/subband.

4. The channel estimates of each RBG (4 PRB) are windowed and averaged to yield one channel estimate per RBG per cyclic shift/comb/subband.

The window function length is 24 for comb2 [CB008322-D] and 12 for comb4 [End CB008322-D]

---

**5.5.5.3.4.5.1.0-2**  (ID: `11461973`)

Average
(Information)

SRS\_BM shall do channel estimation for all the REs allocated for the current SRS subband/comb/cyclic shift, perform averaging per RBG level.

For each RBG within the current SRS subband/comb/cyclic shit of one polarization, the CE matrix size equals to (row) x (col).

1. If numberOfTRX (IE in UlCell\_SetupReq message 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) == 8, row = 1, col = 4.

If numberOfTRX (IE in UlCell\_SetupReq message 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) == 32 and numberOfRowTRX (IE in UlCell\_SetupReq message 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  == 2, row = 2, col = 8.
3. If numberOfTRX (IE in UlCell\_SetupReq message 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) == 32 and numberOfRowTRX (IE in UlCell\_SetupReq message 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  == 4, row = 4, col = 4.

###### 5.5.5.3.4.5.2 Structured least-squares

#### 5.5.5.3.5 Instantaneous Covariance Matrix Estimate (CoMa) calculation and procesing

##### 5.5.5.3.5.1 covariance matrix generation (Information Text)

**5.5.5.3.5.1.0-2**  (ID: `11462010`)

covariance matrix generation (Information Text)
eCPRI:

5G-L1-UL shall assume SRS reception of current slot with the assumption as below:

* If polarization in srsBm Struct (see 5G\_RAN\_UP\_23906 5G\_L1\_IF\_250\_replaced([11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is plus45, it means covariance matrix of +45pol will be processed and built.
* ElseIf polarization in srsBm Struct (5G\_RAN\_UP\_23906 5G\_L1\_IF\_250\_replaced([11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is minus45, it means covariance matrix of -45pol will be processed and built.
* If covMatrixDirection in srsBm Struct  (5G\_RAN\_UP\_23906 5G\_L1\_IF\_250\_replaced([11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is h, it means covariance matrix for vertically combined horizontal x-pols will be built for current slot.
* If covMatirxDirection in srsBm Struct  (5G\_RAN\_UP\_23906 5G\_L1\_IF\_250\_replaced([11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is v, it means covariance matrix for horizontally combined vertical x-pols will be built for current slot.

In one slot, only one direction can be processed.

1. If numberOfTRX (IE in UlCell\_SetupReq message 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) == 8, SRS\_BM gets 4 streams in only one SRS symbol from the same polarization with indicator polarization in srsBm Struct only for horizontal direction.

[5GC001086-B]

1. If numberOfTRX (IE in UlCell\_SetupReq message 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) == 16, the first 4 streams are from the same polarization with indicator polarization in srsBm Struct. The other 4 streams are from the same polarization in second SRS symbol. There are only horizontal SRS streams.

ElseIf numberOfTRX (IE in UlCell\_SetupReq message 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) == 32, The covMatrixDirection can be horizontal and vertical indicated from L2-PS.

If numberOfRowTRX (IE in UlCell\_SetupReq message 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) == 2

If covMatrixDirection == h, SRS\_BM gets the first 4 streams in first SRS symbol from the same polarization with indicator polarization in srsBm Struct. The other 4 streams in second SRS symbol are from the same polarization.

If covMatrixDirection == v, SRS\_BM gets the 2 streams in only one SRS symbol from the same polarization with indicator polarization in srsBm Struct.

ElseIf numberOfRowTRX (IE in UlCell\_SetupReq message 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) == 4

If covMatrixDirection == h, SRS\_BM gets the 4 streams in only one SRS symbol from the same polarizations.

If covMatrixDirection == v, SRS\_BM gets the 4 streams in only one SRS symbol from the same polarizations.

EndIf

ElseIf numberOfTRX (IE in UlCell\_SetupReq message 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) == 64, The covMatrixDirection can be horizontal and vertical indicated from L2-PS.

If covMatrixDirection == h, SRS\_BM gets the first 4 streams in first SRS symbol are from the same polarization with indicator polarization in srsBm Struct. The other 4 streams in second SRS symbol are from the same polarization.

If covMatrixDirection == v, SRS\_BM gets the 4 streams in only one SRS symbol are from the same polarization with indicator polarization in srsBm.

EndIf

[End 5GC001086-B]

Note:

polarization in srsBm Struct (see 5G\_RAN\_UP\_23906 5G\_L1\_IF\_250\_replaced([11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) does not exist (only in 5G\_RAN\_UP\_23906)

covMatrixDirection in srsBm Struct  (see 5G\_RAN\_UP\_23906 5G\_L1\_IF\_250\_replaced([11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) does not exist (only in 5G\_RAN\_UP\_23906)

IE in UlCell\_SetupReq message 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): numberOfTRX is sriketroughed

###### 5.5.5.3.5.2 Horizontal/Vertical CoMa calculation

**5.5.5.3.5.2.0-1**  (ID: `11462024`)

Horizontal/Vertical CoMa calculation
The covariance matrix calculation per direction is described in the "Massive MIMO algorithm Specification" document:

Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification.doc- <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:w:/r/sites/5gmax/_layouts/15/Doc.aspx?sourcedoc=%7BC7D041A7-9D30-43D5-9233-3FE4F70347B7%7D&file=Massive%20MIMO%20Algorithm%20Specification.docx&action=default&mobileredirect=true>

5G-L1-UL computes one covariance matrix per polarization, per subband, per comb and per cyclic shift.

The algorithm outline is the following:

1. 5G-L1-UL computes covariance matrix by means of outer product of vector containing channel estimates for horizontal direction with its conjugate for every RBG of every subband. Direction and polarization are computed independently.
2. 5G-L1-UL averages over each covariance matrix over the number of RBG in a subband. Average over polarization and direction is not performed in 5G-L1-UL.
3. 5G-L1-UL repeats the process for each cyclic shift/comb/subband combination in use.
4. 5G-L1-UL repeats steps 1-3 for vertical direction.
5. 5G-L1-UL repeats steps 1-4 for each polarization.

[Before-CNI-122313]

[CB009444-U] This requirement is also applicable to RINLINE1 HW. [End CB009444-U]

[CNI-122313]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313]

[CB008325-5G-CA] This requirement is applicable to Thor BB [End CB008325-5G-CA]

[CB007134-B] Note:  This requirement is ported to the Loki-based board ABIN [End CB007134-B]

---

##### 5.5.5.3.5.3 Polarization CoMa calculation

##### 5.5.5.3.5.4 Port validation

##### 5.5.5.3.5.5 Polarization averaging

#### 5.5.5.3.6 Measurements

##### 5.5.5.3.6.1 Response to L2-PS

###### 5.5.5.3.6.1.1 SRS_BM report configuration

**5.5.5.3.6.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11462065`)

SRS\_BM report configuration
Results of SRS evaluation in SRS\_BM block for beam management shall be provided in message UlData\_SrsReceiveRspBmPs  (5G\_L1\_IF\_257\_replaced([11514467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Beam Management part is described in 5G\_L1\_2208\_replaced([11506575](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fFaX4PvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Each complete BM response consists of two instances of UlData\_SrsReceiveRspBmPs, one per polarization.

5G-L1-UL shall send the following UlData\_SrsReceiveRspBmPs with the following charasteristics:

* 1 instance of UlData\_SrsReceiveRspBmPs  for IE polarization=0.
* 1 instance of UlData\_SrsReceiveRspBmPs  for IE polarization=1.

If the payload of a single instance exceeds 62 Kbytes, then fragmentation of the response message is needed. In that case, up to 2 fragments per polarization are sent. In the case of fragmentation, 5G-L1-UL shall send the following UlData\_SrsReceiveRspBmPs:

* 1 instance of UlData\_SrsReceiveRspBmPs  with polarization=0, fragmentIndex=0 and totalFragmentNum=2.
* 1 instance of UlData\_SrsReceiveRspBmPs  with polarization=0, fragmentIndex=1 and totalFragmentNum=2.
* 1 instance of UlData\_SrsReceiveRspBmPs  with polarization=1, fragmentIndex=0 and totalFragmentNum=2.
* 1 instance of UlData\_SrsReceiveRspBmPs  with polarization=1, fragmentIndex=1 and totalFragmentNum=2.

Fragmentation of the response message is indicated with totalFragmentNum=2 in UlData\_SrsReceiveRspBmPs.

[Before-CNI-122313]

[CB009444-U] This requirement is also applicable to RINLINE1 HW. [End CB009444-U]

[CNI-122313]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313]

[CB008325-5G-CA] This requirement is applicable to Thor BB [End CB008325-5G-CA]

[CB007134-B]Note:  This requirement is ported to the Loki-based board ABIN [End CB007134-B]

---

###### 5.5.5.3.6.1.2 covariance matrix report configuration

**5.5.5.3.6.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `11462087`)

covariance matrix report configuration
5G-L1-UL shall report covariance matrices to 5G-L2-PS per polarization, per subband, per comb, per cyclic shift and per direction. [Before CB008322-G] The order of reported subband/comb/cyclic shift matrices follows the same order as indicated in UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message. [CB008322-G] Each SRS BM subband resource is now determined by the combination of subband/comb/cyclic shift directly, no need to loop per subband per comb per cyclic shift sequentially. [end CB008322-G]. Each instance of UlData\_SrsReceiveRspBmPs will contain:

Covariance matrix for horizontal and covariance matrix for vertical direction for each cyclic shift, each comb and each active subband.

If total payload exceeeds 62 Kbyte, message with fragmentIndex=1 contains results for the subbands fitting within the payload limit of 62 Kbyte. Message with fragmentIndex=2 includes results for the remaining subbands.

---
