numOfRowTRX > 1
The size of data (UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs message - 5G\_L1\_IF\_257\_replaced([11514467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is dataSizebytes (UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs message - 5G\_L1\_IF\_257\_replaced([11514467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). To compute the maximum size of data:

Per subband each data structure contains the following (see data structure - 5G\_L1\_IF\_257\_replaced([11514467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

1. Header containing comb and cyclic shift.
2. Scaling for horizontal and vertical directions.
3. Covariance matrix for Horizontal and Vertical directions.

dataSizebytes=((numOfColumnTRX*(numOfColumnTRX+1)+numOfRowTRX*(numOfRowTRX+1)))*2+4)*numComb\*numSrsBmCyclicShifts

* The number of TRX columns and rows is respecitvely obtained from numOfColumnTRX and numOfRowTRX in structure pSRSConfig of UlCell\_SetupReq  (5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_IF\_14077\_replaced([11513492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* The number of combs for a subband is obtained from numComb in structure srsBm of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq (5G\_L1\_IF\_241\_replaced([11514379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_IF\_250\_replaced([11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* The number of cyclic shifts for a comb is obtained from numSrsBmCyclicShifts in structure srsBm of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq (5G\_L1\_IF\_241\_replaced([11514379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_IF\_250\_replaced([11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Note that each subband might have different number of active combs and/or cyclic\_shifts.

The largest dataSizebytes for a particular subband is when numComb=2 and numSrsBmCyclicShifts=4, which yields dataSizebytes=1504 bytes.

For each subband, data is reported using the following order and hierarchy:

> Combs (ascending order of active combs)
>
> > Cyclic shifts (ascending order of active cyclic shifts)

A generic covariance matrix of size mxm is defined as

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a matrix labeled "CovMat". The matrix is square and appears to be of size m x m. The elements of the matrix are denoted by R followed by two indices, for example, R\_{0,0}, R\_{1,0}, etc. Some elements are also denoted with a superscript asterisk, such as R^\**{1,0}. The elements are colored differently, with purple, blue, green, black, orange, and light blue colors used for different elements. The last element in the last row and last column is colored red and is denoted as R*{m-1,m-1}.
The matrix can be represented as follows:

|  | 0 | 1 | 2 | 3 | 4 | 5 | ... | m-1 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **0** | R\_{0,0} | R^\*\_{1,0} | R^\*\_{2,0} | R^\*\_{3,0} | R^\*\_{4,0} | R^\*\_{5,0} | ... | R^\*\_{m-1,0} |
| **1** | R\_{1,0} | R\_{1,1} | R^\*\_{2,1} | R^\*\_{3,1} | R^\*\_{4,1} | R^\*\_{5,1} | ... | R^\*\_{m-1,1} |
| **2** | R\_{2,0} | R\_{2,1} | R\_{2,2} | R^\*\_{3,2} | R^\*\_{4,2} | R^\*\_{5,2} | ... | R^\*\_{m-1,2} |
| **3** | R\_{3,0} | R\_{3,1} | R\_{3,2} | R\_{3,3} | R\_{4,3} | R\_{5,3} | ... | R^\*\_{m-1,3} |
| **4** | R\_{4,0} | R\_{4,1} | R\_{4,2} | R\_{4,3} | R\_{4,4} | R\_{5,4} | ... | R^\*\_{m-1,4} |
| **5** | R\_{5,0} | R\_{5,1} | R\_{5,2} | R\_{5,3} | R\_{5,4} | R\_{5,5} | ... | R^\*\_{m-1,5} |
| **...** | ... | ... | ... | ... | ... | ... | ... | ... |
| **m-1** | R\_{m-1,0} | R\_{m-1,1} | R\_{m-1,2} | R\_{m-1,3} | R\_{m-1,4} | R\_{m-1,5} | ... | R\_{m-1,m-1} |

Matrix CovMat is reported as the arrary CovarianceMatrixHorizontal/CovarianceMatrixVertical in 5G\_L1\_IF\_257\_replaced([11514467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The following mapping matrix-to-vector is used:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression enclosed in square brackets. The expression is a sequence of terms, each of the form $R\_{i,j}$, where $i$ and $j$ are indices. The terms are separated by commas and ellipses, indicating a pattern. The indices appear to follow a structured progression. The first few terms are $R\_{0,0}, R\_{1,0}, R\_{2,0}$, followed by an ellipsis and then $R\_{m-1,0}$. This suggests a row where the first index increases while the second index remains 0.
The next set of terms starts with $R\_{1,1}, R\_{2,1}, R\_{3,1}$, followed by an ellipsis and $R\_{m-1,1}$. This indicates a second row where the first index increases, and the second index is 1.
Following this, there are terms $R\_{2,2}, R\_{3,2}, R\_{4,2}$, with an ellipsis and $R\_{m-1,2}$, suggesting a third row with the second index as 2.
The expression concludes with an ellipsis and the term $R\_{m-1, m-1}$. The coloring of the terms suggests different groups or rows within the expression. The first group ($R\_{0,0}$ to $R\_{m-1,0}$) is purple. The second group ($R\_{1,1}$ to $R\_{m-1,1}$) is light blue. The third group ($R\_{2,2}$ to $R\_{m-1,2}$) is green. The final term ($R\_{m-1, m-1}$) is red.
The overall structure implies a matrix or a similar mathematical object where the indices represent rows and columns, and the expression lists elements of this structure. The use of 'm' suggests a variable dimension.
The text extracted from the image is:
[R0.0, R1.0 R2.0, Rm-1.0 R11 R2.1-R3.1 Rm-1.1 R2.2 R3.2, R4.2, Rm-1.2, Rm-1m-1][/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7150.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

In other words, the covariance matrix is reported column by column in array form, with first entry being R0,0 and last entry being Rm-1,m-1, respectively. Each entry Ri,j  is 32 bits long, consisting of respective Q(1.0.15) for real and imaginary part. Ri,j=[Q(1.0.15) real part , Q(1.0.15) imaginary part].

[Before-CNI-122313]

[CB009444-U] This requirement is also applicable to RINLINE1 HW. [End CB009444-U]

[CNI-122313]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313]

[CB008325-5G-CA] This requirement is applicable to Thor BB [End CB008325-5G-CA]

[CB007134-B] Note: This requirement is applicable to the Loki-based board ABIN [End CB007134-B]

---

###### 5.5.5.3.6.2.2 numOfRowTRX = 1

**5.5.5.3.6.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11462126`)

numOfRowTRX = 1
[PR631564]

When numOfRowTRX=1 (IE of pSRS structure, see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14077\_replaced([11513492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), CovarianceMatrixVertical is not sent to L2 (see data structure in 5G\_L1\_IF\_257\_replaced([11514467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for parameter definition), i.e., CovarianceMatrixVertical=null.

Additionally, for this case:

* scalingVertical=any value within valid range.

[End PR631564]

---

##### 5.5.5.3.6.3 Scaling factors for CoMa

**5.5.5.3.6.3.0-1**  (ID: `11462138`)

Scaling factors for CoMa
For representation purposes of the fixed point data and dynamic range adjsutment, 5G-L1-UL reports to L2 a scaling factor per direction. Scaling for horizontal direction is scalingHorizontal  and scaling for vertical direction is scalingVertical, both in Uldata\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs (5G\_L1\_IF\_257\_replaced([11514467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

scalingHorizontal and scalingVertical are defined as: the largest, in absolute value, of the dynamic scaling factors applied to each of the streams use for covariance matrxi calculation. Dynamic scaling is computed per stream, subband, comb and cyclic shift.

The non-scaled covariance matrix is restored by applying 2^(scalingHorizontal)*Ri,j for the case of horizontal direction and 2^(scalingVertical)*Ri,j for the case of vertical direction.

5G-L1-UL does not report SINR or RSSI in Uldata\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs.

[Before-CNI-122313]

[CB009444-U] This requirement is also applicable to RINLINE1 HW. [End CB009444-U]

[CNI-122313]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313]

[CB008325-5G-CA] This requirement is applicable to Thor BB [End CB008325-5G-CA]

[CB007134-B] Note:  This requirement is ported to the Loki-based board ABIN [End CB007134-B]

---

### 5.5.5.4 SRS_SBF Short-Term Beamforming: Parameter estimation in Antenna (AxC) domain

#### 5.5.5.4.1 General

**5.5.5.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `11462161`)

General
[Before CB008322-A, CB008322-F] Note: This is POC and only be valid until the next commerical features CB008322.

This section describes the SRS reception and measurements when SRS is used for Subband Beamforming (SRS\_SBF) purposes. SRS for Subband Beamforming is activated when IE pSRSBwvAct is set to true (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UlCell\_SetupReq message). SRS for Subband Beamforming is only supported with periodic SRS.

[CB008322-A, CB008322-F] This section describes the SRS reception and measurements when SRS is used for Subband Beamforming (SRS\_SBF) purposes. SRS for Subband Beamforming is activated when IE pSRSBwvAct is set to true (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UlCell\_SetupReq message). SRS for Subband Beamforming is only supported with periodic SRS.

[End CB008322-A, CB008322-F]

---

#### 5.5.5.4.2 Overview

##### 5.5.5.4.2.1 Supported Cell bandwidths for subband beamforming

###### 5.5.5.4.2.1.0-1 Supported Cell bandwidths for subband beamforming When pSRSBwvAct = true is configured, 5G-L1-UL shall support short-term subband beamforming per subband for both polarizations and all UL BWs from 10MHz to 100MHz and all frame structures. Note: Number of subbands equals ceil (M/N),  where M is cell BW in unit of PRB number and N is bwvSubbandsize in 5G_L1_IF_14862_replaced( 11513497 ).  For last subband, if the number of PRBs is less than 8, then short-term subband beamforming weight computation is skipped (5G_UP_ALG_13924_replaced( 11107540 )). In this case, beams from second last subband will be used for the last subband. Refer to CB009496 for the impact on FCP message generation. (ID: 11462178)

##### 5.5.5.4.2.2 Supported using of TAS SRS for subband beamforming

**5.5.5.4.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11462189`)

Supported using of TAS SRS for subband beamforming
When pSRSBwvAct = true is configured, 5G-L1-UL shall support short-term subband beamforming via Transmit Antenna Switching (TAS) SRS using following set:

* beamforming subband size: bwvSubbandsize in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14862\_replaced([11513497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* beam weight vector (BWV) computation method: method in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14862\_replaced([11513497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), only Minimum Mean Squared Error (MMSE) can be used.
* [Before CB008322-G] SRS port quality threshold: srsQualityThreshold in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14862\_replaced([11513497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [CB008322-G] SRS port power and SINR thresholds: srsPortPowerThreshold and srsSinrThreshold in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14862\_replaced([11513497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008322-G]

---

##### 5.5.5.4.2.3 Supported co-exist of srsBM and srsBwv

###### 5.5.5.4.2.3.0-1 Supported co-exist of srsBM and srsBwv When pSRSBwvAct = true is configured, 5G-L1-UL shall support co-exist of non RT UE with long-Term BF (srsBm) and RT UE with short-term BF (srsBwv) in the same slot. (ID: 11462202)

##### 5.5.5.4.2.4 Supported co-exist of srsSuMimo and srsBwv

###### 5.5.5.4.2.4.0-1 Supported co-exist of srsSuMimo and srsBwv When pSRSBwvAct = true is configured, 5G-L1-UL shall support co-exist of non RT UE with SU-MIMO (srsSuMimo) and RT UE with short-term BF (srsBwv) in the same slot. (ID: 11462212)

##### 5.5.5.4.2.5 Supported computation of UE sepecific CSI-RS BWV

###### 5.5.5.4.2.5.0-1 Supported computation of UE sepecific CSI-RS BWV When pSRSBwvAct = true is configured and bfSubbandId[0] is valid, 5G-L1-UL shall support computation of beam weight vector (BWV) for UE sepcific CSI-RS beams via MMSE method. (ID: 11462224)

##### 5.5.5.4.2.6 Supported validation of wideband TAS SRS signal quality

###### 5.5.5.4.2.6.0-1 Supported validation of wideband TAS SRS signal quality When pSRSBwvAct = true is configured, 5G-L1-UL shall support the validation of wideband TAS SRS signal quality and downgrade SRS ports before beam weight vector (BWV) computation if necessary. (ID: 11462235)

###### 5.5.5.4.2.7 Supported computation of BWV for 64/32 TRX

###### 5.5.5.4.2.7.0-1 Supported computation of BWV for 64/32 TRX When pSRSBwvAct = true is configured, 5G-L1-UL shall support the computation of beam weight vector (BWV) per subband for both polarizations via NDM SRS with 64 TRX [CB008322-B] and also 32 TRX [end CB008322-B]. [Before CB008322-A] Each BWV denotes a vector of size Nx1 and corresponds to only one polarization. [CB008322-A] Each BWV denotes a vector of size 2Nx1 and corresponds to both polarizations, [End CB008322-A] where N is the number of TRX per polarization. (ID: 11462250)

##### 5.5.5.4.2.8 Supported computation of SRS CE correlation

###### 5.5.5.4.2.8.0-1 Supported computation of SRS CE correlation When pSRSBwvAct = true is configured, 5G-L1-UL shall support the calculation of SRS channel estimation (CE) correlation using the middle PRB in middle subband between two SRS periods. Refer to IE correlation in 5G_L1_IF_14858_replaced( 11514505 ). Note: for definition of middle PRB and middle subband, refer to Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification document. (ID: 11462263)

##### 5.5.5.4.2.9 Supported generation of 2-D DFT beams

###### 5.5.5.4.2.9.0-1 Supported generation of 2-D DFT beams When pSRSBwvAct = true is configured, 5G-L1-UL shall support the generation of up to 64 2-D DFT beams based on values of numOfRowTRX and numOfColumnTRX in 5G_L1_IF_14077_replaced( 11513492 ). Details refer to 5G_UP_ALG_21903_replaced( 11094630 ). (ID: 11462276)

##### 5.5.5.4.2.10 Supported broken antenna handling

###### 5.5.5.4.2.10.0-1 Supported broken antenna handling When pSRSBwvAct = true is configured, 5G-L1-UL shall support broken antenna handling during SRS channel estimation using brokenAntBitmask from UlData_SrsReceiveReq message (5G_L1_IF_241_replaced( 11514379 )). (ID: 11462287)

##### 5.5.5.4.2.11 Supported computation of DFT expansion coefficients

**5.5.5.4.2.11.0-1**  (ID: `11462299`)

Supported computation of DFT expansion coefficients
When pSRSBwvAct = true is configured and [Before CB008322-G] bfSubbandId[2] [CB008322-G]  bfSubbandId[1] [End CB008322-G] is valid, 5G-L1-UL shall support DFT expansion coefficients computation using following set:

* 2-D DFT beams generated during cell setup
* Short term subband BWVs that correspond to  [Before CB008322-G] bfSubbandId[2] [CB008322-G]  bfSubbandId[1] [End CB008322-G]
* number of BWVs per subband

---

##### 5.5.5.4.2.12 Supported computation of SRS port power

**5.5.5.4.2.12.0-1**  (ID: `11462311`)

Supported computation of SRS port power
To verify the SRS port quality, 5G-L1-UL shall enable the the computation of SRS port power [CB008322-G] regardless of srsSinrThreshold value [End CB008322-G].

[CB008322-G]

In additional, 5G-L1-UL shall also enable the computation of simplified SINR depending on the configured srsSinrThreshold

When srsSinrThreshold = -400 (corresponds to -40 dB), the port power is computed by averaging all TRX (following the legacy case).

When srsSinrThreshold > -400 (corresponds to -40 dB), the port power is calculated based on only the strongest TRX. And since the simplified SINR is deduced from power and interference using the strongest TRX, port power is the intermediate result of simplified SINR computation.

[End CB008322-G]

---

##### 5.5.5.4.2.13 Supported detection of beamforming subband interference

###### 5.5.5.4.2.13.0-1 Supported detection of beamforming subband interference When pSRSBwvAct = true and rdSubbandInterferDetFlag = 1: enabled (5G_L1_19496_replaced( 11465387 )), 5G-L1-UL shall support the detection of beamforming subband interference to obtain beamforming weight vector (BWV) without interference for each subband (or bypass the BWV computation if interference ratio is too high). (ID: 11462322)

##### 5.5.5.4.2.14 Supported new subcell level parameters for SRS

**5.5.5.4.2.14.0-1**  (ID: `11462335`)

Supported new subcell level parameters for SRS
Below parameters are moved to UlCell\_SetupReq message as subcell level SRS configuiration parameters:

* transmissionComb: number of combs. Refer to SRSConfig in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15025\_replaced([11513501](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIx_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* sequenceId: SRS sequence identity. Refer to SRSConfig in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15025\_replaced([11513501](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIx_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* numPrbPerWideband: number of PRBs for wideband SRS resource. Refer to pSRSBwvConfig in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14862\_replaced([11513497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [Before CB008322-G] known as numRbgPerSubband in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14860\_replaced([11514427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PbfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008322-G]
* numPrbPerSubband: number of PRBs for subband SRS resource. Refer to pSRSConfig in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14077\_replaced([11513492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [Before CB008322-G] known as numRbgPerSubband in 5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and numRbgLtCoMa in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14860\_replaced([11514427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PbfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[End CB008322-G]

---

##### 5.5.5.4.2.15 Supported mintain ping-pong scheme for BWV UE

###### 5.5.5.4.2.15.0-1 Supported mintain ping-pong scheme for BWV UE On receiving the two startPatternIds for ping and pong for the same BWV UE from UlData_SrsReceiveReq, 5G-L1-UL shall maintain the ping-pong scheme by switching startPatternId everytime BWV computation is successfully conducted (result = 0 in UlData_SrsReceiveRespBwvPs). (ID: 11462347)

11462380:
subband beamforming calculation procedure
11462380:
subband beamforming calculation procedure
11462380:
subband beamforming calculation procedure
11462380:
subband beamforming calculation procedure
The procedure for subband beamforming calculation is the following:

1. Reception of NDM SRS at L1 High. Same NDM SRS Configuration as legacy. Data is stored in SMEM after EDEC processing.
2. SRS Channel estimate per cyclic shift/SRS port. Channel estimates are stored in memory (SMEM and/or IOMEM).
3. When antenna switching is configured, depending on the UE configuration (1t1r, 1t2r, 1t4r, 2t2r, 2t4r, 4t4r, 1t4r-2t4r), one or several SRS symbols (up to 4) are needed for Channel Estimate of all SRS ports/cyclic shifts of an UE.
4. SRS port validation by comparing [Before CB008322-G] the SRS port power with threshold that is indicated by srsQualityThreshold (5G\_L1\_IF\_14862\_replaced([11513497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB008322-G] the SRS port power and SINR (when available) with thresholds that are indicated by srsPortPowerThreshold and srsSinrThreshold (5G\_L1\_IF\_14862\_replaced([11513497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008322-G] .
5. When all SRS ports are sounded ( IE operation = Calculate is activated in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14860\_replaced([11514427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PbfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB008322-G] and subband interference detection is conducted for each valid SRS port [End CB008322-G], Beam Computer calculates (using MMSE method) a designated number of beams per subband.
6. When Beam Computer has finished, stores beamweight vectors in memory (SMEM) and triggers the creation of the L2PS response.
7. L1 SW FH fetches the beamweight vectors from memory after computation window is closed and proceeds for download of beamweight vectors to radio unit.

Note: step 7 is taken care by CB009496.

The following raw memory requirements (implementation: due to order of processing, certain memory areas might be reused and alleviate raw memory requirements):

Dimension #A (NDM SRS from RU): 2 (polarizations) xnumOfRowTRX x numOfColumnTRX x [Before CB008322-G] numRbgPerSubband x 4 [CB008322-G] numPrbPerWideband [End CB008322-G] x 12 I/Q samples per SRS symbol.

Dimension #B (Channel Estimates for SRS ports): 2 (polarizations) x numOfRowTRX x numOfColumnTRX x numSrsPorts x ( [Before CB008322-G] numRbgPerSubband x 4 [CB008322-G] numPrbPerWideband [End CB008322-G])/bwvSubbandSize complex samples per UE.

Dimension #C (validation of SRS ports for MMSE precoder): 2 (polarizations) x numOfRowTRX x numOfColumnTRX x numOfUsedSRSports x ([Before CB008322-G] numRbgPerSubband x 4 [CB008322-G] numPrbPerWideband [End CB008322-G])/bwvSubbandSize  complex sampes per UE.

Dimension #D (Subband MMSE precoder): 2 (polarizations) x numOfRowTRX x numOfColumnTRX x numOfUsedSRSports x ( [Before CB008322-G] numRbgPerSubband x 4 [CB008322-G] numPrbPerWideband [End CB008322-G])/bwvSubbandSize complex samples per UE.

##### 5.5.5.4.3.2 subband beamforming configuration

**5.5.5.4.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `11462393`)

subband beamforming configuration
The following configuration is supported for subband beamforming:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | CB009459-A | CB009459-B | CB009459-C |
| Antenna Panel |  |  |  |
| Number of Rows | 4 | 4 | 4 |
| Number of Columns | 8 | 8 | 8 |
| Number of Polarizations | 2 | 2 | 2 |
| Cell configuration |  |  |  |
| Number of cells per L1 instance | 1 | 1 | 1 |
| Cells BW | 273 PRB | 273 PRB | 273 PRB |
| Number of UEs per cell | 1 | 2 | 1 |
| Frame Structure | 5GC001116 | 5GC001116 | 5GC001116 |
| SRS configuration |  |  |  |
| Number of SRS RBG (4 PRBs) | 68 (272 PRB) | 68 (272 PRB) | 68 (272 PRB) |
| Number of SRS symbols per special slot | 1 | 1, 2 | 1, 2 |
| Antenna Ports per SRS symbol per UE | 1,2,4 | 1, 2, 4 | 1, 2, 4 |
| Subband BF configuration |  |  |  |
| Subband size (PRB) | 272, 32, 16, 8, 4, 2 | 272, 32, 16, 8, 4, 2 | 272, 32, 16, 8, 4, 2 |
| Number of Subbands per UE | 1, 8, 17, 34, 68, 136 | 1, 8, 17, 34, 68, 136 | 1, 8, 17, 34, 68, 136 |
| Method | MMSE | MMSE | FEBF |
| Channel Estimate Method | subband midPRB | Average of subband PRBs and subband midPRB | Average of subband PRBs and subband midPRB |
| Number of Full-dimension beamweight vectors (per UE per SRS period) | {1,2,3,4}\*Number of Subbands per UE | {1,2,3,4}\*Number of Subbands per UE | {1,2,3,4}\*Number of Subbands per UE |

[CNI-99771] Note: FEBF is not supported from E2E perspective. But, SW codes for this requirement still need to be inherited with deactivation. [End CNI-99771]

##### 5.5.5.4.3.3 NDM SRS configuration for subband beamforming

###### 5.5.5.4.3.3.0-2 NDM SRS configuration for subband beamforming SRS for Subband Beamforming uses the same NDM SRS configuration as decribed in 5G_L1_9865_replaced( 11506879 ). (ID: 11462417)

##### 5.5.5.4.3.4 new subcell level IEs introduction

**5.5.5.4.3.4.0-1**  (ID: `11462430`)

new subcell level IEs introduction
5G-L1-UL shall support the following new IF at UlCell\_SetupReq (5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

- numOfUlBlankedPrbs : Indicates the number of UL blanked PRBs [0,268], The value 0 is for disabling the feature, this parameter shall be taken into account for periodic wideband SRS configuration (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_11077) and for the short-term beamforming subband

(5G\_UP\_ALG\_13924\_replaced([11107540](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kog6QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- numOfUlBlankedPrbsLowEdge : Indicates the number of UL blanked PRBs on the low edge (starting from PRB 0)

PS : The total number of blanked PRBs should be mentioned on numOfUlBlankedPrbs (numOfUlBlankedPrbsLowEdge + High edge)

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
|  | Thor |
| FR1-TDD-CPRI | [CB009915-C] Supported [End CB009915-C] |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | [CB010414-AB] Supported [End CB010414-AB] |

When numOfUlBlankedPrbs ≠ 0, startPrb of srsBwv structure shall be equal to numOfUlBlankedPrbsLowEdge.

[PR786168] If PRB blanking is enabled (parameter numOfBlankedPrbs in message UlCell\_SetupReq is not 0), 5G-L1-UL shall adjust the value of parameter startPrb received from L1/L2 interface relatively to the number of blanked PRBs at lower edge of the cell bandwidth (IE numOfUlBlankedPrbsLowEdge of message UlCell\_SetupReq):

startPrbL1 = startPrbL2 - UlCellSetupReq.numOfUlBlankedPrbsLowEdge

where startPrbL2 is the value of the starting PRB received from L1/L2 interface:

* srsSuMimo.startPrb (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in case of periodic SRS for SU-MIMO (applicable only if ueType is not 0).
* srsBm.startPrb (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_250\_replaced([11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in case of SRS for beam management.
* srsBvw.startPrb (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14860\_replaced([11514427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PbfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in case of sub-band beamforming.

[End PR786168]

###### 5.5.5.4.3.5.2 Supports number of Ul blanked PRB(s) &gt;0

###### 5.5.5.4.3.5.2.0-1 Supports number of Ul blanked PRB(s) &gt;0 5G-L1-UL shall indicates in case of numOfUlBlankedPrbs &gt; 0 (UL blanked PRB enabled CB009915) to avoid the issue of checking the subband size and cell bandwidth, even if the subband size matchs the value in this list {24,28,76,104,132,160,184,216,240,272} it doesn't mean full bandwidth (ID: 11462465)

BWV computation procedure

The boxes and their text content are as follows:
1. **Raw NDM SRS IQ data from RFU** (Orange box)
2. **Channel Estimation** (Light blue box)
3. **SRS port validation** (Light blue box)
4. **BF subband interference detection** (Light blue box)
5. **BW computation (MMSE)** (Light blue box)
6. **Send L2PS response message** (Light green box)
7. **Send RFU BWs** (Light green box)

Finally, there are two output paths: "Send L2PS response message" and "Send RFU BWs". The arrows indicate a sequential progression from left to right, with the last step branching into two outputs.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7207.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

#### 5.5.5.4.4 Channel estimate

##### 5.5.5.4.4.1 Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification

**5.5.5.4.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `11462507`)

Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification
The Channel Estimate algorithm for Subband Beamforming is described at:

Section: 4.1

Document Name: Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification

Document Version (for reference): 3.4.0

Link to Latest Version:

<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:w:/r/sites/5gmax/_layouts/15/Doc.aspx?sourcedoc=%7BC7D041A7-9D30-43D5-9233-3FE4F70347B7%7D&file=Massive%20MIMO%20Algorithm%20Specification.docx&action=default&mobileredirect=true>

---

##### 5.5.5.4.4.2 Channel Estimate procedure

**5.5.5.4.4.2.0-2**  (ID: `11462528`)

Channel Estimate procedure
The Channel Estimate procedure consists of the following steps:

- RAW Channel Estimate, described in Section 4.1.1.1.

- PRBs downsampling, described in Section 5.1.2.2

- Group Partition, described in Section 4.1.1.4.

- Pilot Separation algorithm, described in Section 4.1.1.5.

See 5G\_L1\_13192\_replaced([11462507](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBHGu_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Document Location.

---

##### 5.5.5.4.4.3 Complex numbers for a Channel Estimate

###### 5.5.5.4.4.3.0-2 Complex numbers for a Channel Estimate The Channel Estimate algorithm produces, per subband, an estimate consisiting of 2 x numOfRowTRX x NumOfColumnTRX x numSrsPorts  complex numbers. (ID: 11462545)

##### 5.5.5.4.4.4 MidPRB method

###### 5.5.5.4.4.4.0-2 MidPRB method When rdDownSampleSrsForBf=1, midPRB method is deactivated and all the PRB of each subband are used for channel estimation. See Section 5.1.2.2 of the Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification (5G_L1_10071_replaced( 11462500 )). (ID: 11462565)

##### 5.5.5.4.4.5 PRBs downsampling

###### 5.5.5.4.4.5.0-1 PRBs downsampling PRBs downsampling is activated when rdDownSampleSrsForBf = 0, and middle PRB of each subband is selected for channle estimation. The definition of middle PRB can be found in Section 5.1.2.2 of the Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification (5G_L1_13192_replaced( 11462507 )). (ID: 11462577)

##### 5.5.5.4.4.6 group partition

###### 5.5.5.4.4.6.0-1 group partition For group partition, a set of PRBs which are centered on the selected SRS PRB (middle PRB) with 24 consecutive SRS REs for comb2 and  [CB008322-D] comb4 [End CB008322-D] for each subband. Refer to Section 4.1.1.4 of  the Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification (5G_L1_13192_replaced( 11462507 )). (ID: 11462588)

##### 5.5.5.4.4.7 Separation of different cyclic shifts

###### 5.5.5.4.4.7.0-2 Separation of different cyclic shifts The separation of different cyclic shifts is done by means of the window method described on Section 4.1.1.5 of the Massive MIMO Algorithm Specificatin (5G_L1_13192_replaced( 11462507 )). The window function length is 24 for comb2 [CB008322-D] and comb4 [End CB008322-D]. (ID: 11462607)

##### 5.5.5.4.4.8 Broken antennas handling

###### 5.5.5.4.4.8.0-1 Broken antennas handling For n-th (n=1...N) TRX, if the corresponding bit of brokenAntBitmask is 1, the n-th column of channel estimation results Hs of size P x N should be set to 0, where s is the subband index, P is the SRS port number and N is the TRX number. (ID: 11462620)

##### 5.5.5.4.4.9 Time offset compensation

**5.5.5.4.4.9.0-4**  (ID: `11462651`)

Time offset compensation
Time offset estimation (TOE) and Time offset compensation (TOC) are both active when rdSrsCeToEnabledFlag = 1 (5G\_L1\_14428\_replaced([11414569](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-HdEPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

* TOE is conducted based on the average of raw channel estimates over all SRS ports and TRX. The used beam weight for TOE is defined in pSRSConfig in UlCell\_SetupReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_14077\_replaced([11513492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Refer to Massive MIMO algorithm Specification section 4.1.1.2.
* TOC is performed as described in Massive MIMO algorithm Specification section 4.1.1.3.

---

##### 5.5.5.4.4.10 Raw channel estimation

##### 5.5.5.4.4.11 Port separation

##### 5.5.5.4.4.12 Channel estimate post-processing

###### 5.5.5.4.4.12.1 Structured least-squares

###### 5.5.5.4.4.12.2 Windowing

#### 5.5.5.4.5 Subband averaging

#### 5.5.5.4.6 Port validation

##### 5.5.5.4.6.1 Overview

**5.5.5.4.6.1.0-2**  (ID: `11462708`)

Overview
After Channel Estimate of all SRS ports, 5G-L1-UL needs to:

- Sort SRS ports according their power (Channel norm).

- Validate SRS port against a minimal threshold.

When the number of beamwieght vector per subband is lower than the number of SRS ports (low rank transmission), then some of the validated SRS ports are selected for the Beam Computer.

[Before CB008322-A, CB008322-F] The port selection criterion is described in 5.1.2.2.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification

[CB008322-A, CB008322-F] Depending on the rdparameter rdRtBwvDowngradeMethod (5G\_UP\_ALG\_20551\_replaced([11110305](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpCeuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), SRS port validation has different options. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13935\_replaced([11107463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kofsJfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008322-A, CB008322-F]

[CB008322-G] Simplified SINR estimation is also introduced for SRS port validation. [End CB008322-G]

---

**5.5.5.4.6.2.0-2**  (ID: `11462784`)

SRS port power calculation
For each SRS port, power is calculated according to method described in 5.1.2.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification (5G\_L1\_13192\_replaced([11462507](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBHGu_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and normalized per subcarrier and TRX as

$\overline{P\_p} = P\_p \* K\_{TC} / (12 \* M\_{SRS} \* N\_{RX})$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7247.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

where [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "MSRS" in a stylized font. The letters are colored with a gradient effect, transitioning from orange to yellow to blue. The background is black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7247.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] is the number of PRBs allocated to SRS, [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "N TRX" with a chromatic aberration effect, giving the letters a slightly blurred and colorful appearance. The letters are in a sans-serif font.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7247.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is the number of TRX.

The RMS power value for SRS port [image-3][image\_desc]The image is a close-up, blurry, and abstract depiction of what appears to be a person's face. ##### 5.5.5.4.6.3 SINR calculation

###### 5.5.5.4.6.3.0-1 SINR calculation When srsSinrThreshold  (5G_L1_IF_14862_replaced( 11513497 )) &gt; -400 (-40 dB), 5G-L1-UL shall compute simplified SINR using the strongest TRX. Details can be found in Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification section 4.1.1.6. (ID: 11462793)

The flowchart uses a combination of rectangular boxes for process steps and diamond shapes for decision points. Here's a breakdown of the flowchart: Inputs: 1. SRS Raw channel estimation from L1 2. srsSinr Threshold, srsPort Power Threshold from L3 3. numBwPerSubband from L2 4. rdTrBwDowngradevlet hod Process Flow: * The process starts with a decision point: "srsSinr Threshold &gt; 400?". * If Yes: * "SRSport power computation (sorted)" is performed. * Then, a decision point: "Averaged power &lt; srsPort Power Threshold?". * If Yes: "R = 0, bypass BWV computation". * If No: "R = min {valid SRSport, numBwPerSubband}". * Following this, there's a branching based on "rdRtBwDowngradevlet hod": * If rdRtBwDowngradevlet hod = 0 : "Remove SRS port if power &lt; srsPort Power Threshold". * If rdRtBwDowngradevlet hod = 1 : "First numBwPerSubband SRSports are selected". * If rdRtBwDowngradevlet hod = 2/3/4 : "First rdRtBwDowngradevlet ho d SRS ports are selected". * Finally, if the condition rdRtBwDowngradevlet hod is not 0, the output is "R = numBwPerSubband or rdRtBwDowngradevlet ho d". * If No: * "SRSport power and simplified SINR computation (sorted)" is performed. * Then, a decision point: "Averaged power &lt; srsPort Power Threshold or average sinr &lt; ersSinr Threshold 2?". * If Yes: "R = 0, bypass BVW computation". * If No: "R = min {valid SRSport, numBwPerSubband}". * Following this, there's a branching based on "rdRtBwDowngradevlet hod": * If rdRtBwDowngradevlet hod = 0 : "Remove SRSport if power &lt; srsPort Power Threshold or sinr &lt; srsSinr Threshold". * If rdRtBwDowngradevlet hod = 1 : "First numBwPerSubband SRSports are selected". * If rdRtBwDowngradevlet hod = 2/3/4 : "First rdRtBwDowngradevlet ho d SRS ports are selected". * Finally, if the condition rdRtBwDowngradevlet hod is not 0, the output is "R = numBwPerSubband or rdRtBwDowngradevlet ho d".[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_7252.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] [End CB008322-G] Note: SRS ports selection threshold is given by [Before CB008322-G] [Before CB008322-A] rdparameter rdSrsPowerValidThresh [CB008322-A] srsQualityThreshold in 5G_L1_IF_14862_replaced( 11513497 ). [End CB008322-A] [CB008322-G] srsPortPowerThreshold and srsSinrThreshold in 5G_L1_IF_14862_replaced( 11513497 ). [End CB008322-G] (ID: 11462814)

#### 5.5.5.4.7 Subband interference detection

##### 5.5.5.4.7.1 Overview

**5.5.5.4.7.1.0-1**  (ID: `11462828`)

Overview
This section describes the procedures of beamforming (BF) subband interference detection. The output will be used to replace beamforming weight vector (BWV) of interfered subband or totally bypass the BWV computation of the configured wideband SRS resources. The main steps are:

1. Selection of two pairs of TRXs (both polarizations per pair)

2. Detection of interference BF subband for each SRS symbol and comb with wideband SRS resource

3. Generation of interference BF subband bitmap and map it to each UE

4. Computation of interference BF subband ratio and Non interfered BWV generation.

An example is given in  <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Forms/Tree_View.aspx?csf=1&web=1&e=V8&id=%2Fsites%2F5Gdoc%2FAS%5FTech%5FSpec%2FDrawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G%2FUser%20Plane%2F5G%20UP%20Algorithms%2F2%20L1%20Algorithms%20and%20Configurations%2FUL%20%2D%20SRS%20Reception&viewid=967508b3%2D8e81%2D461c%2Db99d%2D145065cf0c1c>

For more details, refer to requirements below and/or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23228\_replaced([11107431](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kofFG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 5.5.5.4.7.2 TRX selection

**5.5.5.4.7.2.0-1**  (ID: `11462839`)

TRX selection
Depending on NTRX (number of TRXs) and SFN, the indices of 4 selected TRXs for subband interference detection are {i, i+ NTRX/2, j, j+ NTRX/2}, where i = Mod(SFN, NTRX/4) and j = Mod(i+4, NTRX/4) +  NTRX/4. If any of the selected TRX is broken, then let SFN = SFN + 1 and retry the selection procedure until all 4 TRXs are valid.

Below are the examples of TRX selection result for NTRX = 64/32/16 and i = 0..NTRX/4-1.

NTRX = 64

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1st Trx | 2nd Trx | 3rd Trx | 4th Trx |
| 0 | 32 | 20 | 52 |
| 1 | 33 | 21 | 53 |
| 2 | 34 | 22 | 54 |
| 3 | 35 | 23 | 55 |
| 4 | 36 | 24 | 56 |
| 5 | 37 | 25 | 57 |
| 6 | 38 | 26 | 58 |
| 7 | 39 | 27 | 59 |
| 8 | 40 | 28 | 60 |
| 9 | 41 | 29 | 61 |
| 10 | 42 | 30 | 62 |
| 11 | 43 | 31 | 63 |
| 12 | 44 | 16 | 48 |
| 13 | 45 | 17 | 49 |
| 14 | 46 | 18 | 50 |
| 15 | 47 | 19 | 51 |

NTRX = 32

| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1st Trx | 2nd Trx | 3rd Trx | 4th Trx |
| 0 | 16 | 12 | 28 |
| 1 | 17 | 13 | 29 |
| 2 | 18 | 14 | 30 |

detection 11462858: Interference detection 11462858: Interference detection 11462858: Interference detection 11462858: Interference detection To detect the interference BF subband, for each SRS symbol and comb, 5G-L1-UL shall 1. For subband n=1.. N subband, compute the SRS IQ [Before PR852969] linear power P IQ,n, which is the linear average of the signal power of the middle 24 subcarriers for all 4  selected TRXs [End PR852969] [PR852969] power in dBm, P IQ,n (dB)=10log10( P IQ,n), where P IQ,n is the average of the signal power over the middle 24 subcarriers for all 4 selected TRXs. [End PR852969]. * 2.[Before PR852969] Average P IQ,n to obtain [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $\overline{P} {IQ} = \sum {n} P_{IQ,n} / N_{subband}$ The equation represents the average power of the IQ signal, which is calculated by summing the power of the IQ signal in each subband and then dividing by the total number of subbands.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_7259.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] [End PR852969][PR852969] Average P IQ,n (dB) to obtain P IQ,ave=(1/Nsubband)Σn P*IQ,n(dB)[End PR852969]. * 3. For subband n=1.. N subband,  compute [Before PR852969] IQSpike_n = 10 log10( P IQ,n / [image-1][image_desc]The image contains a close-up of a mathematical expression. The expression shows the letter "P" with a horizontal line above it, indicating a vector or a mean. To the right of the "P", there is a subscript "i" followed by a subscript "Q". The "i" and "Q" are small and positioned below and to the right of the "P". The overall appearance suggests a mathematical notation, possibly from a physics or statistics context.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_7259.002.png[/image_path][/image-1]) [End PR852969] [PR852969] IQSpiken=P IQ,n (dB)- P IQ,ave [End PR852969] * 4. If IQSpiken &lt; rdIQSpikeTshForNonInterfer (5G_UP_ALG_23844_replaced( 11110420 )), then current BF subband is considered to have no interference. 5. Average IQSpiken of all subbands that have no interference to obtain AveIqSpikeOfNonInterfer [PR852969] ,i.e., AveIqSpikeOfNonInterfer =(1/Ksubband)Σk P IQ,n (dB), where k=1,...,Ksubband and Ksubband is the number of non-interference subbands from step 4.[End PR852969] * 6. For all BF subbands, [Before PR852969] if IQSpike _n &gt; rdIQSPikeTshForInterfer (5G_UP_ALG_23233_replaced( 11110409 )) + AveIqSpikeOfNonInterfer, [PR852969] if P IQ,n (dB)- AveIqSpikeOfNonInterfer&gt;rdIQSPikeTshForInterfer ( 11110409 ) [End PR852969] then current BF subband is considered to be interfered. * Note: see section 4.1.1.7 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification ( 12708616 ) for more  details. Note: to prevent undefined quantities, 5G-L1-UL (BB) may limit minimum P*IQ,n power prior to logarithm operation in step 1. Fixed-point algorithm specification to cover protection mechanism, see 12804176 . (ID: 11462858)

Interference BF subband bitmap generation
To generate the interference BF subband bitmap which has the length of Nsubband, the interfered subbands are marked as 1 and the rest subbands are filled with 0. The generated bitmap shall be mappted to each UE each port after channel estimation.

Below is the bitmap example of an UE that has 4 valid SRS ports and 8 BF subbands.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a grid of colored cells, each containing a binary digit. The grid is arranged in four rows and eight columns. The cells are colored either red or blue.
The first row contains two red cells with the digit '1', followed by six blue cells with the digit '0'.
The second row starts with a red cell containing '1', followed by a blue cell with '0', then two blue cells with '0', a red cell with '1', a blue cell with '0', a blue cell with '1', and a blue cell with '0'.
The third row begins with a blue cell containing '0', followed by a red cell with '1', then a blue cell with '0', a blue cell with '0', a red cell with '1', and finally three blue cells with '0'.
The fourth row consists of six blue cells with '0', followed by a red cell with '1', and a blue cell with '0'.
There are also two colored blocks at the top left of the image, one red and one blue, which appear to be legend indicators.
The table can be represented as follows:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1 (red) | 1 (red) | 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) |
| 1 (red) | 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) | 1 (red) | 0 (blue) | 1 (red) | 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) |
| 0 (blue) | 1 (red) | 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) | 1 (red) | 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) |
| 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) | 1 (red) | 0 (blue) | 0 (blue) |

---

##### 5.5.5.4.7.5 Interference threshold

**5.5.5.4.7.5.0-1**  (ID: `11462881`)

Interference threshold
For each UE, the interference BF subband ratio is computed by M/(Nsubband \* R), where M is the number of all interference BF subbands (i.e., sum of bitmaps), Nsubband is the number of BF subbands, and R is the number of valid SRS ports.

If interference BF subband > rdRatioTshOfInterferSb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23234\_replaced([11110429](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpET6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

5G-L1-UL shall bypass the BWV computation for current UE and report failure to 5G-L2-PS

Else

The BWV of interferene BF subband (bitmap = 1) shall be replaced by that of the closest non-interfered BF subband

End

Note: 1. For definition of closest subband, refer to 5gmax algorithm specification document.

Example:

For UE 0, Nsubband  = 8 and R = 4, the 4 bitmaps are

1100 0000 port0

1001 0100 port1

0100 1000 port2

0000 0010 port3

The interference BF subband ratio is 8/(8\*4) = 0.25, which is smaller than rdRatioTshOfInterferSb. BWV computation is required. For port0, the first two BF subband shall copy the computed BWV of the third BF subband.

---

Beam Computer block
11462908:
Beam Computer block
The Beam Computer is a logical entity whose black-box behaviour is the following:

Input:

Channel Estimates of the validated SRS Ports.

Configuration Parameters.

Output:

Normalized Beamweight vectors per Subband.

Timeline:

Beam Computer is activated after channel estimation and port validation. Duration of the calculation is specified in the computation window.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a beam computation process. The flowchart is divided into several sections, with boxes representing processes and arrows indicating the flow of data.
The main process is enclosed in a green rectangle labeled "BEAM COMPUTER". Inside this rectangle, there are three sequential processes: "SRS port Validation", "MMSE", and "Precoder Normalization".
Input to the "SRS port Validation" process comes from "CE (SMEM)" and also from several parameters listed above: "Rank/Number of Beams", "Threshold for minimum Port Power", "Number of TRX", and "Number of Subbands".
The output of "SRS port Validation" feeds into the "MMSE" process. The "MMSE" process also receives input parameters: "Number of Subbands", "Number of TRX", and "Rank/Number of Beams".
The output of "MMSE" feeds into "Precoder Normalization". The output of "Precoder Normalization" is split into two outputs: "BWV (DDR)" and "L2PS response".
Below the main "BEAM COMPUTER" block, there are additional processes and data flows depicted with dashed lines, suggesting a temporal or conditional relationship.
A box labeled "SRS Validation" with an output point labeled "A" is connected by a dashed line to a point on the vertical axis labeled "Beam Computation window".
A box labeled "MMSE Calculation for an UE" with an output point labeled "B" is also connected by a dashed line to the "Beam Computation window" axis, positioned further down than point "A".
A box labeled "Normalization of BWVs" with an output point labeled "C" is connected by a dashed line to the "Beam Computation window" axis, positioned further down than point "B".
Finally, a box labeled "BWVs are available" with an output point labeled "D" is connected by a dashed line to the "Beam Computation window" axis, positioned at the lowest point among C, B, and A.
The overall diagram depicts a system where data is processed through validation, estimation, and normalization steps to ultimately produce beam vectors and responses. The "Beam Computation window" axis suggests a time-based or sequential aspect to these operations.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7267.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

---

##### 5.5.5.4.8.2 IE operation

###### 5.5.5.4.8.2.0-2 IE operation To issue a new beam weight vector calculation to the beam computer, bit "Calculate" of operation IE in  srsBwv structure of UlData_SrsReceiveReq message (see 5G_L1_IF_14860_replaced( 11514427 )) shall be activated. (ID: 11462923)

##### 5.5.5.4.8.3 Method

###### 5.5.5.4.8.3.0-2 Method The following methods for beamweight vector calculation can be configured during cell creation, according to method IE of pSRSBwvConfig structure in ULCell_SetupReq message (see 5G_L1_IF_14862_replaced( 11513497 )): -  MMSE (Minumum Mean Square Error)  [CB008322-F] also for Thor [End CB008322-F] (ID: 11462939)

##### 5.5.5.4.8.4 Precondition

**5.5.5.4.8.4.0-2**  (ID: `11462953`)

Precondition
The preconditions for the Beam Computer to start calculation even are:

- The Channel Estimates of the SRS ports are available.

- SRS port(s) power has been validated. [CB008322-A, CB008322-F] The threshold is given by srsQualityThreshold in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14862\_replaced([11513497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008322-A, CB008322-F]

---

##### 5.5.5.4.8.5 Beam computation window

###### 5.5.5.4.8.5.0-1 Beam computation window Beam computation window is the elapsed time between triggering of SRS port validation job (PSM time) and the JCE (Job completion event) time (PSM time) of the beamweight vector normalization job. For all configurations, the beam computation window shall not exceed 800 (placeholder value, TBC by L1 SW) us. (ID: 11462963)

##### 5.5.5.4.8.6 Time domain correlation computation

###### 5.5.5.4.8.6.0-1 Time domain correlation computation 5G-L1-UL supports the computation of time domain correlation of SRS channel estimation for the UE configured with short-term BM per SRS port and report it to 5G-L2-PS for UE movement surveillance via IE 'correlation' in 5G_L1_IF_14858_replaced( 11514505 ). Only the middle PRB of the middle subband and its corresponding CE results over two latest SRS periods are needed. See Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification section 5.1.2.3.2 for more details. Refer to 5G_L1_13192_replaced( 11462507 ) for document location. (ID: 11462975)

##### 5.5.5.4.8.7 UE specific CSI-RS beams computation

**5.5.5.4.8.7.0-1**  (ID: `11462984`)

UE specific CSI-RS beams computation
Beam computer supports the computation of beam weight vectors (BWVs) for UE specific CSI-RS beams.

Only MMSE algorithm is used and the selected beamforming subband is indicated by 5G-L2-PS via the first element of IE bfSubbandId in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14860\_replaced([11514427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PbfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- If bfSubbandId[0] = '0XFF' (invalid value), then UE specific CSI-RS beam computation is ignored

- Else, UE specific CSI-RS beam computation is implemented on the selection BF subband

The size of each BWV for both polarizations is N\_TRX by 4, where N\_TRX is the number of TRX and 4 is the UE specific CSI-RS port number. The computed BWVs are assiciated with additional 4 patternIds [Before CB008322-G] that can be indicated by IE numPatternId in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14860\_replaced([11514427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PbfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008322-G]

---

##### 5.5.5.4.8.8 Beam Computer states

**5.5.5.4.8.8.0-2**  (ID: `11463001`)

Beam Computer states
The following set of actions are performed at the Beam Computer based on operation IE in srsBwv structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14860\_replaced([11514427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PbfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Simple states (1 bit is activated):

Reset: [Before CB008322-O] memory may be reused/overwrite. Any previous data is discarded. [CB008322-O] Indicate that startPatternId in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14860\_replaced([11514427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PbfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be changed (see Note below). [End CB008322-O] IE operation = 1.

Store: intermediate operation, memory allocation. Beamweight vector calculation needs more data. IE operation = 2.

Calculate: Compute new beamweight vectors if preconditions are fulfilled. After computation is completed, store the new vectors in dedicated memory location. Trigger generation of L2PS response. IE operation = 4.

Combined states (2 bits are activated):

Reset+Store: memory reuse/overwrite and intermediate step, memory allocation. IE operation = 3.

Reset+Calculate: memory reuse/overwrite and calculate of new beamweight vectors. After computation is completed, store the new vectors in dedicated memory location. Trigger generation of L2PS response. IE operation = 6.

[Before CB008322-O]

[CB008322-B] Additionally, IE operation can be used to indicate if it is the first BWV report of the UE that configured with wideband SRS resources.

* If LSB+3 bit of operation is 0: not the first BWV report.
* If LSB+3 bit of operation is 1: first BWV report. In this case, 5G-L1-UL shall not trigger the SRS snapshot capture due to abnormal correlation result.

Note:

1. LSB+3 bit is set only if all SRS ports IQ data of a BWV UE are renewed. In other cases, L1 shall expect it as 0.

[End CB008322-B]

[CB008322-O]

LSB+3 bit of operation is used to indicate if time domain correlation of channel estimates (descirbed in 5G\_L1\_13236\_replaced([11462975](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBKKBvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is needed or not.

* If LSB+3 bit of operation is 0: time domain correlation is not needed.
* If LSB+3 bit of operation is 1: time domain correlation is required.

Note:

1.The change of startPatternId  makes it possible for L1 to maintain the ping-pong switch scheme for BWV computation.

1. BWV computation can now be conducted using mixed SRS port IQ data from two consecutive SRS periods.
2. LSB+3 bit is set only if all SRS ports IQ data of a BWV UE are renewed. In other cases, L1 shall expect it as 0.

[End CB008322-O]

---

MMSE figure 11463030: MMSE figure The overall process for Subband computation using MMSE method is depicted in the following figure: [image-0][image_desc]The image depicts a block diagram illustrating a process involving channel estimation (CE) for SRS (Sounding Reference Signal) ports and MMSE precoding. The diagram is organized into three main horizontal sections, each representing a subband: Subband #1, Subband #2, and Subband #j. Each subband section begins with a visual representation of CE for multiple SRS ports (port #1, port #2, and port #4, indicated by vertical bars labeled TRX#1, TRX#2, up to TRX#64). These bars are segmented into different colored blocks, representing "Final CE per subband." The colors used are light blue, dark blue, and orange. Following the CE representation for each subband, there is an arrow pointing to a rectangular block labeled "MMSE Precoder." The formula within this block is "(2 numOfRowTRX num OfColumnTRX) x (numBwPerSubband)". Finally, an arrow from the MMSE Precoder block leads to a series of horizontal colored bars, each labeled as "BWV #X for subband #Y," where X represents the BWV number and Y represents the subband number. The colors of these BWV bars vary depending on the subband. Specifically: - Subband #1 is highlighted with a yellow border around its CE representation. The MMSE precoder for this subband is associated with yellow and light yellow BWV bars, labeled BWV #1, #2, #3, and up to #numBwwPerSubband for subband #1. - Subband #2 is highlighted with a red border around its CE representation. The MMSE precoder for this subband is associated with brown, orange, and light orange BWV bars, labeled BWV #1, #2, #3, and up to #numBwwPerSubband for subband #2. - Subband #j is highlighted with a green border around its CE representation. The MMSE precoder for this subband is associated with dark green, medium green, and light green BWV bars, labeled BWV #1, #2, #3, and up to #numBwwPerSubband for subband #j. The legend at the bottom indicates that the colored blocks within the vertical bars represent "Final CE per subband."[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_7289.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] (ID: 11463030)

###### 5.5.5.4.8.9.2 MMSE Precoder block

**5.5.5.4.8.9.2.0-2**  (ID: `11463046`)

MMSE Precoder block
The MMSE Precoder block subsystem works as follows for a given subband:

Input:

Complex matrix H(k,m) of size (2*numOfRowTRX*numOfColumnTRX)xP representing the channel Estimate of P validated SRS ports for subband k and UE m.

Output:

Complex matrix W(k,m) of size (2*numOfRowTRX*numOfColumnTRX)xP representing the beamweight vectors for subband k and UE m.

Columns of W(k,m) represent each of the P  beamweight vectors of size (2*numOfRowTRX*numOfColumnTRX).

Method:

MMSE involves inversion of a full-rank Hermitian matrix after regularization. The dimension of the inversion is P.

The regularization factor depends on the channel estimates  H(k,m) and some constants that defined by rdThermNoisFlag (5G\_UP\_ALG\_19841\_replaced([11110389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpDs2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

* If rdThermNoisFlag = 0, rdparameter rdMmsePowerFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_19840\_replaced([11110396](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpDs3vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is used (option 0).
* If rdThermNoisFlag = 1, therm noise level is used (option 1).
* [CB008322-G]  if rdThermNoisFlag  = 2, rho in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14860\_replaced([11514427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PbfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is used (option 2). Note: 5G-L1-UL shall ignore rho expect invalid value (-255) when rdThermNoisFlag is different than 2. [End CB008322-G]

The MMSE expresion (option 0/1/2) is detailed in 5.1.2.3 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification Document, see 5G\_L1\_13192\_replaced([11462507](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBHGu_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Document Location.

---

FEBF figure
[Before CNI-99771] The overall process for Subband computation using FBEF method is depicted in the following figure:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a signal processing method. It depicts three parallel processing paths, each corresponding to a different subband: Subband #1, Subband #2, and Subband #j.
Each subband processing path begins with a visual representation of "CE for SRS port" data, broken down by TRX (transceiver) numbers (TRX#1 to TRX#64). This data is presented as stacked bars of varying colors, indicating different components or values. The bars are grouped into multiple sets, suggesting processing across different ports and transceivers.
Following the initial data representation, each subband path feeds into a block labeled "FEBF method". This method is further broken down into sequential steps: "CoMa", "Power Iteration", and a combined step of "Left-singular vectors Right-singular vectors", culminating in "Power balance".
The output of each "FEBF method" block is a series of colored horizontal bars, each labeled as "BWV #X for subband #Y", where X represents a sequential number and Y indicates the subband. The number of these output bars varies per subband, indicated by a colon and the label "BWV #numBwwPerSubband for subband #".
A legend at the bottom of the image clarifies that the stacked bars in the initial data representation and the colored segments within them represent "Final CE per subband".
The overall diagram shows a process that takes input data for different subbands, applies a specific method (FEBF method) involving several iterative steps, and produces a set of output values (BWV) for each subband. The colors used in the diagram are consistent within each subband's processing path and output.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7295.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CNI-99771]

Note: Subband beamforming via FEBF is not supported from E2E perspective. But, SW codes for this requirement still need to be inherited with deactivation.

[End CNI-99771]

---

###### 5.5.5.4.8.10.2 SVD

**5.5.5.4.8.10.2.0-1**  (ID: `11463075`)

SVD
[Before CNI-99771] When rdEigenVectorMethod (see 5G\_UL\_ALG\_15320 for details) is set to "SVD", then, for a given subband,  the FEBF block subsystem works as follows:

Input:

Complex matrix H(k,m) of size P x (2*numOfRowTRX*numOfColumnTRX) representing the channel Estimate of P validated SRS ports for subband k and UE m.

Output:

Complex matrix W(k,m) of size (2*numOfRowTRX*numOfColumnTRX)xP representing the beamweight vectors for subband k and UE m.

Columns of W(k,m) represent each of the P  beamweight vectors of size (2*numOfRowTRX*numOfColumnTRX).

Method:

The SVD decomposition is detailed in 5.1.2.1.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification Document, see 5G\_L1\_10071\_replaced([11462500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBHGuvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Document Location. It consists of three main steps:

* CoMa calculation of the SRS ports subspace, i.e., H(k,m)\*hermitian(H(k,m)) with size PxP. See Section 4.2.1.2 of of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification Document, 5G\_L1\_10071\_replaced([11462500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBHGuvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Document Location.
* Power iteration to compute eigenvalues and eigenvectors of previous step CoMa. Singular values are related to eigenvalues by means of a (positive) square root operation.  See Section 4.3.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification Document, 5G\_L1\_10071\_replaced([11462500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBHGuvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Document Location.
* Singular vectors. Left singular vectors are directly obtained from previous step eigenvectors and right singular vectors are obtained from the product of Channel estimate H(k,m), singular values and left singular values.  See Section 5.1.2.1.1 of of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification Document, 5G\_L1\_10071\_replaced([11462500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBHGuvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Document Location.

SVD involves the factorization of a rank deficient matrix. The dimension of the factorization is P, 2*numOfRowTRX*numOfColumnTRX.

As beamweights are eigenvectors of the channel, they are inherently normalized.

[CNI-99771]

Note: Subband beamforming via FEBF is not supported from E2E perspective. But, SW codes for this requirement still need to be inherited with deactivation.

[End CNI-99771]

---

###### 5.5.5.4.8.10.3 EVD

**5.5.5.4.8.10.3.0-1**  (ID: `11463083`)

EVD
[Before CNI-99771] When rdEigenVectorMethod (see 5G\_UL\_ALG\_15320 for details) is set to "EVD", then, for a given subband,  the FEBF block subsystem works as follows:

Input:

bwvSubbandSize Complex matrices H(t,k,m) of size P x (2*numOfRowTRX*numOfColumnTRX) representing the channel Estimate of the t-th PRB from P validated SRS ports for subband k and UE m.

Output:

Complex matrix W(k,m) of size (2*numOfRowTRX*numOfColumnTRX)xP representing the beamweight vectors for subband k and UE m.

Columns of W(k,m) represent each of the P  beamweight vectors of size (2*numOfRowTRX*numOfColumnTRX).

Method:

The EVD decomposiition is detailed in 5.1.2.1.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification Document, see 5G\_L1\_10071\_replaced([11462500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBHGuvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Document Location. It consists of three main steps:

* CoMa calculation of the SRS ports subspace, i.e., hermitian(H(t,k,m))*H(t,k,m) with size (2*numOfRowTRX*numOfColumnTRX)x(2*numOfRowTRX\*numOfColumnTRX) for every PRB in the subband. Average over the bwvSubbandSize PRBs within the subband. See Section 4.2.1.2 of of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification Document, 5G\_L1\_10071\_replaced([11462500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBHGuvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Document Location.
* Power iteration computes eigenvalues and eigenvectors of previous averaged CoMa. See Section 4.3.1 of of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification Document, 5G\_L1\_10071\_replaced([11462500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBHGuvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Document Location.

EVD involves the factorization of a rank deficient matrix. The dimension of the factorization is 2*numOfRowTRX*numOfColumnTRX, P.

As beamweights are eigenvectors of the channel, they are inherently normalized.

[CNI-99771]

Note: Subband beamforming via FEBF is not supported from E2E perspective. But, SW codes for this requirement still need to be inherited with deactivation.

[End CNI-99771]

---

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is a fraction where the numerator is the difference between the L2 norm of $Ax\_{Maxiter}$ and the L2 norm of $Ax\_{Maxiter-1}$, and the denominator is the L2 norm of $Ax\_{Maxiter-1}$.
The expression can be written as:
$$ \frac{|Ax\_{Maxiter}|*2 - |Ax*{Maxiter-1}|*2}{|Ax*{Maxiter-1}|\_2} $$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7301.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

##### 5.5.5.4.8.11 Power Balance

**5.5.5.4.8.11.0-2**  (ID: `11463113`)

Power Balance
[Before CNI-99771] When FEBF method is used (method=1) and the following conditions are met

- rdPowerBalance is set to "code rate". See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14934\_replaced([11110340](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpDFyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details.

- The SINR reported from L2PS is not invalid.

then power balance, based on MCS, between layers is enabled. This procedure scales the power of each layer proportionally to eigenvalues of the channel, i.e., better channel propagation paths get less power budget. For the worst propagation paths, additional power is allocated based on the SNR difference between current and highest MCS (within same modulation order) Link Adaptation working points.

The power balance based on MCS procedure is described in Section 5.1.2.1.2.2 of the Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification Document, 5G\_L1\_10071\_replaced([11462500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBHGuvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Document Location.

[CNI-99771]

FEBF method and its related procedures are not supported from E2E perspective. But, SW codes for this requirement still need to be inherited with deactivation.

[End CNI-99771]

---

##### 5.5.5.4.8.12 Normalization of beamweight vectors

###### 5.5.5.4.8.12.1 General

**5.5.5.4.8.12.1.0-2**  (ID: `11463135`)

General
The beam computer normalizes, per subband, the precoder W according to the following criteria:

* Layer-wise normalization, as described in step1) of 5.1.2.3.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification document.
* TRX-wise normalization, as described in step2) of  5.1.2.3.1 of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification document.

Depending on rdparameter rdMmseNorm (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13938\_replaced([11107483](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kofsLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

* Effectively, per subband, each beamweight vector (columns of W) is first normalized to number of TRX. After that, each TRX (rows of W) is normalized to unity. (rdMmseNorm  = 0)
* Effectively, per subband, each TRX (rows of W) is normalized to unity.(rdMmseNorm  = 1)

BWV normalization is also needed for UE specific CSI-RS beams that computed.

See 5G\_L1\_13192\_replaced([11462507](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBHGu_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Document Location.

---

###### 5.5.5.4.8.12.2 Normalization for FBEF

**5.5.5.4.8.12.2.0-1**  (ID: `11463144`)

Normalization for FBEF
[Before CNI-99771] When FBEF method is selected (method=1), the layer-wise normalization step in 5G\_L1\_15580\_replaced([11463118](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBLYIfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is skipped.

Layer-wise normalization is embedded in the FEBF algorithm.

[CNI-99771] Note: FEBF is not supported from E2E perspective. But, SW codes for this requirement still need to be inherited with deactivation.[End CNI-99771]

---

#### 5.5.5.4.9 Beamweight vectors processing

##### 5.5.5.4.9.1 Beamweight vector to PatternID mapping

###### 5.5.5.4.9.1.1 Beamweight vector to PatternID mapping

**5.5.5.4.9.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `11463171`)

Beamweight vector to PatternID mapping
Per calculation, the beam Computer assigns PatternID to the different beams according to the following mapping:

Input:

from UlData\_SrsReceiveReq: startPatternId, numBwvPerSubband, [Before CB008322-G] numRbgPerSubband [End CB008322-G], [CB008322-A] bfSubbandId [End CB008322-A]

from UlCell\_SetupReq: bwvSubbandSize, [CB008322-G] numPrbPerWideband  [End CB008322-G]

Output:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Beam/Layer |  |  | 0 | 1 | … | numBwvPerSubband-1 |
|  | Subband |  | Start PRB |  |  |  |  |
| UE#j | Ping | 0 | startPrb | startPatternId | startPatternId+1 | startPatternId+numBwvPerSubband-1 |  |
| 1 | startPrb+bwvSubbandSize | startPatternId+1\*numBwvPerSubband | startPatternId+1\*numBwvPerSubband+1 | startPatternId+2\*numBwvPerSubband-1 |  |  |  |
| 2 | startPrb+2\*bwvSubbandSize | startPatternId+2\*numBwvPerSubband | startPatternId+2\*numBwvPerSubband+1 | startPatternId+3\*numBwvPerSubband-1 |  |  |  |
| 3 | startPrb+3\*bwvSubbandSize | startPatternId+3\*numBwvPerSubband | startPatternId+3\*numBwvPerSubband+1 | startPatternId+4\*numBwvPerSubband-1 |  |  |  |
| … | … | … | … | … |  |  |  |
| K-1=ceil([Before CB008322-G] 4\*numRbgPerSubband [CB008322-G] numPrbPerWideband [End CB008322-G]/bwvSubbandSize)-1 | startPrb+ (K-1)\*bwvSubbandSize | startPatternId+(K-1)\*numBwvPerSubband | startPatternId+(K-1)\*numBwvPerSubband+1 | startPatternId+K\*numBwvPerSubband-1 |  |  |  |
| K (UE specific CSI-RS) | See Note 1 | startPatternId+K \*numBwvPerSubband | startPatternId+K\*numBwvPerSubband+1 | startPatternId+(K+1)\*numBwvPerSubband-1 |  |  |  |
| Pong | 0 | startPrb | startPatternId+(K+1)\*numBwvPerSubband | startPatternId+(K+1)\*numBwvPerSubband +1 | startPatternId+(K+2)\*numBwvPerSubband -1 |  |  |
| 1 | startPrb+bwvSubbandSize | startPatternId+(K+2)\*numBwvPerSubband | startPatternId+(K+2)\*numBwvPerSubband +1 | startPatternId+(K+3)\*numBwvPerSubband -1 |  |  |  |
| 2 | startPrb+2\*bwvSubbandSize | startPatternId+(K+3)\*numBwvPerSubband | startPatternId+(K+3)\*numBwvPerSubband +1 | startPatternId+(K+4)\*numBwvPerSubband 1 |  |  |  |
| 3 | startPrb+3\*bwvSubbandSize | startPatternId+(K+4)\*numBwvPerSubband | startPatternId+(K+4)\*numBwvPerSubband +1 | startPatternId+(K+5)\*numBwvPerSubband -1 |  |  |  |
| … | … | … | … | … |  |  |  |
| K-1=ceil([Before CB008322-G] 4\*numRbgPerSubband [CB008322-G] numPrbPerWideband [End CB008322-G]/bwvSubbandSize)-1 | startPrb+ (K-1)\*bwvSubbandSize | startPatternId+(2*K-1)*numBwvPerSubband | startPatternId+(2*K-1)*numBwvPerSubband +1 | startPatternId+2*K*numBwvPerSubband-1 |  |  |  |
| K (UE specific CSI-RS) | See Note 1 | startPatternId+2*K* numBwvPerSubband | startPatternId+2*K*numBwvPerSubband+1 | startPatternId+(2*K+1)*numBwvPerSubband-1 |  |  |  |

In words, mapping follows ascending order of layer, and subband respectively.

Note1:  number of total subbands K takes into account of one additional subband that is selected by 5G-L2-PS for UE specific CSI-RS beam. The selected subband for UE specific CSI-RS is indicated by bfSubbandId[0] in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14860\_replaced([11514427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PbfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note2: the total number of patternIds is numBwvPerSubband*K. Ping-Pong mechanism is used, which means up to 2*numBwvPerSubband\*K patternIds will be reserved for a single UE.

Note3: each full-dimension beamweight vector of size numOfRowTRX x numOfColumnTRX is mapped to one unique patternId. How the same patternId and corresponding full-dimension beamweight vector are used and mapped to PDSCH data for different polarizations can be found in CB009496.

---

###### 5.5.5.4.9.1.2 validataion failure

###### 5.5.5.4.9.1.2.0-2 validataion failure If some of the SRS ports do not pass validation, some PatternIds are skipped. In that case, Beam Computer reports less beamweight vectors than numPatternId. [CB008322-A, CB008322-F] When bfSubbandId[0] is not invalid value, 4 additional patternIds are reserved for UE specific CSI-RS beams. [End CB008322-A, CB008322-F] (ID: 11463187)

##### 5.5.5.4.9.2 Delivery to L1 SW FH

###### 5.5.5.4.9.2.1 Beamweight vectors ready indication

###### 5.5.5.4.9.2.1.0-1 Beamweight vectors ready indication Beam Computer sends event to L1 SW FH when new beamweight vectors are ready. (ID: 11463200)

###### 5.5.5.4.9.2.2 Beamweight calculation within the computation window

###### 5.5.5.4.9.2.2.0-1 Beamweight calculation within the computation window Beam Computer ensures proper delivery of beamweight vectors by finishing calculation and saving to memory before the end of the computation window. (ID: 11463210)

###### 5.5.5.4.9.2.3 PING-PONG buffer management

###### 5.5.5.4.9.2.3.0-1 PING-PONG buffer management L1 implements a PING-PONG buffer to store beamweight vectors results, i.e.,  after calculation #n is ready (end of computation window), L1 keeps VALID results for calculation #n and #n-1 till the start of next computation window. The Ping-Pong buffer separates the memory dedicated for calculation #n and calculation #n-1. (ID: 11463223)

#### 5.5.5.4.10 Measurements

##### 5.5.5.4.10.0-1 Measurements For the selected SRS subband, the DFT expansion coefficients (used for EIRP coefficient calculation) computation is described in 5GMAX Massive MIMO Algorithm specification section 5.1.2.3.3. The computation is per layer per polarization. Refer to 5G_L1_13192_replaced( 11462507 ) for document location. (ID: 11463233)

### 5.5.5.5 SRS_SU SU-MIMO: Parameter estimation in Beam (SxC) domain or Non-BF Antenna (AxC) domain

#### 5.5.5.5.1 Overview, receiver architecture and algorithms

##### 5.5.5.5.1.1 5GMax algorithm specification for SU-MIMO

###### 5.5.5.5.1.1.0-1 5GMax algorithm specification for SU-MIMO For SU-MIMO usage, SRS detection algorithm is described in section '2.6 SRS' of the 5GMax algorithm specification, please see 5G_L1_5G21A_916 5G_L1_7703_replaced( 11396538 ). [5GC001868-C, 5GC001868-D, 5GC001868-E] 5G-L1-UL shall support SRS detection algorithm as described above in Loki L1 HW [End 5GC001868-C, 5GC001868-D, 5GC001868-E] (ID: 11463252)

##### 5.5.5.5.1.2 SRS receiver algorithm in FDD

**5.5.5.5.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `11463272`)

SRS receiver algorithm in FDD
SRS receiver algorithm in FDD

Receiver with 2 and 4 antenna streams are supported. Use of 2Rx or 4Rx is configurable per cell during cell setup phase by using IE ulSubcellType.

Refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for configured ulSubcellType.

Refer to 5G\_L1\_12924\_replaced([11481485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fDeeO_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for mapping of ulSubcellType to number of Rx antennas.

Note: The corresponding AxC/eAxC mapping can be found in 5G\_UP\_2501.

[CB011178-A] This requirement is applicable for Thor (BB) for FR1-FDD-eCPRI-7-2a. [End CB011178-A]

###### 5.5.5.5.1.2.1 Thor

**5.5.5.5.1.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `12590617`)

Thor
The SRS SU-MIMO receiver supports the following modes:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Receiver Order (Subcell Type) |  |
| Frequency range | FDD |
| FR1 | 2RX (A2), 4RX (A4), [CB013442-SR-D] 8RX (A8) [End CB013442-SR-D] |

Receiver order is configurable per cell during cell setup phase by means of IE ulSubcellType.

Refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for configured ulSubcellType.

Refer to 5G\_L1\_12924\_replaced([11481485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fDeeO_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for mapping of ulSubcellType to number of Rx antennas.

**Note: Configuration-wise, some SiSo functionality is dependent on FH technology, *Receiver with 8 antenna streams is currently restricted to eCPRI FH.***

##### 5.5.5.5.1.4 Architecture diagram

**5.5.5.5.1.4.0-1**  (ID: `11463326`)

Architecture diagram
For each subcell, a SRS receiver is needed. This SRS receiver ignores the interference potentially coming from other Ues transmitting SRS on the same comb in the same cell. The assumption is that this interference is small thanks to SDMA. In addition, the fact that Ues using the same SRS comb use different cyclic shifts for their SRS sequences introduces a “natural” interference rejection in the per subcell SRS processing that is described in the sequel.

The following diagram summarizes the SRS receiver processing, within each subcell, from a functional point of view.

Source: 5G\_L1\_9572\_replaced([11459335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0y0PvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L1\_9573\_replaced([11459355](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0y0_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Top level view of SRS receiver (this figure provides a functional view)

(Figure 7-77-1)

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating the "SRS channel estimation (Rx Antenna specific processing)" and "rest of the SRS processing".
The flowchart begins with "SRS subcarriers of a Rx antenna" which can be from ULFE in case of CPRI or from eCPRI common uplink MDAB in case of eCPRI. This input is fed into a "Symbol and RE splitter" along with "symbolPosition transmissionComb transmissionCombld". The output of the splitter goes to "SRS raw channel estimation".
The "SRS raw channel estimation" feeds into "SRS Pilot separation" and "TO estimation". The "SRS pilot generator" receives "sequenceld cyclicShift" and also feeds into "SRS raw channel estimation" and "SRS Pilot separation".
The "SRS Pilot separation" and "TO estimation" outputs are fed into the "rest of the SRS processing" block. Within this block, the following processes are shown:
1. **Frequency domain Channel Smoothing**: Receives input from "SRS Pilot separation" and "TO estimation". It outputs to "Noise power estimation" and "SRS signal power estimation".
2. **Noise power estimation**: Receives input from "Frequency domain Channel Smoothing" and "SRS Pilot separation". It outputs to "snrMeas", "shortTermTaMetric Meas\_antX, shortTermTaPeak AmpMeas\_antX", and "noisePowerMeas\_antX".
3. **SRS signal power estimation**: Receives input from "Frequency domain Channel Smoothing" and "SRS raw channel estimation". It outputs to "SRS DTX detection (antenna-wise)" and "RI selection".
4. **SRS DTX detection (antenna-wise)**: Receives input from "SRS signal power estimation". It outputs to "ulRankMeas" and "dbxMeas".
5. **RI selection**: Receives input from "SRS signal power estimation". It outputs to "PMI selection".
6. **PMI selection**: Receives input from "RI selection". It outputs to "ulPmiRank1Meas ulPmiRank2Meas ulPmiRank1SinrMeas ulPmiRank2SinrMeas" and "rxPowerMeas".
The outputs of the "rest of the SRS processing" block are:
\* snrMeas
\* shortTermTaMetric Meas\_antX, shortTermTaPeak AmpMeas\_antX
\* noisePowerMeas\_antX
\* ulPmiRank1Meas ulPmiRank2Meas ulPmiRank1SinrMeas ulPmiRank2SinrMeas
\* ulRankMeas
\* dbxMeas
\* rxPowerMeas[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7347.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Source: 5G\_L1\_9573\_replaced([11459355](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0y0_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
