11463370:
Supported UE specific beamforming for SU-MIMO
11463370:
Supported UE specific beamforming for SU-MIMO
For periodic SRS, 5G-L1-UL needs to support UE specific beamforming for SRS reception for SU-MIMO measurements.

The supported beamset is provided to L1 in the pSRSConfig structure of the UlCell\_SetupReq message.

Besides application of UE-specific beams, processing for periodic and aperiodic SRS is the same.

Extension of the beamset. DFT beams are supported.

5G-L1-UL also needs to support UE specific beamforming for SRS reception for SU-MIMO measurements when wideband TAS SRS resource is configured.

The supported beamset is provided to L1 in pSRSConfig structure of the UlCell\_SetupReq message, [CB014005-SR-A] or online updated in UlCell\_BeamConfigUpdateReq message ([11513613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxv3PvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_CqlKNu3yEe-rL47x_rCCmw)). [End CB014005-SR-A].

Consequently, following three types of SRS signal can be used for SU-MIMO measurements.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating different types of Sounding Reference Signals (SRS) and their associated User Equipment (UE) types, along with a block for RI/PMI, SINR measurement. The diagram is organized into several gray rectangular blocks with white text.
On the left, there are two blocks stacked vertically. The top block reads "Aperiodic SRS". The bottom block reads "Periodic SRS".
To the right of the "Aperiodic SRS" block, there is a block labeled "SU-MIMO (ueType = 0)".
Below the "SU-MIMO" block, there are two smaller blocks stacked vertically. The top one reads "Long term BF (ueType = 1)", and the bottom one reads "Subband BF (ueType= 3)".
To the right of the "Periodic SRS" block and spanning the height of the "SU-MIMO", "Long term BF", and "Subband BF" blocks, there is a large rectangular block labeled "RI/PMI, SINR measurement".
The overall layout suggests a categorization of SRS transmission modes and related measurements.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7350.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

12442946:
General
Only for periodic SRS, 5G-L1-UL shall perform beamforming operation over the NDM SRS streams.

For each UE and and all the resource elements of the subband, the 64, 32 or 16 configured TRX for the cell are coherently  combined (amplitude and phase rotation) by the beamweight vector indicated by L2.

The beamweight vectors are selected from the beamset sent to L1 during Cell Set up [CB014005-SR-A] or online updated in UlCell\_BeamConfigUpdateReq message ([11513613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxv3PvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Frm%2Fcm%2Fstream%2F_CqlKNu3yEe-rL47x_rCCmw)) [End CB014005-SR-A]. Each beamweight vector in the beamset is indexed by *PatternId IE.*

The beamweight vector consists of *realPartOfWeight and* imagPartOfWeight, which denotes the real and imaginary part of the vector, respectively.\*\*

Each beamweight vector, with complex components,  is of size *NumOfColumnTRX*NumOfRowTRX and is applied to each polarization indepedently.\*

The same beamweight vector is used for both polarizations, i.e., *patternId*is used for both polarizations.\*\*

The supported cell configuration is:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **NumOfTRX** | **NumOfRowTRX** | **NumOfColumnTRX** |
| 64 | 4 | 8 |
| 32 (split mode on/off) | 4 | 4 |
| 32 (split mode on/off) | 2 | 8 |
| 16 (split mode on) | 2 | 4 |
| 16 (split mode on) | 1 | 8 |

For simplicity *N=numOfColumnTRX  and* R=numOfRowTRX.\*\*

**W denotes N*R the complex beamweight vector indexed by *patternId and the TRX number containing a SRS stream is indexed by* localCeAxCId.***\*

The beamforming operation is depicted in the following figure:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image depicts a complex signal processing or data flow diagram, likely representing a component of a larger system such as a communication receiver or a digital signal processor. The diagram is structured in stages, with signals flowing from left to right.
The initial stage on the far left shows several input lines labeled with expressions involving variables 'R' and 'N', such as "[2R-1]N", "[R-1]N", "[2R-1]N+1", "[R-1]N+1", "[R+1]N", "N", "0", "[R+1]N+1", "RN", "RN+1", and "1". These inputs are processed through a series of "cross-over" or "permutation" blocks, indicated by diagonal lines (green and red) crossing over signal paths. Some of these paths are marked with red 'X' symbols, suggesting that certain signals are being discarded or not used in subsequent stages.
Following the permutation blocks, the signals are routed to stages involving summation operations, indicated by circular symbols with a '+' sign inside. These summation blocks take multiple input signals and produce a single output signal. There are several such summation blocks, organized in a hierarchical manner.
The diagram also shows a progression of signal paths, with some paths being combined and others branching out. The overall structure suggests a series of transformations and aggregations of the input signals. The use of different colors for the diagonal lines (green and red) might indicate different types of operations or signal properties. The red 'X' marks on some of the diagonal lines are a strong visual cue that specific signal paths are being intentionally interrupted or deselected.
The final stage of the diagram shows a few output lines, suggesting the final processed signals from this particular block. The labels and the structure imply a mathematical or algorithmic process is being visualized.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7353.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Previous operation is repeated for each UE, for each resource element in the subband and each *patternId configured for each UE.*

---

##### 5.5.5.5.2.2 Normalization

###### 5.5.5.5.2.2.0-2 Normalization After beamforming with column vector w of size NumOfColumnTRX NumOfRowTRX, the result must be normalised with factor: 1/sqrt( w^H *w). **** Equivalently, during cell setup [CB014005-SR-A] or online updated in UlCell_BeamConfigUpdateReq message ( 11513613 ) [End CB014005-SR-A], each beam weight vector component must be divided by 1/sqrt( w^H w).**** (ID: 12442947)

##### 5.5.5.5.2.3 Beamweight vectors construction

###### 5.5.5.5.2.3.0-2 Beamweight vectors construction 5G-L1-UL shall use only the first numOfColumnTRX numOfRowTRX vector components from IE realPartOfWeight and imagPartOfWeight, which are contained in pSRSConfig structure (5G_L1_IF_14077_replaced( 11513492 )) of UlCell_SetupReq message (5G_L1_IF_152_replaced( 11513449 )) [CB014005-SR-A] or online updated in UlCell_BeamConfigUpdateReq message ( 11513613 ) [End CB014005-SR-A], to construct the beamweight vectors in 5G_L1_5974_replaced( 11506456 ). The remaining (32- numOfColumnTRX numOfRowTRX) vector components shall be ignored. * *** Note: when numOfColumnTRX* numOfRowTRX=32, all the vector components from IE realPartOfWeight and *imagPartOfWeight are used. *** (ID: 12442955)

##### 5.5.5.5.2.4 Split panel model

**5.5.5.5.2.4.0-1**  (ID: `13312829`)

Split panel model
For FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI with Beamforming, spatial streams from RU are generated by linearly combine the signals across the full panel (per polarization) or across a subarea of the panel (per polarization), the so-called, sub-panel beamforming mode.

In 5G-L1-UL(BB), the use of subpanel beamforming affects some of the measurements, wherein a compensation factor shall be used, see [compensationFactor](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kB9-8cmnEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

5G-L2-PS indicates the subpanel model by means of IE suSplitPanelModel in srsSuMimo struct in UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message, see [srsSuMimo structure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

The different subpanel modes, with respective suSplitPanelModel values, are listed in [suSplitPanelMode options.vsdx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:u:/r/sites/ATFL1Spec/L1%20AS%20documents/Reference%20materials/suSplitPanelMode%20options.vsdx?d=wd00db8f48ecc4cb29c06b2e5397f538e&csf=1&web=1&e=kzSxxv):

Note: For FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI, subpanel split mode is introduced with feature CB008577.

#### 5.5.5.5.3 SRS receiver configuration

#### 5.5.5.5.4 Frequency offset compensation

##### 5.5.5.5.4.0-1 Frequency offset compensation No Frequency Offset Compensation for SRS for SU-MIMO. (ID: 12714246)

#### 5.5.5.5.5 Time offset compensation

##### 5.5.5.5.5.0-2 Time offset compensation 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall perform Time Offset Compensation, in the frequency domain, for each SRS symbol and spatial stream, before Raw Channel Estimation, as described in §2.6.1 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification ( 12689047 ). [CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] (ID: 12714254)

#### 5.5.5.5.6 Raw channel estimation

**5.5.5.5.6.0-2**  (ID: `12714268`)

Raw channel estimation
5G-L1-UL (BB)  shall perform Raw Channel Estimate for each SRS symbol and beam/spatial stream, as described in §2.6.2 of *5GMax Algorithm Specification ([12689047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7O57slZQEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).*

**Note: Raw Channel estimate uses the SRS sequence from the first SRS port (*cyclicShift in \*UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveReq, see [11517212](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSJjSPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).***\*

[CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA]

---

#### 5.5.5.5.7 Port separation

##### 5.5.5.5.7.0-1 Port separation Algorithm (ID: 11463472)

**5.5.5.5.7.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12873995`)

Port separation
5G-L1-UL (BB)  shall perform Pilot Separation for each SRS symbol and beam/spatial stream, as described in §2.6.4 of *5GMax Algorithm Specification ([12689047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7O57slZQEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).*

Frequency domain pilot separation is achieved by averaging consecutive channel estimation (from raw channel estimate). Depending on the SRS configuration, (raw) channel estimates are used in overlapping or non overlapping fashion. See below table for details.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Comb load | **Averaging method** |
| 2 CS per comb | Non-overlapping, average of 2 neighboring raw channel estimates ([11463497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBN0ZvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) |
| 4 CS per comb | Overlapping, average of 4 neighboring raw channel estimates ([11463497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBN0ZvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) |

For positioning: In Thor, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall parse all srsPos Users (contains in *UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message, [11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and suMiMo users (contains in* srsSuMimo structure of *UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message, [11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to check if any other UEs are multiplexed in the same comb with same* sequenceId*but different cyclic shifts for pilot separation. Note: because the rnti is not in* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message and wideband SRS is used for positioning, If the values of *sequenceId/symbolPosition/transmissionComb/transmissionCombId/cyclicShift for positioning and suMiMo are same, the suMimo request and positioning request are for the same UE.***\***\*

[CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA].

Note: for more information about overlapping and non-overlapping see the informative text in [11463497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBN0ZvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), showcasing examples for the smallest subband allocation of 4 PRB.

---

11463883:
Port separation
*Information text*
 
Based on 5gmax simulation, at least 12 channel estimation samples are required for high accuracy SRS SU MIMO measurement as the output of FD domain pilot separation per cyclic shift.
 
In case of only one cyclic shift is configured (no CS multiplexing, e.g., for 1 SRS port case), frequency domain pilot separation can be skipped.
 
In case of more than one cyclic shifts are multiplexed (for different SRS ports from same or different UEs), FD pilot separation needs to be conducted based on SRS configuration. The CS interval shall be at least 2 to keep the quality of FD pilot separation, which is ensured by cplane configuration (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_11168).
 If 2 CS per combId (usually for one UE, mono UE mode), two contiguous raw CE results are averaged to fully remove the phase residual from other CS. Refer to table 1&2 for comb2 and comb4 case. After obtaining the CE result of the first CS, the second CS result can be computed from the first CS by compensating the fixed phase difference.
o When SRS is comb2, min SRS subband is 4 PRB. Raw channel estimates have 4*(12/2) = 24 samples.
o When SRS is comb4, min SRS subband is 8 PRB. Raw channel estimates have 8*(12/4) = 24 samples.
 If 4 CS per combId (usually for multiple UEs, multiple UE mode), four contiguous raw CE results are averaged to fully remove the phase residual from other CS. Refer to table 3&4 for comb2 and comb4 case. After obtaining the CE result of the first CS, the second CS result can be computed from the first CS by compensating the fixed phase difference.
o When SRS is comb2, min SRS subband is 4 PRB. Raw channel estimates have 4*(12/2) = 24 samples.
o When SRS is comb4, min SRS subband is 8 PRB. Raw channel estimates have 8*(12/4) = 24 samples.
 If 6 CS per combId (usually for multiple UEs, multiple UE mode), six contiguous raw CE results are averaged to fully remove the phase residual from other CS. Refer to table 5. After obtaining the CE result of the first CS, the second CS result can be computed from the first CS by compensating the fixed phase difference.
o Only SRS comb4 can configure 6CS per combId, min SRS subband is 8 PRB. Raw channel estimates have 8\*(12/4) = 24 samples.
Note: When 6CS per combId is configured, SINR measurement can be easily biased especially for radio channel with large delay spread. The performance degradation is expected but mainly in high SINR region.
Table 1: comb2 and 2 CS per combId

| --- | --- | --- |

| [image-94][image\_desc]The image displays a collection of tables that illustrate the mapping of "Raw CE" (Resource Element) indices to "CE index of 1st CS" (Channel Estimation index of the first Channel State Information) across different configurations of "Comb" (Component Carrier) and "CS" (Code Stream). |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| The tables are organized into two main rows. The top row contains two tables: "Comb2 and 2 CS per comb" and "Comb2 and 4 CS per comb". The bottom row contains three tables: "Comb4 and 2 CS per comb", "Comb4 and 4 CS per comb", and "Comb4 and 6 CS per comb". |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Each table has columns for "PRB Index" (Physical Resource Block Index) and "Raw CE index aw CE inde", and "CE index of 1st CS". The "PRB Index" column lists PRBs from PRB1 to PRB4 in the top row tables, and PRB1 to PRB8 in the bottom row tables. The "Raw CE index aw CE inde" column lists "Raw CE" indices from 1 to 24. The "CE index of 1st CS" column shows colored blocks representing the mapped CE indices. |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| The colors used in the "CE index of 1st CS" columns are: |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| - Green: CE 1 |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| - Light Blue: CE 2 |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| - Yellow: CE 3 |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| - Red: CE 8 |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| - Yellow: CE 11 |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| - Red: CE 12 |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| The tables demonstrate how different combinations of Component Carriers and Code Streams affect the allocation of Channel Estimation indices. For instance, in "Comb2 and 2 CS per comb", PRB1 maps to CE 1, PRB2 to CE 5, PRB3 to CE 8, and PRB4 to CE 12. As the number of CS per comb increases, the number of PRBs also increases, and the mapping of CE indices becomes more distributed. |  |  |  |  |  |  |

---

#### 5.5.5.5.8 Channel estimate post processing

##### 5.5.5.5.8.1 SNR estimation

##### 5.5.5.5.8.2 MMSE smoother selection

###### 5.5.5.5.8.2.0-1 MMSE smoother selection 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall select the smoother, per SRS symbol, SRS port and spatial stream, as described in §2.6.7 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification ( 12689047 ). [CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] (ID: 12714423)

##### 5.5.5.5.8.3 MMSE smoothing

**5.5.5.5.8.3.0-2**  (ID: `12714461`)

MMSE smoothing
5G-L1-UL (BB)  shall perform channel smoothing and subcarrier selection for each SRS symbol, SRS port and spatial stream, as described in §2.6.7 of *5GMax Algorithm Specification ([12689047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7O57slZQEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).*

The number of selected subcarriers after channel smoothing is 12, evenly distributed across the SRS Resource Elements.

[CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA]

---

#### 5.5.5.5.9 Parameter estimation

##### 5.5.5.5.9.1 Power delay profile length estimation

**5.5.5.5.9.1.0-1**  (ID: `12714379`)

Power delay profile length estimation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall calculate Channel Impulse Response (CIR) for each SRS symbol and spatial stream, as described in §2.6.3 of *5GMax Algorithm Specification ([12689047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7O57slZQEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).*

The calcualtion of CIR uses raw channel estimates in frequency domain. The size of the IFFT depends on the SRS number of Resource Elements (RE) as follows:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Number of SRS RE | CIR/IFFT size |
| (0..64] | 64 |
| [65..128] | 128 |
| ≥129 | 256 |

When the number of SRS RE is less than CIR/IFFT size, zeros are appended (upsampling). When the number of SRS RE is larger than CIR/IFFT size, only CIR/IFFT size number of SRS RE elements are selected (downsampling).

[CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA]

---

##### 5.5.5.5.9.2 Time offset estimation

**5.5.5.5.9.2.0-2**  (ID: `12715117`)

Time offset estimation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall estimate Short-Term Timing Offset, combined and per spatial stream, as described in §2.6.3 of *5GMax Algorithm Specification ([12689047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7O57slZQEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).*

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall calculate Short-Term Timing Offset metric, combined and per spatial stream, as described in §2.6.3 of *5GMax Algorithm Specification ([12689047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7O57slZQEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).*

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the result of combined Short-Term Timing Offset estimate to 5G-L1-UL (BB) as part of message *UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs.*

IE field of UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs:

-*shortTermTaMetric*

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the result of Short-Term Timing Offset estimate, per spatial stream , to 5G-L1-UL (BB) as part of message *UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs.*

IE field of UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs:

-*shortTermTaMetricOfAnt*

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the result of combined Short-Term Timing Offset peak estimate to 5G-L1-UL (BB) as part of message *UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs.*

IE field of UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs:

-*shortTermTaPeakMetric*

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the result of Short-Term Timing Offset peak estimate, per spatial stream, to 5G-L1-UL (BB) as part of message *UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs.*

IE field of UlDataFH\_SrsSuMimoReceiveRespPs:

-*shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt*

[CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA]

---

Interference-plus-noise power estimation
Simplification of the noise power estimation algorithm for SRS for SU-MIMO is introduced by substituting weighting Matrix **S with alternative matrix** M. Matrix **M is derived from LDL decomposition of** S, i.e.,***\*****[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in dark text on a white background. The equation is:
S = V · E · VH = (VE1/2) · (VE1/2)H = MMH
The equation appears to be related to matrix operations, where 'V' and 'E' are likely matrices, and 'H' denotes the conjugate transpose (Hermitian transpose). 'S' and 'M' are also likely matrices. The term E1/2 suggests a matrix square root.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7383.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
Matrix* *M is precomputed and stored in memory. No performance loss expected and, due to* *M having reduced column dimension, less DSP operations are required. The simplified noise power estimate (per chunk block* i, antenna port *p and spatial stream* ant)  is:***\****
[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$\hat{\sigma}*{noise,i,p,ant}^2 = (\hat{H}*{p,sep}^{pilot})^H MM^H \hat{H}*{p,sep}^{pilot} = (M^H \hat{H}*{p,sep}^{pilot})^H (M^H \hat{H}*{p,sep}^{pilot}) = \sum*{k=1}^{R} |[M^H \hat{H}*{p,sep}]*{k}|^2$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7383.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]
 
Full description of the simplification and notation in section "2.6.5" of 5Gmax algorithm specification (5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
[CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA]

##### 5.5.5.5.9.4 Signal power estimation

###### 5.5.5.5.9.4.0-2 Signal power estimation 5G-L1-UL (Radio)  shall estimate signal power per SRS symbol, SRS ports and spatial stream, as described in §2.6.8 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification ( 12689047 ). [CB012115-SR-HA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-HA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] (ID: 12715111)

Rank selection:

The rank selection (also loosely called “RI selection”) based on SRS depends on the SRS SINR, averaged over all receive antenna, and the SRS boost, as described in Section §2.9 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification (5G\_L1\_3966\_replaced([11459265](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The RI selection algorithm is described in Section §2.9 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification document. The RI algorithm consists of the following steps:

* Firstly, if SRS SINR is below the threshold alpha, rank is selected as 1, otherwise a new threshold is computed based on SRS SINR:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$Thr = \frac{\alpha \* SINR\_{SRS}}{(\alpha + SINR\_{SRS})^2}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7390.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

-Secondly, the MMSE smoothed channel estimates of 6 subcarriers, equally spaced over the SRS bandwidth, are used for RI selection. A correlation matrix is computed for each of the chosen MMSE smoothed channel estimates:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$R\_{subc} = H\_{subc}^H H\_{subc}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7390.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

Note that each Rsubc is of size 2x2 (2 SRS ports).

-Finally, the Rank selection decides the preferred transmission rank for a UE as follows:

- If [spectral flatness squared (eigenvalue geometric mean over eigenvalue arithmetic mean squared, i.e., determinant(Rsubc )/trace2(Rsubc )) of every                               Rsubc is greater than or equal to Thr] AND [SINR is larger than alpha], THEN rank=2.

- Otherwise, rank=1.

Quantities needed for RI selection:

1. Signal and noise power:

Antenna specific SRS SNR is computed based on receive antenna specific signal power (Section  §2.6.8 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification) and noise power (Section §2.6.5 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification).

1. SRS power boost:

The SRS power boost value is defined as:

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$P\_{boost\_SRS} = \frac{SRS \ transmit \ power \ per \ subcarrier}{PUSCH \ data \ transmit \ power \ per \ subcarrier}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7390.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

And transmitted to L1 by L2 using parameter powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe in UlData\_srsReceiveReq message. See 5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for info on powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe.

1. RI Selection Threshold, alpha:

[PR711406]

RI selection threshold is given by rdparameter rdUlRiSelectionThresh. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8455\_replaced([11110270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpB3rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: This rdparameter is implemented as integer value with range from 1 to 200 and step size 1, but need to multiple 0.05 when use it to determine RI threshold. This is due to SW limitation. For example, the default value 0.1 corresponds to integer 2.

[End PR711406]

Note: Reference document is 5GMax Algorithm Specification Document (version 11.213) located in 5G\_L1\_3966\_replaced([11459265](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note2: This requirement is applicable regardless of the Fronthaul-duplex technology.

---

Rank selection:

The rank selection (also loosely called “RI selection”) based on SRS depends on the SRS SINR, averaged over all receive antenna, and the SRS boost, as described in Section §2.9 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification (5G\_L1\_3966\_replaced([11459265](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The RI selection algorithm is described in Section §2.9 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification document. The RI algorithm consists of the following steps:

* Firstly, if SRS SINR is below the threshold alpha, rank is selected as 1, otherwise a new threshold is computed based on SRS SINR:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$Thr = \frac{\alpha \* SINR\_{SRS}}{(\alpha + SINR\_{SRS})^2}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7395.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

-Secondly, the MMSE smoothed channel estimates of 6 subcarriers, equally spaced over the SRS bandwidth, are used for RI selection. A correlation matrix is computed for each of the chosen MMSE smoothed channel estimates:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$R\_{subc} = H\_{subc}^H H\_{subc}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7395.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

Note that each Rsubc is of size 2x2 (2 SRS ports).

-Finally, the Rank selection decides the preferred transmission rank for a UE as follows:

- If [spectral flatness squared (eigenvalue geometric mean over eigenvalue arithmetic mean squared, i.e., determinant(Rsubc )/trace2(Rsubc )) of every                               Rsubc is greater than or equal to Thr] AND [SINR is larger than alpha], THEN rank=2.

- Otherwise, rank=1.

Quantities needed for RI selection:

1. Signal and noise (+interference) power:

Antenna specific SRS SNR is computed based on receive antenna specific signal power (Section  §2.6.8 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification) and noise power (Section §2.6.5 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification).

1. SRS power boost:

The SRS power boost value is defined as:

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$P\_{boost\_SRS} = \frac{SRS \ transmit \ power \ per \ subcarrier}{PUSCH \ data \ transmit \ power \ per \ subcarrier}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7395.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

And transmitted to L1 by L2 using parameter powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe [CB013202-A] including 4RX IRC gain [End CB013202-A] in UlData\_srsReceiveReq message. See 5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for info on powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe.

1. RI Selection Threshold, alpha:

FOR [FR2-TDD],

RI selection threshold is given by rdparameter rdUlRiSelectionThresh. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8455\_replaced([11110270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpB3rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: This rdparameter is implemented as integer value with range from 1 to 200 and step size 1, but need to multiple 0.05 when use it to determine RI threshold. This is due to SW limitation. For example, the default value 0.1 corresponds to integer 2.

FOR [FR1-TDD] AND [FR1-FDD],

RI selection threshold is UE specific and provided to L1 by L2 using parameter ulRiSelectionThreshold in UlData\_srsReceiveReq message. See 5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for info on ulRiSelectionThreshold.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Frequency range | RI selection threshold, α |
| FR1-TDD | ulRiSelectionThreshold (5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) |
| FR2-TDD | ulRiSelectionThresh (5G\_UP\_ALG\_8455\_replaced([11110270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpB3rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) |
| FR1-FDD | ulRiSelectionThreshold (5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) |

Note: Reference document is 5GMax Algorithm Specification Document (version 11.213) located in 5G\_L1\_3966\_replaced([11459265](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note2: This requirement is applicable regardless of the Frequency Range-Duplex-Fronthaul technology.

Rank selection:

The rank selection (also loosely called “RI selection”) based on SRS depends on the SRS SINR, averaged over all receive antenna, and the SRS boost, as described in Section §2.9 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification (5G\_L1\_3966\_replaced([11459265](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The RI selection algorithm is described in Section §2.9 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification document. The RI algorithm consists of the following steps:

* Firstly, if SRS SINR is below the threshold alpha, rank is selected as 1, otherwise a new threshold is computed based on SRS SINR:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$Thr = \frac{\alpha \* SINR\_{SRS}}{(\alpha + SINR\_{SRS})^2}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7401.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

-Secondly, the MMSE smoothed channel estimates of 6 subcarriers, equally spaced over the SRS bandwidth, are used for RI selection. A correlation matrix is computed for each of the chosen MMSE smoothed channel estimates:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$R\_{subc} = H\_{subc}^H H\_{subc}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7401.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

Note that each Rsubc is of size 2x2 (2 SRS ports).

-Finally, the Rank selection decides the preferred transmission rank for a UE as follows:

- If [spectral flatness squared (eigenvalue geometric mean over eigenvalue arithmetic mean squared, i.e., determinant(Rsubc )/trace2(Rsubc )) of every                               Rsubc is greater than or equal to Thr] AND [SINR is larger than alpha], THEN rank=2.

- Otherwise, rank=1.

Quantities needed for RI selection:

1. Signal and noise (+interference) power:

Antenna specific SRS SNR is computed based on receive antenna specific signal power (Section  §2.6.8 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification) and noise power (Section §2.6.5 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification).

1. SRS power boost:

The SRS power boost value is defined as:

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$P\_{boost\_SRS} = \frac{SRS \ transmit \ power \ per \ subcarrier}{PUSCH \ data \ transmit \ power \ per \ subcarrier}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_7401.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

And transmitted to L1 by L2 using parameter powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe including [CB013202-A] 4RX or [End CB013202-A] 8RX IRC gain in UlData\_srsReceiveReq message. See 5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for info on powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe.

1. RI Selection Threshold, alpha:

FOR [FR2-TDD],

RI selection threshold is given by rdparameter rdUlRiSelectionThresh. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8455\_replaced([11110270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpB3rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: This rdparameter is implemented as integer value with range from 1 to 200 and step size 1, but need to multiple 0.05 when use it to determine RI threshold. This is due to SW limitation. For example, the default value 0.1 corresponds to integer 2.

FOR [FR1-TDD] AND [FR1-FDD],

RI selection threshold is UE specific and provided to L1 by L2 using parameter ulRiSelectionThreshold in UlData\_srsReceiveReq message. See 5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for info on ulRiSelectionThreshold.

**Rank selection:**

The rank selection (also loosely called “RI selection”) based on SRS depends on the SRS SINR, averaged over all receive antenna, and the SRS boost, as described in Section §2.9.1 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification ([12689047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7O57slZQEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)). The RI algorithm consists of the following steps:

* Firstly, if SRS SINR is below the threshold *alpha, rank is selected as 1, otherwise a new threshold is computed based on SRS SINR:*

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$Thr = \frac{\alpha \* SINR\_{SRS}}{(\alpha + SINR\_{SRS})^2}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_8495.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

-Secondly, the MMSE smoothed channel estimates of 6 subcarriers, equally spaced over the SRS bandwidth, are used for RI selection. A correlation matrix is computed for each of the chosen MMSE smoothed channel estimates:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$R\_{subc} = H\_{subc}^H H\_{subc}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_8495.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

Note that each **Rsubc is of size 2x2 (2 SRS ports).**

-Finally, the **Rank selection decides the preferred transmission rank for a UE as follows:**

- If [spectral flatness squared (eigenvalue geometric mean over eigenvalue arithmetic mean squared, i.e., determinant(**Rsubc )/trace2(**Rsubc )) of every                               **Rsubc is greater than or equal to *Thr] AND [SINR is larger than \*alpha], THEN rank=2.*****\***

- Otherwise, rank=1.

**Quantities needed for RI selection:**

**1. Signal and noise (+interference) power:**

Antenna specific SRS SNR is computed based on receive antenna specific signal power (Section  §2.6.8 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification) and noise power (Section §2.6.5 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification).

**2. SRS power boost:**

The SRS power boost value is defined as:

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$P\_{\text{boost\_SRS}} = \frac{\text{SRS transmit power per subcarrier}}{\text{PUSCH data transmit power per subcarrier}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_8495.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

And transmitted to L1-RU by L1-DU using parameter *powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe in* UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message. See [11517212](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSJjSPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for info on *powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe.*\*\*

**3. RI Selection Threshold, alpha:**

RI selection threshold is UE specific and provided to 5G-L1-UL (Radio) by 5G-L1-UL (BB) using parameter *ulRiSelectionThreshold in* UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message. See [11517212](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSJjSPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for info on *ulRiSelectionThreshold.*\*\*

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Frequency range** | **RI selection threshold,** **α** |
| FR1-TDD | *ulRiSelectionThreshold* ([11517212](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSJjSPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |

**Note: Reference document is 5GMax Algorithm Specification Document located in [11469930](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fB5w5vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).**

**Note3: For Rank Indicator selection the decimated 12 subcarriers after channel smoothing are downsampled to 6 subcarriers evenly distributed across the entire SRS Bandwidth, see IE *SRSBandwidth and *SRSBandwidthConfig in* UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message ([11517212](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSJjSPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).***\*\*

**Note4: *ulRiSelectionThreshold in \*UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message ([11517212](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSJjSPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is forwarded and calculated by L2-PS.***\*

---

##### 5.5.5.5.10.2 Precoding Matrix Indication selection

###### 5.5.5.5.10.2.0-1 Precoding Matrix Indication selection SINR extimation for the prefered Precoding Matrix Index (ID: 11464192)

**5.5.5.5.10.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11464205`)

Precoding Matrix Indication selection
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall estimate the SINR for the prefered Precoding Matrix Index:

* For rank1, as described in §2.9.1.1 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification (5G\_L1\_3957\_replaced([11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* For rank2, as described in §2.9.1.2 of 5GMax Algorithm Specification (5G\_L1\_3957\_replaced([11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

IE in srsSuMimo structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq (5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

-powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe:

* For Loki: corresponds to pBoost value [CB013202-A] including 4RX IRC gain [End CB013202-A] in PMI selection algorithm.
* For Thor: corresponds to pBoost value including [CB013202-A] 4RX or [End CB013202-A] 8RX IRC gain in PMI selection algorithm.

-puschTransCoherence, used to select the correct precoding matrix table

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the predicted SINR, If the computed value is larger than 40dB, 5G-L1-UL (Radio) shall cap it to 40dB, for the prefered Precoding Matrix Index to 5G-L1-UL (BB) as part of message UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs (5G\_L1\_IF\_253\_replaced([11514446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PcfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

* For rank1:

IE in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs :

-ulPmiRank1Sinr

* For rank2:

IE in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs :

-ulPmiRank2Sinr

---

###### 5.5.5.5.10.2.0-2 Precoding Matrix Indication selection Supported new IE fullPowerPuschPowerScalingRatio (ID: 11464213)

**5.5.5.5.10.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11464218`)

Precoding Matrix Indication selection
L1L2 itf shall support a new IE in srsSuMimoStruct of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq called fullPowerPuschPowerScalingRatio. See 5G\_L1\_IF\_14078\_replaced([11514394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008325-5G-AA] The requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor HW [End CB008325-5G-AA].

[CB007814-G] This requirement also applies to ABIO FR1-FDD-eCPRI. [End CB007814-G]

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009443-C] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.[End CB009443-C]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

[CB010969-SR-CB] This requirement shall be supported in Thor for FR1-FDD-OBSAI. [End CB010969-SR-CB]

---

##### 5.5.5.5.10.3 Noise-plus-Interference power calculation

###### 5.5.5.5.10.3.0-1 Noise-plus-Interference power calculation [Information Text] Noise-plus-Interference power calculation is part of SINR calculation ( 11464238 ). No separated Noise-plus-Interference measurement is reported to L2PS. Implicitly included within SINR measurement. (ID: 12715160)

##### 5.5.5.5.10.4 Signal power calculation

###### 5.5.5.5.10.4.0-1 Signal power calculation [Information Text] Signal power calculation is part of SINR calculation (( 11470200 )). No separated Signal power measurement is reported to L2PS. Implicitly included within SINR measurement. (ID: 12715159)

##### 5.5.5.5.10.5 SINR calculation

**5.5.5.5.10.5.0-1**  (ID: `12715189`)

SINR calculation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall compute the combined and per spatial stream Signal-to-Interference-plus-Noise-Ratio (SINR), as described in §2.7.5.3 of *5GMax Algorithm Specification ([11469927](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fB5w5fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the SINR estimate to 5G-L2-PS as part of message *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs.*

IE fields in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs:

-*sinr.*

-*sinrOfAnt.*

[CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA]

---

##### 5.5.5.5.10.6 Measurement report

###### 5.5.5.5.10.6.1 DTX

**5.5.5.5.10.6.1.0-1**  (ID: `12715214`)

DTX
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall calculate the DTX (discontinous transmission) estimate using *antenna-wise processing method as described in §2.6.6 of* 5GMax Algorithm Specification ([12689047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7O57slZQEfC45IKMrv0u7Q)).\*\*

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the result of DTX estimate to 5G-L2-PS as part of message *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs.*

IE field in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs:

-*dtx*

[CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA]

---

###### 5.5.5.5.10.6.2 Time Offset Estimate

**5.5.5.5.10.6.2.0-2**  (ID: `12715350`)

Time Offset Estimate
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the result of combined Short-Term Timing Offset estimate to 5G-L2-PS as part of message *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs.*

IE field of UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs:

-*shortTermTaMetric*

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the result of Short-Term Timing Offset estimate, per spatial stream , to 5G-L2-PS as part of message *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs.*

IE field of UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs:

-*shortTermTaMetricOfAnt*

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the result of combined Short-Term Timing Offset peak estimate to 5G-L2-PS as part of message *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs.*

IE field of UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs:

-*shortTermTaPeakMetric*

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the result of Short-Term Timing Offset peak estimate, per spatial stream, to 5G-L2-PS as part of message *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs.*

IE field of UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs:

-*shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt*

[CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA]

---

###### 5.5.5.5.10.6.3 Received Power

**5.5.5.5.10.6.3.0-1**  (ID: `12715219`)

Received Power
5G**-L1-UL (BB) shall estimate, per spatial stream, UL received power on SRS as described in §2.7.4.3 of *5GMax Algorithm Specification ([12689047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7O57slZQEfC45IKMrv0u7Q)).***

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report, per spatial stream, the result UL received power to 5G-L2-PS as part of message *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs.*

IE field of UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs:

-*rxPowerOfAnt*

[CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA]

---

###### 5.5.5.5.10.6.4 Antenna-wise measurements

**5.5.5.5.10.6.4.0-1**  (ID: `12715220`)

Antenna-wise measurements
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the result of antenna-wise measurements in below order:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Antenna-wise measurement index** | **patternId index** | ceAxcIndex |
| antenna-wise meas[0] | patternId[0] | ceAxCIndex[0] |
| antenna-wise meas[1] | patternId[0] | ceAxCIndex[1] |
| antenna-wise meas[2] | patternId[1] | ceAxCIndex[2] |
| … | … |  |
| antenna-wise meas[k-2] | patternId[k/2-1] | ceAxCIndex[k-2] |
| antenna-wise meas[k-1] | patternId[k/2-1] | ceAxCIndex[k-1] |

where **k is the value of *numCeAxcIndex in *srsSuMimo structure of message* UlData\_SrsReceiveReq  ([11514379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).***\*\*

The antenna-wise measurements are *rxPowerOfAnt,* sinrOfAnt, *shortTermTaMetricOfAnt and* shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt.\*\*\*\*

Note: for non-BF configurations, 'patternId index' is meaningless.

[CB012115-SR-IA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA]

---

###### 5.5.5.5.10.6.5 Compensation factor

**5.5.5.5.10.6.5.0-1**  (ID: `13239726`)

Compensation factor
When split-panel is configured (ulSubcellType=15, A8, and suSplitpanelMode in UlData\_SrsReceiveReq is validated according to ([13240176](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_gqk8MsBuEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))), the following measurements:

* Antenna-wise measurements: rxPowerOfAnt in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs ([11514446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PcfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

are scaled according to ([13283493](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2081UMsyEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_2081umsyefcybiz6acpphw?oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9")), where a subpanel compensation factor (scomp) is included.

Note2: Compensation factor (scomp) is described in §5.3.1.1 section of Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification ([12708616](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aUzKUWMCEfC3KtQ77je1xA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) and received signal power metric is described in §2.8.4.3 ("Measurements.UL Receive Signal Power.SRS") section of 5GMax - 5G New Radio Algorithm Specification ([12689047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7O57slZQEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

---

#### 5.5.5.5.11 Interworking with other channels

##### 5.5.5.5.11.1 Loner

###### 5.5.5.5.11.1.0-1 Loner L1-SW shall support long PUCCH with scheduled SRS SU-MIMO in same OFDM symbol of a slot for FR1 TDD. PRBs are divided into PUCCH area and PUSCH area by L2-PS. PRBs related to PUSCH area are assigned to SRS SU-MIMO, by L2-PS, with the restriction that the number of PRBs assigned for SRS SU-MIMO should be integer multiple of 4. FDM of long PUCCH and "SRS for SU-MIMO" on same OFDM symbol should be supported by L1. (ID: 11464260)

##### 5.5.5.5.11.2 Loki

**5.5.5.5.11.2.0-1**  (ID: `11464272`)

Loki
L1-SW shall support SRS for SU-MIMO inside the PRB region allocated for PUSCH.

No SRS can be allocated outside the PRB region for PUSCH.

The number of PRB allocated for SRS must be a multiple of 4.

FDM of Long PUCCH and SRS SU-MIMO in the same OFDM symbol shall be supported.

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009881-A, CB009881-W] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.[End CB009443-A, CB009881-W]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

---

##### 5.5.5.5.11.3 Thor

**5.5.5.5.11.3.0-2**  (ID: `12591209`)

Thor
5G-L1-UL(BB) shall support SRS for SU-MIMO inside the PRB region allocated for PUSCH.

5G-L1-UL(BB) shall not expect SRS to be allocated outside the PRB region for PUSCH.

Frequency-Domain Multiplex of Long PUCCH and SRS for SU-MIMO in the same OFDM symbol shall be supported.

[CB013442-SR-D] Note: This requirement is common for all FR1 technologies. **[End CB013442-SR-D]**

---

##### 5.5.5.5.11.4 Odin

**5.5.5.5.11.4.0-1**  (ID: `12715156`)

Odin
5G-L1-UL(BB) shall support SRS for SU-MIMO inside the PRB region allocated for PUSCH.

5G-L1-UL(BB) shall not expect SRS to be allocated outside the PRB region for PUSCH.

Frequency-Domain Multiplex of Long PUCCH and SRS for SU-MIMO in the same OFDM symbol shall be supported.

---

### 5.5.5.6 SRS_POS Precise Positioning: Parameter estimation in Antenna (AxC) domain

#### 5.5.5.6.0-1 SRS_POS Precise Positioning: Parameter estimation in Antenna (AxC) domain This section describes the SRS reception and measurements when SRS is used for Precise Positioning purposes. (ID: 11464294)

#### 5.5.5.6.1 Overview, receiver architecture and algorithms

##### 5.5.5.6.1.1 Positioning message support

###### 5.5.5.6.1.1.0-1 Positioning message support 5G-L1-UL shall use the IEs in the UlData_SrsPosReceiveReq message (5G_L1_IF_15340_replaced( 11514526 )) for Precise Positioning as described in this chapter. (ID: 11464314)

##### 5.5.5.6.1.2 SRS streams support or positioning purpose

**5.5.5.6.1.2.0-3**  (ID: `12720952`)

SRS streams support or positioning purpose
5G-L1-UL shall extract SRS streams per antenna.

In C4 [CB013273-C] /C2 [End CB013273-C] subcell, the order of ceAxCId is PUSCH, PRACH, and NDM-SRS when SRS is used for Precise Positioning ([11513484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In C4S subcell, there is only 4 NDM-SRS streams.

[CB013273-A] In C8S subcell, there is only 8 NDM-SRS streams. [End CB013273-A]

---

co-located Rx antennas

There are some different scenarios where Rx antennas are located per radio:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a series of diagrams illustrating different arrangements of "eAxCs" originating from a larger rectangular block. Each diagram is numbered and has a descriptive label.
Here's a breakdown of each diagram:
1. **Diagram 1:** Labeled "1) All co-located". It shows a single oval encompassing multiple arrows originating from the block, indicating all eAxCs are at the same location.
2. **Diagram 2:** Labeled "2) 2 locations". It shows two separate ovals, each containing multiple arrows, indicating eAxCs are distributed across two distinct locations.
3. **Diagram 3:** Labeled "3) 4 locations". It shows four individual arrows, each with a small circle at its tip, originating from the block and spaced apart, indicating eAxCs are at four separate locations.
4. **Diagram 4:** Labeled "4) All co-located". Similar to diagram 1, it shows a single oval encompassing a larger number of arrows originating from the block, reinforcing the concept of all eAxCs being at the same location.
5. **Diagram 5:** Labeled "5) 2 locations". Similar to diagram 2, it shows two separate ovals, each containing multiple arrows, indicating eAxCs are distributed across two distinct locations.
6. **Diagram 6:** Labeled "6) 4 locations". Similar to diagram 3, it shows four individual arrows, each with a small circle at its tip, originating from the block and spaced apart, indicating eAxCs are at four separate locations.
7. **Diagram 7:** Labeled "7) 8 locations". It shows eight individual arrows, each with a small circle at its tip, originating from the block and spaced apart, indicating eAxCs are at eight separate locations.
The diagrams visually represent different spatial distributions or groupings of eAxCs. The text "eAxCs" is consistently placed to the left of each diagram, serving as a label for the elements depicted. The overall color scheme is a dark teal for the blocks and arrows, against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-07301318.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Case 1) is supported in C4 and C4S subcell

Case 2) is supported only in C4S [CB013273-C] and C2 [End CB013273-C] subcell

Case 3) is supported only in C4S subcell

[CB013273-A]

Case 4) is supported in C8S subcell.

Case 5) is supported in C4, C4S and C8S subcell

Case 6) is supported in [CB013273-C] C2, [End CB013273-C] C4S and C8S subcell.

Case 7) is supported in C4S, C8S subcell.

[End CB013273-A]

C4S [CB013273-A] or C8S [End CB013273-A] has to know which case is configured, and that is done with UlCell\_SetupReq message, see object [12719804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Vpe44GxREfCRGai1q1VTeQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

Original document is stored in [CB013273](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:f:/r/sites/ATFL1Spec/L1%20AS%20documents/Reference%20materials/CB013273?csf=1&web=1&e=lbHSfZ).

#### 5.5.5.6.2 Raw channel estimation

##### 5.5.5.6.2.0-3 Raw channel estimation Informaiton text Due to properties of Low PAPR sequences, each RawCE contains the frequency domain channel response of all the channels that share the same triplet of {sequenceId, transmissionComb, numPrb}. UE port specific channel responses are multiplexed. (ID: 11464373)

estimation The goal of High Precision TOE is to reach a level of precision that translates to sub-meter precision in locating the UE. This goal is achieved by applying certain interpolation processes that are described in this chapter. The following diagram provides a general comparitive depiction of time-steps, granularities, and ranges. The details shall be specified when required. [image-0][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating the structure of an OFDM symbol and its processing. The diagram shows a timeline with different segments labeled. At the top, there are two horizontal arrows indicating time durations. The top arrow spans approximately 0.5ms/14, which is about 35.714 microseconds. The second arrow below it is divided into two parts: the first part is approximately 2.381 microseconds, and the second part is 1/30KHz, which is approximately 33.333 microseconds. Below these time indicators, there is a representation of an OFDM symbol divided into two parts: "CP" (Cyclic Prefix) and "OFDM symbol". The CP segment is shown as a shorter duration at the beginning, followed by the main OFDM symbol. Further down, "FFT Length: 2048" is indicated, with a horizontal arrow spanning this length. Below this, there is a segment labeled "146 samples" with a bracket indicating its duration. An arrow pointing downwards signifies an "Interpolation" process. Finally, below the interpolation arrow, a longer segment is labeled "16384 samples". At the bottom, there is a smaller segment labeled "1170 samples" with the text "4Tc granularity" in red below it. This segment also has a bracket indicating its duration. The overall diagram visually represents the relationship between different time durations, sample counts, and processing steps in an OFDM system.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_pukkola_5G_L1_Entity_Level_file_7434.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] (ID: 11464389)

##### 5.5.5.6.3.1 Channel impulse response calculation

**5.5.5.6.3.1.0-2**  (ID: `11464407`)

Channel impulse response calculation
5G-L1-UL shall calculate the time domain Channel Impulse Response (CIR) from each RawCE (5G\_L1\_15615\_replaced([11464353](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBQQpvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) by applying IFFT, as described in section 2.7.2 of 5GMax Specification.

When SRS is used for Precise Positioning, the IFFT size is only determined by transmissionComb in SrsPosReportRequest:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| transmissionComb | IFFT size |
| 2 | 2048 |
| 4 | 1024 |

Since the size of RawCE may not match the IFFT size, size matching is required as described in 5GMax Specification. It includes zero-padding to the right and left sides of RawCE, then swapping the first and second half of the result.

The output of IFFT is the time-domain CIR of all the channels that share the same base sequence.

[Before CB007880-A]

Note: Only 1 attached UE shall be tested in CB010332-B, for which only 1 unique base sequence is needed. The restriction will be lifted by another feature in the same release.

[End CB007880-A]

---

##### 5.5.5.6.3.2 Base rate peak detection

###### 5.5.5.6.3.2.0-1 Base rate peak detection 'Base Rate' refers to the sampling rate before upsampling (interpolation). 'Base Rate Peak Detection' is performed to find an initial estimate of TO which will be further refined by the 'High Precision Time-Offset Calculation'. (ID: 11464418)

###### 5.5.5.6.3.2.1 PDP calculation

###### 5.5.5.6.3.2.1.0-1 PDP calculation 5G-L1-UL shall calculate Power Delay Profile (PDP) from each CIR, and extract UE port specific PDP according to corresponding cyclicShift in srsPosReceiveRequest, as described in section 2.7.2 of 5GMax Specification. (ID: 11464429)

###### 5.5.5.6.3.2.2 TOE search window calculation

**5.5.5.6.3.2.2.0-2**  (ID: `11464449`)

TOE search window calculation
5G-L1-UL(BB) shall calculate the TOE search window for high precision TOE calculation for each co-located antenna(s) (as TRPs, see 5G\_L1\_17026\_replaced([11464787](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBTT8fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as the following steps:

* 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall get the number of multiplexed cyclic shifts for L1-search-window calculation:
* For the Users attached to the current cell, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall parse all srsPos Users (contains in UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message, 5G\_L1\_IF\_15340\_replaced([11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and suMiMo users (contains in srsSuMimo structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message, 5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to get the number of multiplexed cyclic shifts in the comb with same sequenceId.
* For all the from neighbour cells, [CB007880-D] per TRP, [End CB007880-D] 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall parse all srsPos Users (contains in UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message, 5G\_L1\_IF\_15340\_replaced([11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to get the number of multiplexed cyclic shifts in the comb with same sequenceId for each neighbour cell (See decision #15 in CFAM chapter1.1.4 for details).
* 5G-L1-UL(BB) shall convert sfnInitTimeOffset of UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15340\_replaced([11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to window offset Woffset for L1-search-window calculation.

[CB007880-F]

* 5G-L1-UL(BB) shall calculate the LMF-search-window using the parameters expectedPropagationDelay[], delayUncertainty[] and sfnInitTimeOffset in UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15340\_replaced([11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and also calculate the LMF-search-window length.
* 5G-L1-UL(BB) shall calculate the L1-search-window length as NIFFT /NCS,

where

* NIFFT is IFFT length and defined in 5G\_L1\_16873\_replaced([11464395](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBQQrPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),
* NCS is the number of multiplexed cyclic shifts per comb. Note: In case two ports SRS and one port SRS are multiplexed in the same comb with same sequenceId, the number of multiplexed cyclic shifts is 4.
* IF R&D parameter rdSearchWindowOption (5G\_L1\_17164\_replaced([11465368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBW-XfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) =0 (L1SearchWindow):

[End CB007880-F]

* 5G-L1-UL(BB) shall set the TOE search window as L1-search-window.

[CB007880-F]

* IF case R&D parameter rdSearchWindowOption (5G\_L1\_17164\_replaced([11465368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBW-XfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) =1 (LMFSearchWindow)
* IF LMF-search-window length > L1-search-window length:

o 5G-L1-UL(BB) shall set the TOE search window as L1-search-window.

* ELSE:

o 5G-L1-UL(BB) shall set the TOE search window as LMF-search-window.

* IF case R&D parameter rdSearchWindowOption (5G\_L1\_17164\_replaced([11465368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBW-XfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) =2 (LMFL1TOECombined)
* IF LMF-search-window length > L1-search-window length:

o 5G-L1-UL(BB) shall set the TOE search window as L1-search-window.

* ELSE IF the LMF-search-window range within the L1-search-window range:

o 5G-L1-UL(BB) shall set the TOE search window as L1-search-window.

* ELSE:

o 5G-L1-UL(BB) shall set the TOE search window as LMF-search-window.

[End CB007880-F]

Note:

* In shared TRP case, the FFT size (used for search window calculation) for the precision positioning UEs from neighbour cell are obtained according to the bandwidth of current cell because all shared TRP cells have same cell bandwidth configuration (see decision #16 in CFAM 1.1.4 for details).
* The algorithm of TOE search window calculation is described in section 2.7.2.1 of 5G New Radio Algorithm Specification.

###### 5.5.5.6.3.2.3 PDP combination

**5.5.5.6.3.2.3.0-4**  (ID: `12721131`)

PDP combination
When SRS is used for Precise Positioning,

* **[Before CB013273-A] In case**[CB013273-A] IF **[End CB013273-A]  (R&D parameter rdToEAlgoSelection ([11465378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBXlYfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) =0 (‘CombinedToE’))**\*\*\*\*

**[CB013273-A] OR (ulsubcellType = C8S ([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))** AND 8 co-located antennas ([12719810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_siyy-WxREfCRGai1q1VTeQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), 1 TRP)):**[End CB013273-A]**\*\*\*\*

-  5G-L1-UL shall linearly combine all PDPs within the TOE search window (as described in[11464436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBQ3tPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) sent from all ports and received from all co-located antenna(s) (as TRPs, see [11464787](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBTT8fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), for each UE, as described in section 2.7.2.1 of 5GMax Specification.

* **[Before CB013273-A] In case**[CB013273-A] ELSE IF **[End CB013273-A] R&D parameter rdToEAlgoSelection ([11465378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBXlYfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) =1 (‘MinimumToE’):**\*\*\*\*
* Per each antenna stream of the TRP (co-located antenna(s)), 5G-L1-UL shall linearly combine all PDPs within the TOE search window (as described in[11464436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBQ3tPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) **sent from all ports, for each UE, as described in section 2.7.2.2 of 5GMax Specification.**

###### 5.5.5.6.3.2.4 Peak determination

###### 5.5.5.6.3.2.4.1 Combined method

**5.5.5.6.3.2.4.1.0-4**  (ID: `12721285`)

Combined method
In case R&D parameter rdToEAlgoSelection (5G\_L1\_17166\_replaced([11465378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBXlYfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) =0 (‘CombinedToE’) **[CB013273-A] OR (ulsubcellType = C8S ([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))** AND 8 co-located antennas ([12719810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_siyy-WxREfCRGai1q1VTeQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), 1 TRP)):**[End CB013273-A]**\*\*\*\*

* When PDP of all streams co-located antenna(s) **and ports are combined for each UE, 5G-L1-UL shall perform the following steps**

IF srsTdoaJumpMethodEnable ([12980767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FwWhsLksEfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) = false:

1. Find the maximum value of the combined PDP for each UE. (PDPMax)
2. Find local maxima of the combined PDP for each UE, by searching in sliding window of the size 3, that is, a local maximum shall be detected when a combined PDP sample is greater than its immediate neighboring samples.
3. The index pertaining to the first local maximum that equals or exceeds (*rdSrsFirstPeakDetecThreshold ^2) \* PDPMax shall be considered as the Base Precision Time-Offset. R&D parameter used in this process is defined in 5G\_L1\_15989\_replaced([11465363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBW-XPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*

IF srsTdoaJumpMethodEnable ([12980767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FwWhsLksEfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) = true:

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall detect the first local peak as described in 5GMax Specification using the parameters srsTdoaJumpFirstPeakThreshold and srsTdoaJumpRate (provided in ([12980767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FwWhsLksEfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)))

Note:

* The configuration of co-located antenna(s) (as TRPs) is provided by *trpAntStreamMapping in* UlCell\_SetupReq message ([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*
* The co-located antenna(s)(as TRPs) for measurement are indicated by *measTrps of* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message ([11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))\*\*
* The algorithm of peak determination is described in section 2.7.2.1 of 5GMax Specification

###### 5.5.5.6.3.2.4.2 Min method

**5.5.5.6.3.2.4.2.0-2**  (ID: `12721321`)

Min method
In case R&D parameter rdToEAlgoSelection (5G\_L1\_17166\_replaced([11465378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBXlYfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) =1 ( ‘MinimumToE’):

**[CB013273-A]**

IF ulsubcellType = C8S ([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) **AND 8 co-located antennas ([12719810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_siyy-WxREfCRGai1q1VTeQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), 1 TRP):**

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall perform PDP peak determination with Combined method as described in [11464485: Combined method](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBQ3vPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

ELSE:

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall perform PDP peak determination with Min method with the following steps:

**[End CB013273-A]**

IF srsTdoaJumpMethodEnable ([12980767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FwWhsLksEfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) = false:

* When PDP combination for all ports are combined for each UE ([11464456](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBQ3t_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G-L1-UL shall perform the following steps.
* Find the maximum value of the combined PDP over all streams co-located antenna(s). (PDPMax)
* Per each antenna stream:
* Find local maxima of the combined PDP for each UE, by searching in sliding window of the size 3, that is, a local maximum shall be detected when a combined PDP sample is greater than its immediate neighboring samples.
* The index pertaining to the first local maximum that equals or exceeds (*rdSrsFirstPeakDetecThreshold ^2) \* PDPMax shall be considered as the Base Precision Time-Offset. R&D parameter used in this process is defined in [11465363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBW-XPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).*

IF srsTdoaJumpMethodEnable ([12980767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FwWhsLksEfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) = true:

* 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall detect the first local peak as described in 5GMax Specification using the parameters srsTdoaJumpFirstPeakThreshold and srsTdoaJumpRate (provided in ([12980767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FwWhsLksEfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))).

Note:

* The configuration of co-located antenna(s) (as TRPs) is provided by *trpAntStreamMapping in* UlCell\_SetupReq message ([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*
* The co-located antenna(s)(as TRPs) for measurement are indicated by *measTrps of* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message ([11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))\*\*
* The algorithm of peak determination is described in section 2.7.2.2 of 5GMax Specification

##### 5.5.5.6.3.3 High precision time offset calculation

###### 5.5.5.6.3.3.0-1 High precision time offset calculation Time step between 2 samples of time domain CIR (or equivalently, PDP) is ~16ns, which corresponds to ~5m distance granularity. In order to achieve sub-meter granularity, it is needed to upsample (interpolate) CIR (or PDP) by a factor of 8. (ID: 11464526)

###### 5.5.5.6.3.3.1 High precision time offset calculation for PRBs &gt; 60

###### 5.5.5.6.3.3.1.1 Combined method

**5.5.5.6.3.3.1.1.0-4**  (ID: `12721347`)

Combined method
In case R&D parameter rdToEAlgoSelection (([11465378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBXlYfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) =0 (‘CombinedToE’) **[CB013273-A] OR (ulsubcellType = C8S ([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))** AND 8 co-located antennas ([12719810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_siyy-WxREfCRGai1q1VTeQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), 1 TRP)):**[End CB013273-A]**\*\*\*\*

* **According to 5GMax Specification, per each UE and per each co-located antenna(s) (as TRPs, indicated by *measTrps of *UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message, [11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),* *when* numPrb > 60, \*\*5G-L1-UL shall perform the following steps, as described in section 2.7.2.1 of 5GMax Specification*****\***\*
* 5G-L1-UL shall perform Truncated Sinc Interpolation by applying Polyphase filter on the time domain CIR around the Base Precision Time-Offset ([11464485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBQ3vPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* 5G-L1-UL shall calculate PDP of the upsampled CIR, then linearly combine all PDPs sent from all ports and received from all **co-located antennas.**
* 5G-L1-UL shall find the peak of the result, further apply Parabolic Interpolation around the peak, and find the time index corresponding to the maximum PDP, relative to Base Rate Time-Offset.
* 5G-L1-UL shall calculate High Precision Time-Offset as described in section 2.7.2.1 of 5GMax Specification.

Note 1: Design parameters of the Polyphase filter are: upsampling rate of 4, group delay of 6, and roll-off factor of 0.25.

Note 2: Polyphase filtering is done at base rate. For each CIR sample, Polyphase filter returns 4 samples.

Note 3: Maximum memory required to perform Polyphase filtering is determined by the length of filter.

**Note 4: Polyphase filtering is done as convolution in time domain. The number of samples fed to the filter shall be chosen accordingly, not to further compromise the precision.**

**Note 5: Cyclic Prefix and FFT window shall be accounted for when final Time-Offset is being calculated.**

---

###### 5.5.5.6.3.3.1.2 Min method

**5.5.5.6.3.3.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `12721385`)

Min method
In case R&D parameter rdToEAlgoSelection (5G\_L1\_17166\_replaced([11465378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBXlYfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) =1 (‘MinimumToE’):

**[CB013273-A]**

IF ulsubcellType = C8S ([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) **AND 8 co-located antennas ([12719810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_siyy-WxREfCRGai1q1VTeQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), 1 TRP)):**

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall perform High precision time offset calculation for PRBs > 60 with Combined method as described in [11464537: Combined method](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBRexvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

ELSE:

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall perform High precision time offset calculation for PRBs > 60 with Min method as the following steps:

**[End CB013273-A]**

**According to 5GMax Specification, per each UE per each co-located antenna(s) (as TRPs, indicated by *measTrps of *UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message, [11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),* *when* numPrb > 60, 5G-L1-UL shall perform the following steps , as described in section 2.7.2.2 of 5GMax Specification.***\*\*\*\*

* Per each antenna stream of the TRP:
* 5G-L1-UL shall perform Truncated Sinc Interpolation by applying Polyphase filter on the time domain CIR around the Base Precision Time-Offset ([11464485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBQ3vPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* 5G-L1-UL shall calculate PDP of the upsampled CIR, then linearly combine all PDPs sent from all ports and received from all antennas of the TRP.
* 5G-L1-UL shall find the peak of the result, further apply Parabolic Interpolation around the peak, and find the time index corresponding to the maximum PDP, relative to Base Rate Time-Offset.
* 5G-L1-UL shall calculate High Precision Time-Offset as described in section 2.7.2.2 of 5GMax Specification.
* The final High Precision Time-Offset of the TRP for the UE is the minimum time-offset over all antenna streams of the TRP.

Note 1: Design parameters of the Polyphase filter are: upsampling rate of 4, group delay of 6, and roll-off factor of 0.25.

Note 2: Polyphase filtering is done at base rate. For each CIR sample, Polyphase filter returns 4 samples.

Note 3: Maximum memory required to perform Polyphase filtering is determined by the length of filter.

**Note 4: Polyphase filtering is done as convolution in time domain. The number of samples fed to the filter shall be chosen accordingly, not to further compromise the precision.**

**Note 5: Cyclic Prefix and FFT window shall be accounted for when final Time-Offset is being calculated.**

---

###### 5.5.5.6.3.3.2 High precision time offset calculation for PRBs &lt;= 60

###### 5.5.5.6.3.3.2.1 Combined method

###### 5.5.5.6.3.3.2.1.0-4 Combined method In case R&amp;D parameter rdToEAlgoSelection ( 11465378 ) =0 (‘CombinedToE’) [CB013273-A] OR (ulsubcellType = C8S ( 11513449 ) AND 8 co-located antennas ( 12719810 , 1 TRP)): [End CB013273-A] **** According to 5GMax Specification, per each UE and per each co-located antenna(s) (as TRPs, indicated by measTrps of UlData_SrsPosReceiveReq message, 11514526 ), when numPrb &lt;= 60, 5G-L1-UL shall perform Parabolic Interpolation on the combined PDP ( 11464456 ) around the Base Rate Time-Offset, and calculate High Precision Time-Offset as described in section 2.7.2.1 of 5GMax Specification. ** (ID: 12721454)

###### 5.5.5.6.3.3.2.2 Min method

**5.5.5.6.3.3.2.2.0-2**  (ID: `12721456`)

Min method
In case R&D parameter rdToEAlgoSelection ([11465378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBXlYfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) =1 (‘MinimumToE’):

**[CB013273-A]**

IF ulsubcellType = C8S ([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) **AND 8 co-located antennas ([12719810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_siyy-WxREfCRGai1q1VTeQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), 1 TRP):**

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall perform High precision time offset calculation for PRBs <= 60 with Combined method as described in [11464580: Combined method](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBRezfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

ELSE:

5G-L1-UL (BB) shall perform High precision time offset calculation for PRBs <= 60 with Min method as the following steps:

**[End CB013273-A]**

**According to 5GMax Specification, per each UE and per each co-located antenna(s) (as TRPs, indicated by *measTrps of *UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message, [11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), when* numPrb <= 60:***\*\*

* Per each antenna stream of the TRP:

o 5G-L1-UL shall perform Parabolic Interpolation on the combined PDP ([11464456](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBQ3t_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) around the Base Rate Time-Offset, and calculate High Precision Time-Offset as described in section 2.7.2.2 of 5GMax Specification.

-  The final High Precision Time-Offset of the TRP for the UE is the minimum time-offset over all antenna streams of the TRP.
