#### 5.5.5.6.4 Time offset compensation

##### 5.5.5.6.4.0-1 Time offset compensation When SRS is used for Precise Positioning, 5G-L1-UL shall further compensate the Time Offset using High Precision Time-Offset, as described in section 2.7.3 of 5GMax Specification. Notice: According to decision #13, the Priority is not set to ACSCT/M. The test shall be conducted in future feature. Please change the priority when updating this requirement. (ID: 11464626)

#### 5.5.5.6.5 User (Pilot) separation

##### 5.5.5.6.5.0-1 User (Pilot) separation When SRS is used for Precise Positioning, 5G-L1-UL shall perform cyclic prefix removal on the High Precision Time-Offset compensated channel estimate for each UE port. See section 2.7.4 of 5GMax Specification. Notice: According to decision #13, the Priority is not set to ACSCT/M. The test shall be conducted in future feature. Please change the priority when updating this requirement. (ID: 11464637)

#### 5.5.5.6.6 RSRP calculation for positioning SRS

**5.5.5.6.6.0-1**  (ID: `11464655`)

RSRP calculation for positioning SRS
Per each UE, If *measurements LSB+2 bit in* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_15340\_replaced([11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 1, [**PR825728] 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall calculate the srs-rsrp with the following steps:**[End PR825728]**\***\*

1. 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall calculate the [Before **PR825728] srs-rsrp [End**PR825728][**PR825728]raw-srs-rsrp**[End **PR825728] of positioning SRS after user separation (5G\_L1\_15618\_replaced([11464632](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBSF1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) per each co-located antenna(s) (as TRPs,  see 5G\_L1\_17026\_replaced([11464787](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBTT8fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) indicated by *measTrps in \*UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message, as described in section 2.7.5 of 5G New Radio Algorithm Specification.******\****\*\*

[**PR825728]**

2. 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall calculate the sinr of positioning SRS as described in ([11464662](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBSF2_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (regardless the value of *measurement LSB+3).*

1. If the sinr of the TRP is above the threshold (defined in [11464679](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBSs4PvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), srs-rsrp is set to raw-srs-rsrp, otherwise,  srs-rsrp is set to invalid value as defined in UlData\_SrsPosReceiveRespPs message ([11514549](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32gfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

4. 5G-L1-UL (BB) reports srs-rsrp to L2PS

**[End PR825728]**

For details of co-located antenna(s) (TRPs) configuration for the cell, see 5G\_L1\_17026\_replaced([11464787](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBTT8fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

#### 5.5.5.6.7 SINR calculation for positioning SRS

**5.5.5.6.7.0-3**  (ID: `12721460`)

SINR calculation for positioning SRS
Per each UE, if *measurements LSB+3 bit in* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message ([11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is set to 1, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall calculate the sinr of positioning SRS per each co-located antenna(s) (as TRPs, see [11464787](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBTT8fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) indicated by *measTrps in* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message:\*\*\*\*

* **[Before CB013273-A] In case** [CB013273-A] IF **[End CB013273-A] R&D parameter rdToEAlgoSelection ([11465378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBXlYfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) =0 (‘CombinedToE’)**\*\*\*\*

**[CB013273-A] OR (ulsubcellType = C8S ([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))** AND 8 co-located antennas ([12719810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_siyy-WxREfCRGai1q1VTeQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), 1 TRP)):**[End CB013273-A]**\*\*\*\*

* The sinr algorithm is described in section 2.7.6.1 of 5G New Radio Algorithm Specification.
* **[Before CB013273-A] In case** [CB013273-A] ELSE IF **[End CB013273-A] R&D parameter rdToEAlgoSelection ([11465378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBXlYfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) =1 (‘MinimumToE’):**\*\*\*\*
* The sinr algorithm is described in section 2.7.6.2 of 5G New Radio Algorithm Specification.

For details of co-located antenna(s) (TRPs) configuration for the cell, see [11464787](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBTT8fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

#### 5.5.5.6.8 Precise positioning reliability determination

**5.5.5.6.8.0-3**  (ID: `12721485`)

Precise positioning reliability determination
For each UE, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall perform TOE reliability determination per TRP and report the result to L2PS.

reliabilityThreshold = rawReliabilityThreshold+ offsetThreshold

Where:

* reliabilityThreshold: used for TOE reliability determination.
* rawReliabilityThreshold: raw reliability threshold from 5GMax based on assumption of 4 co-located Rx antennas and Combined ToE method and 1m measurement accuracy. 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall retrieve rawReliabilityThreshold by the index Roundup(NPRB/(4 ∗KTC)) from the following table, where NPRB is *numPrb provided in* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message ([11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and KTC is *transmissionComb provided in* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message.\*\*\*\*
* offsetThreshold: the additional offset, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall retrieve offsetThreshold based on co-located antenna configuration (provided by *trpAntStreamMapping in* UlCell\_SetupReq message, [11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and TOE algorithm selection (provided by *rdToEAlgoSelection in [11465378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBXlYfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*\*\*

- **[CB013273-A] IF  8 co-located antennas ([12719810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_siyy-WxREfCRGai1q1VTeQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), 1 TRP):**

offsetThreshold=-0.8 dB

**[End CB013273-A]**

**- ELSE IF (4 co-located antennas)** AND (*rdToEAlgoSelection = ‘CombinedToE’) :*\*\*\*\*

offsetThreshold=0 dB

* **ELSE IF (2 co-located antennas)**AND (*rdToEAlgoSelection = ‘CombinedToE’) :*\*\*\*\*

offsetThreshold=2 dB

* **ELSE IF (1 co-located antenna)**OR (*rdToEAlgoSelection = ‘MinimumToE’) :*\*\*\*\*

offsetThreshold=4 dB

Note: The offsetThreshold is defined in 5G New Radio Algorithm Specification with **tag sec-SrsTOEDet**.\*\*\*\*

For each UE and each TRP (indicated by measTrps in [11514526: UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)):

* When *measurements LSB+0 bit in* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message ([11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) *is set to '1', 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall first calculate the sinr of positioning SRS as described in[11464662](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fBSF2_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) (regardless the value of* measurement LSB+3), if the sinr of positioning SRS for that TRP is higher than reliabilityThreshold, the *result of corresponding TRP in* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveRespPs message ([11514545](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32gPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be set to 1 (reliable). Otherwise, the *result of corresponding TRP shall be set to 0 (unreliable).***\***\*
* When *measurements LSB+0 bit in* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message *is set to '0', the* result of corresponding TRP shall be set to 0 (unreliable).\*\*\*\*

**Note: The algorithm of TOE reliability determination is described in 5G New Radio Algorithm Specification with** tag tab-PosSrsToeReliabilityThr.\*\*\*\*

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Index | SRS PRB Number (*numPrb in* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message)\*\* | SINR Threshold (dB, rawReliabilityThreshold) |

#### 5.5.5.6.9 Interworking with RimRs

##### 5.5.5.6.9.0-1 Interworking with RimRs In case both UlData_SrsPosReceiveReq message (5G_L1_IF_15341_replaced( 11514530 )) and UlData_RimReceiveReq message (with rimRsDetectionRequest = True, 5G_L1_IF_14748_replaced( 11514602 )) are received in the same slot and same subcell, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall discard UlData_SrsPosReceiveReq message, send UlData_SrsPosReceiveRespPs message (5G_L1_IF_15345_replaced( 11514549 )) to L2PS with the invalid values as defined in 5G_L1_IF_15344_replaced( 11514545 ). * * Set IE status to "DiscardByRimRs". (ID: 11464710)

#### 5.5.5.6.10 Multiple sequenceId(s) on the same symbol

**5.5.5.6.10.0-1**  (ID: `12874668`)

Multiple sequenceId(s) on the same symbol
5G-L1-UL (BB) supports only one sequenceId ([11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) per symbol/slot/subcell for SRS positioning.

If more than one sequenceId(s) on the same symbol/slot/subcell are received in UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message ([11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report invalid timeOffsetPos/rsrp/sinr with result = "unreliable (as defined in [11514545: UlData\_SrsPosReceiveRespPs](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32gPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) to L2PS for all TRP(s) on that symbol.

Reason: SRS(s) with different sequenceId(s) on the same symbol may interfere with each other.

#### 5.5.5.6.11 Measurements

##### 5.5.5.6.11.1 High Precision Time-Offset

###### 5.5.5.6.11.1.1 Normal cell

###### 5.5.5.6.11.1.1.0-2 Normal cell When LSB of measurements in srsPosReportRequest is set to '1' for a specific UE, 5G-L1-UL shall report the High Precision Time-Offset (5G_L1_15616_replaced( 11464379 )) in corresponding srsPosReport parameter of UlData_SrsPosReceiveRespPs message. (5G_L1_IF_15344_replaced( 11514545 )) UE is specified with the pair of [Before CB007880-A] { RNTI, sequenceId}[CB007880-A]{ measId, sequenceId} [End CB007880-A] . * * Note: L2PS may use any identifier instead of [Before CB007880-A] RNTI [CB007880-A] measId [End CB007880-A] in UlData_SrsPosReceiveReq. 5G-L1-UL shall set the same indentifier as [Before CB007880-A] RNTI [CB007880-A] measId [End CB007880-A] while creating the report for the corresponding UE in UlData_SrsPosReceiveRespPs. * * (ID: 13331339)

###### 5.5.5.6.11.1.2 Suppercell

###### 5.5.5.6.11.1.2.0-1 Suppercell When Supercell is deployed, that is, for subcells with identical physCellId  (5G_L1_IF_152_replaced( 11513449 ), in UlCell_SetupReq), L1 shall report the High Precision Time-Offset in all the subcells of the Supercell for which Precise Positioning is requested via UlData_SrsPosReceiveReq. (ID: 11464743)

##### 5.5.5.6.11.2 rsrp for Positioning SRS

###### 5.5.5.6.11.2.0-1 rsrp for Positioning SRS When measurements LSB+2 bit in UlData_SrsPosReceiveReq message (5G_L1_IF_15340_replaced( 11514526 )) is set to '1' for a specific UE, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the srs-rsrp as described in 5G_L1_17143_replaced( 11464650 ) for this UE per each co-located antenna(s) (as TRPs,  see 5G_L1_17026_replaced( 11464787 ), indicated by measTrps in UlData_SrsPosReceiveReq message) to L2PS via rsrp in UlData_SrsPosReceiveRespPs (5G_L1_IF_15344_replaced( 11514545 )) message. * * (ID: 11464755)

##### 5.5.5.6.11.3 sinr for Positioning SRS

###### 5.5.5.6.11.3.0-1 sinr for Positioning SRS When measurements LSB+3 bit in UlData_SrsPosReceiveReq message (5G_L1_IF_15340_replaced( 11514526 )) is set to '1' for a specific UE, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the sinr as described in 5G_L1_17144_replaced( 11464662 ) for this UE per each co-located antenna(s) (as TRPs,  see 5G_L1_17026_replaced( 11464787 ), indicated by measTrps in UlData_SrsPosReceiveReq message) to L2PS via sinr in UlData_SrsPosReceiveRespPs (5G_L1_IF_15344_replaced( 11514545 )) message. * * (ID: 11464768)

##### 5.5.5.6.11.4 Result of Reliability determination for Positioning SRS

###### 5.5.5.6.11.4.0-1 Result of Reliability determination for Positioning SRS 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall report the result of TOE reliability determination as described in 5G_L1_18628_replaced( 11464679 ) for each UE and each co-located antenna(s) (as TRPs, see 5G_L1_17026_replaced( 11464787 ), indicated by measTrps in UlData_SrsPosReceiveReq message) to L2PS via result in UlData_SrsPosReceiveRespPs (5G_L1_IF_15344_replaced( 11514545 )) message.**** (ID: 11464782)

##### 5.5.5.6.11.5 TRP based High Precision Time-Offset measurement

**5.5.5.6.11.5.0-2**  (ID: `12721900`)

TRP based High Precision Time-Offset measurement
In C4S [CB013273-A] and C8S [End CB013273-A] subcell case, SRS receiver shall read this parameter:

UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq.srsPosReportRequests.measTrps ([11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

which is a bitmap and it tells from which TRP(s) Time-Offset measurement is done for UE.

measTrps bits are mapped to TRP indexes starting counting from LSB:

LSB+0 maps to TRP index 0

LSB+1 maps to TRP index 1

LSB+2 maps to TRP index 2

[CB013273-A]

...

LSB+7 maps to TRP index 7

For C4S, TRP index is in range of [0..3]

For C8S, TRP index is in range of [0..7]

[End CB013273-A]

When measTrps bit ([11514526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32fPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) is set to true, High Precision Time-Offset measurement is done from corresponding TRP.

After measurement(/s) are done, they are reported in:

UlData\_SrsPosReceiveResp.SrsPosReport.timeOffsetPos[ ] parameter ([11514545](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32gPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

Array values are mapped based on TRP index like this: timeOffsetPos[TRP index].

timeOffsetPos[TRP index] contains valid measurement value when TRP index was used to Time-Offset measurement.

timeOffsetPos[TRP index] contains invalid measurement value when TRP index was not used to Time-Offset measurement.

All timeOffsetPos[ ] values contain invalid value if measurement is requested at least from one TRP, which was not configured in Cell Setup with UlCell\_SetupReq.TrpAntStreamMapping[].

Example:

[Before CB013273-A]

UlCell\_SetupReq:

> TrpAntStreamMapping[4] = [0, 0, 1, 1],

2x2 distributed case, eAxc[0+1] belong to TRP0 and eAxc[2+3] to TRP1

UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq:

> measTrps = 0010,

Lsb maps to TRP0, Lsb+1 maps to TRP1 -> only TRP1 is used for measurement, thus eAxcs[2+3]

UlData\_SrsPosReceiveResp

> timeOffsetPos[4] = [invalid, valid, invalid, invalid] ' timeOffsetPos[1] contains value for TRP1

Note that array above contains indexes in this order:

timeOffsetPos[4] = [TRP0, TRP1, TRP2, TRP3].

[CB013273-A]

UlCell\_SetupReq:

->ulSubcelltype= C4S

> TrpAntStreamMapping[0..7] = [0, 0, 1, 1, 255, 255, 255, 255],

2x2 distributed case, eAxc[0+1] belong to TRP0 and eAxc[2+3] to TRP1

UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq:

> measTrps = 0000 0010,

Lsb maps to TRP0, Lsb+1 maps to TRP1 -> only TRP1 is used for measurement, thus eAxcs[2+3]

UlData\_SrsPosReceiveResp

> timeOffsetPos[] = [invalid, valid, invalid, invalid, invalid, invalid, invalid, invalid] ' timeOffsetPos[1] contains value for TRP1

Note that array above contains indexes in this order:

timeOffsetPos[] = [TRP0, TRP1, TRP2, TRP3, TRP4, TRP5, TRP6, TRP7].

[End CB013273-A]

In C4 [CB013273-C] or C2 [End CB013273-C] subcell case, all antennas are co-located and belong to TRP index 0.

[Before CB013273-A]

* *TrpAntStreamMapping[4] in* UlCell\_SetupReq message is set to = [0, 0, 0, 0].\*\*
* *measTrps in* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message is set to 0001.\*\*

[CB013273-A]

* *TrpAntStreamMapping[] in* UlCell\_SetupReq message is set to = [0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0].\*\*
* *measTrps in* UlData\_SrsPosReceiveReq message is set to value 0000 0001.\*\*

[End CB013273-A]

## 5.5.6 Measurements

### 5.5.6.1 Common measurements

#### 5.5.6.1.1 Timing advance

##### 5.5.6.1.1.1 TO estimation on SRS for Loner L1 HW

**5.5.6.1.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11464963`)

TO estimation on SRS for Loner L1 HW
[CNI-59405]: CP2 part moved

5GNB 5G-L1-UL estimates a short term (ST) timing offset (TO) on SRS and reports it to 5G-L2-PS, within the UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message. This report, could be used by 5G-L2-PS to update the TA measurement, but is currently used for debug purposes only. A single correlation peak shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS in TO parameters shortTermTaMetric and shortTermTaPeakAmp sent in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message. The reported shortTermTaMetric value shall be in unit of Tsμ = (1/2μ) \* Ts, as described in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_251.

The search window length for time offset estimation is changed for SRS and the shortTermTaMetric shall be adjusted with the new search window range (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1201).

The timing offset estimation algorithm on SRS is described in section 2.6.4 of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916).

[5GC002244-A] Loner-L1-Only. additionally, 5GNB 5G-L1-UL estimates and reports per rx antenna stream shortTermTaMetricOfAnt and shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt, and sends them in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message.

Note: although antenna-wise SRS TO is introduced for FR1 TDD Rx beamforming cells with eCPRI RU, L1's behavior is the same among:

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX beamforming

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 TDD 4Rx non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 4Rx non beamforming

- FR2 TDD 2Rx

For eCPRI case, the order eAxC spatial stream values of the antennas-wise SRS TO (shortTermTaMetricOfAnt) in the array and their mapping to beam patternId shall follow the same mapping order of EcpriConfig struct in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_263. The same rational applies for all antenna-wise values in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6333.

For CPRI case, table below is used for the order of AxC spatial stream values. The same rationale applies for all antenna-wise values in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_254.

Mapping between antenna-wise TO and spatial stream for CPRI

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Subcell Type (IE ulSubcellType, see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151) | TO for antenna i (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_254) | CPRI spatial stream |
| A2 or C2 | shortTermTaMetricOfAnt [0] | AxC0 |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt [1] | AxC1 |  |
| A4 or C4 | shortTermTaMetricOfAnt [0] | AxC0 |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt [1] | AxC1 |  |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt [2] | AxC2 |  |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt [3] | AxC3 |  |

[End 5GC002244-A]

[End CNI-59405]

---

##### 5.5.6.1.1.2 TO estimation on SRS for Loki, Thor and Odin L1 HW

###### 5.5.6.1.1.2.1 General

**5.5.6.1.1.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11464983`)

General
Content of this requirement is frozen and valid until 23R4 release, For later releases please refer to the objects below.

5GNB 5G-L1-UL estimates a short term (ST) timing offset (TO) on SRS and reports it to 5G-L2-PS, within the UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message. This report, could be used by 5G-L2-PS to update the TA measurement, but is currently used for debug purposes only. A single correlation peak shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS in TO parameters shortTermTaMetric and shortTermTaPeakAmp sent in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message. The reported shortTermTaMetric value shall be in unit of Tsμ = (1/2μ) \* Ts, as described in 5G\_L1\_IF\_253\_replaced([11514446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PcfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The timing offset estimation algorithm on SRS is described in section 2.6.4 of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_3957\_replaced([11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For Loki [RP003187-M, RP003187-F] and Thor [End RP003187-M, RP003187-F]: additionally, 5GNB 5G-L1-UL estimates and reports per rx antenna stream shortTermTaMetricOfAnt and shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt, and sends them in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message.

Note: although antenna-wise SRS TO is introduced for FR1 TDD Rx beamforming cells with eCPRI RU, L1's behavior is the same among:

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX beamforming

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 TDD 4Rx non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 4Rx non beamforming

-     [CB008205-B] For Loki L1 HW, eCPRI FR1 FDD 4Rx non beamforming [End CB008205-B]

-     [CB008205-C] For Loki L1 HW, eCPRI FR1 FDD 2Rx non beamforming [End CB008205-C]

- FR2 TDD 2Rx

For eCPRI case, the order eAxC spatial stream values of the antennas-wise SRS TO (shortTermTaMetricOfAnt) in the array and their mapping to beam patternId shall follow the same mapping order of EcpriConfig struct in 5G\_L1\_IF\_266\_replaced([11514653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR4dkfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (see also 5G\_L1\_ALG\_1739).

For CPRI case, table below is used for the order of AxC spatial stream values.

Mapping between antenna-wise TO on SRS and spatial stream for CPRI

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Subcell Type (IE ulSubcellType, see 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | TO for antenna i (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) |  | CPRI spatial stream |
| A2 or C2 | shortTermTaMetricOfAnt [0] | shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt [0] | AxC0 |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt [1] | shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt [1] | AxC1 |  |
| A4 or C4 | shortTermTaMetricOfAnt [0] | shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt [0] | AxC0 |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt [1] | shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt [1] | AxC1 |  |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt [2] | shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt [2] | AxC2 |  |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt [3] | shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt [3] | AxC3 |  |

Note:In case of 2Rx, the last two elements of array shall be filled with invalid values (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[RP003187-M] The requirement is also applicable for Thor for FR1-FDD-CPRI [End RP003187-M]

[RP003187-F] The requirement is also applicable for Thor for FR1-TDD-eCPRI [End RP003187-F]

[CB009443-C] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI. [End CB009443-C]

###### 5.5.6.1.1.2.1.1 Loki

**5.5.6.1.1.2.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11464996`)

Loki
For Loki:

5GNB 5G-L1-UL estimates a short term (ST) timing offset (TO) on SRS and reports it to 5G-L2-PS, within the UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message. This report, could be used by 5G-L2-PS to update the TA measurement, but is currently used for debug purposes only. A single correlation peak shall be provided to 5G-L2-PS in TO parameters shortTermTaMetric and shortTermTaPeakAmp sent in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message. The reported shortTermTaMetric value shall be in unit of Tsμ = (1/2μ) \* Ts, as described in 5G\_L1\_IF\_253\_replaced([11514446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PcfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The timing offset estimation algorithm on SRS is described in section 2.6.4 of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_3957\_replaced([11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Additionally, 5GNB 5G-L1-UL estimates and reports per rx antenna stream shortTermTaMetricOfAnt and shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt, and sends them in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message.

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX beamforming

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 TDD 4Rx non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 4Rx non beamforming

-     For Loki L1 HW, eCPRI FR1 FDD 4Rx non beamforming

-     For Loki L1 HW, eCPRI FR1 FDD 2Rx non beamforming

- FR2 TDD 2Rx

For eCPRI case, the order eAxC spatial stream values of the antennas-wise SRS TO (shortTermTaMetricOfAnt) in the array and their mapping to beam patternId shall follow the same mapping order of EcpriConfig struct in 5G\_L1\_IF\_266\_replaced([11514653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR4dkfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (see also 5G\_L1\_ALG\_1739).

###### 5.5.6.1.1.2.1.2 Thor

**5.5.6.1.1.2.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `12590682`)

Thor
5G-L1-UL estimates a short-term (ST) timing offset (TO) on SRS and reports it to 5G-L2-PS, within the *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message. A single correlation peak shall be reported to 5G-L2-PS in TO parameters* shortTermTaMetric and *shortTermTaPeakAmp sent in* UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message. The reported shortTermTaMetric value shall be in unit of Tsμ = (1/2μ) \* Ts, as described in [11514446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PcfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).\*\*\*\*

The timing offset estimation algorithm on SRS is described in section 2.6.4 of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see [11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L1-UL estimates and reports per RX antenna stream *shortTermTaMetricOfAnt and* shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt, and reports them in *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message.*\*\*

Note: Antenna-wise SRS TO is the same among the different deployments.

For eCPRI case: the order eAxC spatial stream values of the antennas-wise SRS TO (shortTermTaMetricOfAnt) in the dynamic array structure **SrsAntMeas and their mapping to beam *patternId shall follow the same mapping order of \*EcpriConfig struct in [11514653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR4dkfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).***\*

###### 5.5.6.1.1.2.2 Antenna-wise” TO estimation on periodic SRS

**5.5.6.1.1.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11465022`)

Antenna-wise” TO estimation on periodic SRS
Content of this requirement is frozen and valid until 23R4 release, For later releases please refer to the objects below.

[PR635445]

5G-L1-UL shall compute per RX-antenna stream short-term (ST) time offset (TO) based on periodic SRS and report it to 5G-L2-PS with parameters shortTermTaMetricOfAnt and shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message. SRS RX time offset for each UL received antenna stream is estimated as described in section 2.6.4 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_3957\_replaced([11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For the periodic SRS case, the “antenna-wise” (spatial stream) time offset value, shortTermTaMetricOfAnt, and time offset amplitude, shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt, in SrsAntMeas structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) follows the mapping in the Table below:

Mapping between antenna-wise SINR for periodic SRS and patternID/polarization

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| TO metric of antenna i (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | TO peak amplitude of antenna i (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | Beam (patternId) and polarization bit (pol\_ID) measurement association |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt[0] | shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt[0] | patternId[0] and pol\_ID=1 |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt[1] | shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt[1] | patternId[0] and pol\_ID=0 |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt[2] | shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt[2] | patternId[1] and pol\_ID=1 |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt[3] | shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt[3] | patternId[1] and pol\_ID=0 |

where patternId is in the SrsSuMimo structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14078\_replaced([11514394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the polarization bit pol\_ID is in the eAxC definition.

[End PR635445]

---

###### 5.5.6.1.1.2.2.1 Loki

**5.5.6.1.1.2.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11465036`)

Loki
For Loki:

5G-L1-UL shall compute per RX-antenna stream short-term (ST) time offset (TO) based on periodic SRS and report it to 5G-L2-PS with parameters shortTermTaMetricOfAnt and shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message. SRS RX time offset for each UL received antenna stream is estimated as described in section 2.6.4 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_3957\_replaced([11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For the periodic SRS case, the “antenna-wise” (spatial stream) time offset value, shortTermTaMetricOfAnt, and time offset amplitude, shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt, in SrsAntMeas structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) follows the mapping in the Table below:

Mapping between antenna-wise SINR for periodic SRS and patternID/polarization

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| TO metric of antenna i (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | TO peak amplitude of antenna i (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | Beam (patternId) and polarization bit (pol\_ID) measurement association |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt[0] | shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt[0] | patternId[0] and pol\_ID=1 |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt[1] | shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt[1] | patternId[0] and pol\_ID=0 |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt[2] | shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt[2] | patternId[1] and pol\_ID=1 |
| shortTermTaMetricOfAnt[3] | shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt[3] | patternId[1] and pol\_ID=0 |

where patternId is in the SrsSuMimo structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14078\_replaced([11514394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the polarization bit pol\_ID is in the eAxC definition.

---

###### 5.5.6.1.1.2.2.2 Thor

**5.5.6.1.1.2.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11465049`)

Thor
For Thor:

5G-L1-UL shall compute per RX-antenna stream short-term (ST) time offset (TO) based on periodic SRS and report it to 5G-L2-PS with parameters shortTermTaMetricOfAnt and shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message.

SRS RX time offset for each UL received antenna stream is estimated as described in section 2.6.4 2.6.3 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_3957\_replaced([11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For the periodic SRS case, the “antenna-wise” (spatial stream) time offset value, shortTermTaMetricOfAnt, and time offset amplitude, shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt, in SrsAntMeas structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) follows the mapping in the Table below:

Mapping between antenna-wise SINR for periodic SRS and patternID/polarization

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| TO metric of antenna i (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | TO peak amplitude of antenna i (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | Beam (patternId) and polarization bit (pol\_ID) measurement association | The First Feature |
| SrsAntMeas[0].shortTermTaMetricOfAnt | SrsAntMeas[0].shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt | patternId[0] and pol\_ID=1 | CB009363-D |
| SrsAntMeas[1].shortTermTaMetricOfAnt | SrsAntMeas[1].shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt | patternId[0] and pol\_ID=0 |  |
| SrsAntMeas[2].shortTermTaMetricOfAnt | SrsAntMeas[2].shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt | patternId[1] and pol\_ID=1 |  |
| SrsAntMeas[3].shortTermTaMetricOfAnt | SrsAntMeas[3].shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt | patternId[1] and pol\_ID=0 |  |
| SrsAntMeas[4].shortTermTaMetricOfAnt | SrsAntMeas[4].shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt | patternId[2] and pol\_ID=1 | CB009363-D |
| SrsAntMeas[5].shortTermTaMetricOfAnt | SrsAntMeas[5].shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt | patternId[2] and pol\_ID=0 |  |
| SrsAntMeas[6].shortTermTaMetricOfAnt | SrsAntMeas[6].shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt | patternId[3] and pol\_ID=1 |  |
| SrsAntMeas[7].shortTermTaMetricOfAnt | SrsAntMeas[7].shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt | patternId[3] and pol\_ID=0 |  |

where patternId is in the SrsSuMimo structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14078\_replaced([11514394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the polarization bit pol\_ID is in the eAxC definition.

[CB009363-D]

Note: The structure SrsAntMeas in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message is changed to dynamic array based on subcell type. Refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_255\_replaced([11514457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The parametershortTermTaMetricOfAnt  and shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt in the structure SrsAntMeas are no longer arrays. Refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB009363-D]

##### 5.5.6.1.1.3 Invalid timing advance

###### 5.5.6.1.1.3.1 Loner

**5.5.6.1.1.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `11465068`)

Loner
For SRS, 5G-L1-UL shall report invalid measurement for antenna-wise TOE(shortTermTaMetricOfAnt) and its associated peak amplitude(shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt) with message UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs when the Rx is failed (typically the case of RU lost or fiber broken or Rx failure).

Message detail is defined in 5G\_L1\_IF\_255\_replaced([11514457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Invalid value of shortTermTaMetricOfAnt shall be set to −32768. Invalid value of shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt shall be set to −1.

---

###### 5.5.6.1.1.3.2 Loki

**5.5.6.1.1.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `11465080`)

Loki
For SRS, 5G-L1-UL shall report invalid measurement for antenna-wise TOE(shortTermTaMetricOfAnt) and its associated peak amplitude(shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt) with message UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs when the Rx is failed (typically the case of RU lost or fiber broken or Rx failure).

Message detail is defined in 5G\_L1\_IF\_255\_replaced([11514457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Invalid value of shortTermTaMetricOfAnt shall be set to −32768. Invalid value of shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt shall be set to −1.

---

###### 5.5.6.1.1.3.3 Thor

**5.5.6.1.1.3.3.0-2**  (ID: `12591423`)

Thor
5G-L1-UL shall report invalid measurement for antenna-wise TOE(shortTermTaMetricOfAnt) and its associated peak amplitude(shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt) with message UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs **when the Rx is failed (typically the case of RU lost or fiber broken or Rx failure).**

Message detail is defined in [11514457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and [11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

Invalid value of shortTermTaMetricOfAnt shall be set to −32768. Invalid value of shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt shall be set to −1.

[CB013442-SR-D] Note: This requirement is common for all FR1 technologies. [EndCB013442-SR-D]

---

###### 5.5.6.1.1.3.4 Odin

**5.5.6.1.1.3.4.0-1**  (ID: `12715844`)

Odin
5G-L1-UL shall report invalid measurement for antenna-wise TOE(shortTermTaMetricOfAnt) and its associated peak amplitude (shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt) with message UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs **when the RX is failed (typically the case of RU lost or fiber broken or Rx failure).**

Message detail is defined in [11514457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and [11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

Invalid value of shortTermTaMetricOfAnt shall be set to −32768. Invalid value of shortTermTaPeakAmpOfAnt shall be set to −1.

---

#### 5.5.6.1.2 Received power

**5.5.6.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11465105`)

Received power
Content of this requirement is frozen and valid until 23R4 release, For later releases please refer to the objects below.

For Loki [RP003187-M, RP003187-F] and Thor [End RP003187-M, RP003187-F]:

5GNB 5G-L1-UL shall estimate per rx antenna UL received power on SRS and report it to 5G-L2-PS within the parameter rxPowerOfAnt sent in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message. The rxPowerOfAnt parameter is defined in dBm unit.

When only zero-valued samples are received from the radio module or eCPRI interface for each the receiving antenna stream, 5G-L1-UL shall set the rxPowerOfAnt parameter to -140dBm.

SRS rx antenna power for each UL received antenna stream is estimated per PRBs as described in section 2.7.3.3 of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_3957\_replaced([11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: although antenna-wise UL value is introduced for FR1 TDD Rx beamforming cells with eCPRI RU, L1's behavior is the same among:

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX beamforming

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 TDD 4Rx non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 4Rx non beamforming

-     FR2 TDD 2Rx

For eCPRI case, the order eAxC spatial stream values of the antennas-wise UL received power on SRS (rxPowerOfAnt ) in the array and their mapping to beam patternId shall follow the same mapping order of EcpriConfig struct in 5G\_L1\_IF\_266\_replaced([11514653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR4dkfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (see also 5G\_L1\_ALG\_1739).

For CPRI case, table below is used for the order of AxC spatial stream values.

Mapping between antenna-wise UL received power on SRS and spatial stream for CPRI

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Subcell Type (IE ulSubcellType, see 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | Received power of antenna i (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | CPRI spatial stream |
| A2 or C2 | rxPowerOfAnt [0] | AxC0 |
| rxPowerOfAnt [1] | AxC1 |  |
| A4 or C4 | rxPowerOfAnt [0] | AxC0 |
| rxPowerOfAnt [1] | AxC1 |  |
| rxPowerOfAnt [2] | AxC2 |  |
| rxPowerOfAnt [3] | AxC3 |  |

Note:In case of 2Rx, the last two elements of array shall be filled with invalid values (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[RP003187-M] The requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-FDD-CPRI [End RP003187-M]

[RP003187-F] The requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-eCPRI [End RP003187-F]

[CB009443-C] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI. [End CB009443-C]

---

**5.5.6.1.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11465118`)

Loner
[CNI-59405]: CP2 part moved

Loner-L1-Only. FR1 TDD eCPRI beamforming only.

5GNB 5G-L1-UL shall estimate per rx antenna UL received power on SRS and report it to 5G-L2-PS within the parameter rxPowerOfAnt sent in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message. The rxPowerOfAnt parameter is defined in dBm unit.

When only zero-valued samples are received from the radio module or eCPRI interface for each the receiving antenna stream, 5G-L1-UL shall set the rxPowerOfAnt parameter to -140dBm.

SRS rx antenna power for each UL received antenna stream is estimated as described in section 2.7.3.3 of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916).

Note: although antenna-wise UL value is introduced for FR1 TDD Rx beamforming cells with eCPRI RU, L1's behavior is the same among:

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX beamforming

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 TDD 4Rx non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 4Rx non beamforming

-     FR2 TDD 2Rx

[End CNI-59405]

**5.5.6.1.2.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `11465135`)

Loki

[PR635445]

5G-L1-UL shall compute per RX-antenna stream UL received power based on periodic SRS and report it to 5G-L2-PS within the parameter rxPowerOfAnt in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message. SRS RX antenna power for each UL received antenna stream is estimated per PRB as described in section 2.7.4.3 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_3957\_replaced([11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For the periodic SRS case, the “antenna-wise” (spatial stream) received power, rxPowerOfAnt, in SrsAntMeas structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) follows the mapping in the Table below:

Mapping between antenna-wise SINR for periodic SRS and patternID/polarization

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Rx Power of antenna i (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | Beam (patternId) and polarization bit (pol\_ID) measurement association |
| rxPowerOfAnt[0] | patternId[0] and pol\_ID=1 |
| rxPowerOfAnt[1] | patternId[0] and pol\_ID=0 |
| rxPowerOfAnt[2] | patternId[1] and pol\_ID=1 |
| rxPowerOfAnt[3] | patternId[1] and pol\_ID=0 |

where patternId is in the SrsSuMimo structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14078\_replaced([11514394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the polarization bit pol\_ID is in the eAxC definition.

[End PR635445]

---

###### 5.5.6.1.2.3.2 Thor

**5.5.6.1.2.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `11465154`)

Thor
For Thor:

5G-L1-UL shall compute per RX-antenna stream UL received power based on periodic SRS and report it to 5G-L2-PS within the parameter rxPowerOfAnt in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message. SRS RX antenna power for each UL received antenna stream is estimated per PRB as described in section 2.7.4.3 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_3957\_replaced([11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For the periodic SRS case, the “antenna-wise” (spatial stream) received power, rxPowerOfAnt, in SrsAntMeas structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) follows the mapping in the Table below:

Mapping between antenna-wise SINR for periodic SRS and patternID/polarization

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Rx Power of antenna j (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | Beam (patternId) and polarization bit (pol\_ID) measurement association |
| SrsAntMeas[0].rxPowerOfAnt | patternId[0] and pol\_ID=1 |
| SrsAntMeas[1].rxPowerOfAnt | patternId[0] and pol\_ID=0 |
| SrsAntMeas[2].rxPowerOfAnt | patternId[1] and pol\_ID=1 |
| SrsAntMeas[3].rxPowerOfAnt | patternId[1] and pol\_ID=0 |
| SrsAntMeas[4].rxPowerOfAnt | patternId[2] and pol\_ID=1 |
| SrsAntMeas[5].rxPowerOfAnt | patternId[2] and pol\_ID=0 |
| SrsAntMeas[6].rxPowerOfAnt | patternId[3] and pol\_ID=1 |
| SrsAntMeas[7].rxPowerOfAnt | patternId[3] and pol\_ID=0 |

where patternId is in the SrsSuMimo structure of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14078\_replaced([11514394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZ_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the polarization bit pol\_ID is in the eAxC definition.

[CB009363-D]

Note: The structure SrsAntMeas in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message is changed to dynamic array based on subcell type. Refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_255\_replaced([11514457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The parameter rxPowerOfAnt in the structure SrsAntMeas is no longer arrays. Refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB009363-D]

#### 5.5.6.1.3 DTX (Discontinous transmission)

#### 5.5.6.1.4 SINR (Signal-to-Interference-plus-Noise Ratio)

##### 5.5.6.1.4.1 General

**5.5.6.1.4.1.0-1**  (ID: `11465180`)

General
5G-L1-UL shall compute the UL SINR based on SRS and report it to 5G-L2-PS within the parameter snr sent in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message, for FSS (Frequency Selection Scheduling) purpose.

The SINR measurement report for SRS is calculated as described in section “2.7.4.3 SRS” in 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_3957\_replaced([11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB007166-C] For invalid measurement values, reported snr is set to invalid defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8414. [End CB007166-C]

[5GC001868-D] 5G-L1-UL shall also estimate the SINR on SRS as explained above in Loki L1 HW. [5GC001868-D]

[CB007814-G] This requirement also applies to ABIO FR1-FDD-eCPRI. [End CB007814-G]

[RP003187-M, RP003187-F] 5G-L1-UL shall also estimate the SINR on SRS as explained above in L1 Thor [End RP003187-M, RP003187-F]

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009443-C] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI. [End CB009443-C]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

[CB010969-SR-CB] This requirement shall be supported by Thor in FR1-FDD-OBSAI [End CB010969-SR-CB]

---

##### 5.5.6.1.4.2 UL antenna-wise SINR computation for aperiodical SRS

**5.5.6.1.4.2.0-1**  (ID: `11465193`)

UL antenna-wise SINR computation for aperiodical SRS
Content of this requirement is frozen and valid until 23R4 release, For later releases please refer to the objects below.

Loki [RP003187-M, RP003187-F] and Thor [End RP003187-M, RP003187-F]. 5GNB 5G-L1-UL shall compute per rx antenna stream UL SINR based on aperiodical SRS and report it to 5G-L2-PS within the parameter sinrOfAnt sent in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message.

The SINR estimation algorithm on SRS is described in section 2.7.5.3 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_3957\_replaced([11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: although antenna-wise value is introduced for FR1 TDD Rx beamforming cells with eCPRI RU, L1's behavior is the same among:

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX beamforming

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 TDD 4Rx non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 4Rx non beamforming

- FR2 TDD 2Rx

For eCPRI case, the order eAxC spatial stream values of the antennas-wise SINR on SRS (sinrOfAnt) in the array and their mapping to beam patternId shall follow the same mapping order of EcpriConfig struct in 5G\_L1\_IF\_266\_replaced([11514653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR4dkfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (see also 5G\_L1\_ALG\_1739).

For CPRI case, table below is used for the order of AxC spatial stream values.

Mapping between antenna-wise SINR on SRS and spatial stream for (e)CPRI

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Subcell Type (IE ulSubcellType, see 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | SINR of antenna i (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | CPRI spatial stream |
| A2 or C2 | sinrOfAnt [0] | AxC0 |
| sinrOfAnt [1] | AxC1 |  |
| A4 or C4 | sinrOfAnt [0] | AxC0 |
| sinrOfAnt [1] | AxC1 |  |
| sinrOfAnt [2] | AxC2 |  |
| sinrOfAnt [3] | AxC3 |  |

Note:In case of 2Rx, the last two elements of array shall be filled with invalid values (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-FDD-CPRI

The requirement is also applicable for L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-eCPRI

---

**5.5.6.1.4.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11465205`)

Loner
[CNI-59405]: CP2 part moved

Loner-L1-Only. FR1 TDD eCPRI beamforming only. 5GNB 5G-L1-UL shall compute per rx antenna stream UL SINR based on aperiodical SRS and report it to 5G-L2-PS within the parameter sinrOfAntStream sent in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message.

The SINR estimation algorithm on SRS is described in section 2.6.10 of the 5Gmax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916).

Note: although antenna-wise value is introduced for FR1 TDD Rx beamforming cells with eCPRI RU, L1's behavior is the same among:

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX beamforming

- CPRI or eCPRI FR1 TDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 TDD 4Rx non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 2RX non beamforming

- CPRI FR1 FDD 4Rx non beamforming

- FR2 TDD 2Rx

[End CNI-59405]

##### 5.5.6.1.4.4 Invalid measurement for antenna-wise SINR

###### 5.5.6.1.4.4.1 Loner

**5.5.6.1.4.4.1.0-1**  (ID: `11465267`)

Loner
For SRS, 5G-L1-UL shall report invalid measurement for antenna-wise SINR (sinrOfAnt) with message UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs when the Rx is failed (typically the case of RU lost or fiber broken or Rx failure).

Message detail is defined in 5G\_L1\_IF\_255\_replaced([11514457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Invalid value of sinrOfAnt shall be set to -255(dB).

---

###### 5.5.6.1.4.4.2 Loki

**5.5.6.1.4.4.2.0-1**  (ID: `11465275`)

Loki
For SRS, 5G-L1-UL shall report invalid measurement for antenna-wise SINR (sinrOfAnt) with message UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs when the Rx is failed (typically the case of RU lost or fiber broken or Rx failure).

Message detail is defined in 5G\_L1\_IF\_255\_replaced([11514457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_IF\_256\_replaced([11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Invalid value of sinrOfAnt shall be set to -255(dB).

---

###### 5.5.6.1.4.4.3 Thor

**5.5.6.1.4.4.3.0-2**  (ID: `12591445`)

Thor
5G-L1-UL(BB) shall report invalid measurement for antenna-wise SINR (sinrOfAnt) with message UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs **when the Rx is failed (typically the case of RU lost or fiber broken or Rx failure). Message detail is defined in [11514457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and [11514463](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).**

Invalid value of sinrOfAnt shall be set to -255(dB).

[CB013442-SR-D] Note: requirement refactored and made common for FR1. [End CB013442-SR-D]

---

###### 5.5.6.1.4.4.4 Odin

###### 5.5.6.1.4.4.4.0-1 Odin 5G-L1-UL(BB) shall report invalid measurement for antenna-wise SINR (sinrOfAnt) with message UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs when reception has failed (typically the case of RU lost or fiber broken or Rx failure). Message detail is defined in 11514457 and 11514463 . Invalid value of sinrOfAnt shall be set to -255(dB). (ID: 12715970)

### 5.5.6.2 SU-MIMO related measurements

#### 5.5.6.2.1 Rank calculation

**5.5.6.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `12716322`)

Rank calculation
Based on SRS smoothed channel estimates, 5G-L1-UL shall compute the preferred UL rank. The rank metric computation is described in section 2.10 of the 5Gmax Algorithm Specification [11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

The number of equidistant subcarriers considered for rank computation on SRS is 6 over the entire allocated SRS PRBs.

The computed UL rank shall be sent as *ulRank to 5G-L2-PS in the* UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message.\*\*

Note: The link level simulations motivating Rank calculation algorithm  are available under

<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Forms/Tree_View.aspx?RootFolder=%2Fsites%2F5Gdoc%2FAS%5FTech%5FSpec%2FCFAMs%2F5GC0400%2D5GC0599%2F5GC000532%20%2D%20UL%202x2%20SU%20MIMO%2FSimulations%5Freports&FolderCTID=0x012000F0A0A3BA325F7648AD307E6959BA7376>

[CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA]

---

#### 5.5.6.2.2 TPMI calculation

**5.5.6.2.2.0-2**  (ID: `12716335`)

TPMI calculation
Based on SRS smoothed channel estimates, TPMI selection is performed. TPMI selection metrics are described in section 2.9 of the 5Gmax Algorithm Specification [11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

TPMI prefered index is calculated for the possible rank options (rank1 and rank2).

Based on the different rank options, 5G-L1-UL shall use the following methods:

-For rank1 TPMI selection, maximization of MECG metric (Maximal Effective Channel Gain) is used.

-For rank 2 TPMI selection, maximization of SLP metric (Sum Layer Power) is used.

The codebook for rank1 and rank2 are listed in [11398799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e84G9_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). A restricted codebook set depends on the value of *puschTransCoherence in*UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message ([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):\*\*

-When *puschTransCoherence == nonCoherent, the codebook is given by [11398799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e84G9_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).*

-When *puschTransCoherence == fullCoherent, the codebook is given by [11398799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e84G9_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).*

The number of equidistant subcarriers considered for PMI evaluation on SRS is 12.

The selected TPMIs shall be sent to 5G-L2-PS in the *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message ([11514446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PcfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):*

- Preferred index for rank1 is included in *ulPmiRank1*

- Preferred index for rank2 is included in *ulPmiRank2*

Note: The link level simulations motivating TPMI selection algorithm are under:

<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Forms/Tree_View.aspx?RootFolder=%2Fsites%2F5Gdoc%2FAS%5FTech%5FSpec%2FCFAMs%2F5GC0400%2D5GC0599%2F5GC000532%20%2D%20UL%202x2%20SU%20MIMO%2FSimulations%5Freports&FolderCTID=0x012000F0A0A3BA325F7648AD307E6959BA7376>

[CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA]

---

#### 5.5.6.2.3 SRS DTX detection

**5.5.6.2.3.0-2**  (ID: `12717019`)

SRS DTX detection
5G-L1-UL performs detection (presence vs non-presence hypothesis) of the SRS within the frequency domain samples, the so-called discontinuous transmission (DTX). The detection is based on a threshold detector targeting 0.5% of False Alarm. The SRS DTX detection algorithm, based on 'Antenna-wise processing', is described in section '2.6.6 SRS DTX Detection' of the 5Gmax algorithm specification ([11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The threshold is a function of the number of SRS PRB, the number of SRS ports, the number of RX streams and the number of combs. Thresholds are tabulated (as a function of SRS PRB, SRS ports and RX streams) in Tables 2.149-2.152 for the case comb2 and Tables 2.153-2.156 for the case comb4, respectively. Thresholds for non-tabulated cases are derived from tabulated cases. Refer to section '2.6.6 SRS DTX Detection' of the 5Gmax algorithm specification ([11459270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fA0LxfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the aforementioned tables.

The binary DTX decision (i.e. DTX or nonDTX) is forward to 5G-L2-PS in the messages *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs.*

[CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA] Shall be also supported in Odin L1 HW. [End CB012115-SR-IA, CB012115-SR-JA, CB012115-SR-LA]

---

## 5.5.9 SRS capacity

### 5.5.9.0-2 SRS capacity In this section, SRS capacity stands for the maximum number of SRS detections (i.e., from IQ samples to L1 measurements) per subcell and per slot. Depending on the platform, aperiodic and periodic SRS types are supported. In the same symbol and for periodic SRS, SU-MIMO and BM calculations are allowed. (ID: 11465426)

### 5.5.9.1 SRS capacity for SU-MIMO (aperiodic SRS)

**5.5.9.1.0-1**  (ID: `11465435`)

SRS capacity for SU-MIMO (aperiodic SRS)
Number of UEs per sub-band is conveyed:

* by the IE numOfUes in srsSuMimoStruct  (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_243) srsSuMimo structure (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_244\_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_240 5G\_L1\_IF\_241\_replaced([11514379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));
* by the IE numOfUes in UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_251 5G\_L1\_IF\_253\_replaced([11514446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PcfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

### 5.5.9.2 SRS capacity for SU-MIMO (periodic SRS)

#### 5.5.9.2.0-1 SRS capacity for SU-MIMO (periodic SRS) Check section 5G_L1_15536_replaced( 11465479 ) SRS combined capacity for SU-MIMO + BM for capacity values. (ID: 11465474)

### 5.5.9.3 SRS capacity for BM (Wideband Beamforming) + SU-MIMO (periodic SRS)

#### 5.5.9.3.0-1 SRS capacity for BM (Wideband Beamforming) + SU-MIMO (periodic SRS) For capacity purposes, we define an L1 BM resource as reception of the SRS signal using a cyclic shift of a comb of a subband. For a given SRS configuration (c-SRS, b-SRS), an L1 BM resource is completely defined by the triplet (srsBmSubbandId, transmissionCombId, BmCyclicHsifts) from srsBm structure in UlData_SrsReceiveReq (see 5G_L1_IF_252_replaced( 11514409 )). (ID: 11465483)

#### 5.5.9.3.1 Loki HW

**5.5.9.3.1.0-4**  (ID: `11465512`)

Loki HW
When both SU-MIMO and BM UEs are active in a cell, the following capacity value are used:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  |  |  |  | Capacity value (per cell per SRS symbol) |  |  |  |
| Frame structure | SRS Delay budget (ms) | SRS Processing budget per cell (μs) | Cells per Half Thor | Subband size (PRBs) | SU-MIMO case | BM case | mixed SU-MIMO+BM case (resources are pooled within a cell) |  |
| Max Num of SU-MIMO UEs (Note 3) | Max Num of L1 BM resource | Baseline target Num of SU-MIMO UEs (Note 3) | Max Num of L1 BM resource |  |  |  |  |  |
| 5GC001070 | 1 | 2000 | 3 | >=4 | 8 | 136 when pSRSBwvAct = false, 16 or 30 or 50 when pSRSBwvAct = True (Note 6) | 2 | 136 when pSRSBwvAct = false, 16 or 30 or 50 when pSRSBwvAct = True (Note 6) |
| 5GC001208 | 1.5 | 3000 | 3 | >=4 | 8 | 136 | 4 | 136 |
| 5GC001116 | 1.785 | 3570 | 3 | >=4 | 8 | 272 or 304 when pSRSBwvAct = false, 136 when pSRSBWVAct = True (Note 7) | 6 | 272 or 304 when pSRSBwvAct = false, 136 when pSRSBWVAct = True (Note 7) |
| CB008406 | 1 | 2000 | 3 | >=4 | 8 | 136 when pSRSBwvAct = false, 16 or 30 or 50 when pSRSBwvAct = True (Note 6) | 2 | 136 when pSRSBwvAct = false, 16 or 30 or 50 when pSRSBwvAct = True (Note 6) |
| [CB009422-B] CB009422 [End CB009422-B] | 1 |  | 3 | >=4 | 8 | 136 when pSRSBwvAct = false, 16 or 30 or 50 when pSRSBwvAct = True (Note 6) | 2 | 136 when pSRSBwvAct = false, 16 or 30 or 50 when pSRSBwvAct = True (Note 6) |

SRS Delay budget:  time from first NDM SRS job triggering to next UL slot start boundary. Also, SRS Delay Budget=SRS Processing budget/numberOfAllocatedDSPCores.

SRS Processing budget: time to process I/Q samples and send response to L2PS with 1 allocated DSP core.

numberOfAllocatedDSPCores=2. Up to 28 DSP cores can be used (shared by all cells)

SU-MIMO case: only SU-MIMO UEs are allocated in a particular SRS symbol. No BM processing.

BM case: only L1 BM resources present in a particular SRS symbol. No SU-MIMO calculations.

Note:

1. Minimal SRS subband size is 4 PRB for comb2 and 8 for comb4, respectively. For larger SRS subband size (e.g., 8PRB, 16PRB), the maximum number of L1 BM resource is limited by both L1 capacity and SRS configuration. For example, (272/8) subbands \* 2 combs \* 4 cyclic shifts \* 1 symbol = 272 BM resources.
2. Different delay budgets for different frame structures lead to different SRS capacity results.
3. SRS capacity splits into two parts. The first part is dedicated for SU MIMO case while the second part is reserved for both SU MIMO and BM cases (mixed case). From E2E point of view, the maximum number of SU MIMO UEs (RI/PMI for an 2 SRS AP UE) is always 8 regardless of frame structure and SRS configuration. See max number of SU-MIMO UEs column. However, the capacity of the first part (SU MIMO case only) is defined in baseline target num of SU-MIMO UEs column. Taking frame structure 5GC001070 for example, baseline target number of SU MIMO UEs is just 2 and the other 6 UEs shall consume the capacity reserved for both SU MIMO and BM cases (mixed case). This is achieved by the relationship 1 SU-MIMO UE = 6 L1 BM resources.
4. CP and L2PS ensure that L1 capacity numbers are never exceeded. The maximum capacity of NDM SRS for L1 pool is still 3 cells. In case of more than 3 cells, NDM SRS are divided into two cell groups and distributed in special slots according to the cell group. Look also 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_5804.
5. In case of short term subband beamforming is activated (pSrsBwvAct = True in 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), half comb SRS resources will be reserved for it. Only the other half resource can be used for long term BF. Refer to 5G\_UP\_3297 and 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_6070.
6. When bwvSubbandSize >= 8 PRBs (5G\_L1\_IF\_14862\_replaced([11513497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), value is 50. When bwvSubbandSize = 4 PRBs and numPrbPerWideband <= 8 PRBs (5G\_L1\_IF\_14862\_replaced([11513497](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), value is 30. When bwvSubbandSize = 4 PRBs and numPrbPerWideband ! = 8 PRBs, value is 16.
7. When pSrsBwvAct = True (5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), value is 136. When pSrsBwvAct = False and numPrbPerSubband = 8 or 16 PRBs (5G\_L1\_IF\_14077\_replaced([11513492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), value is 272. When pSrsBwvAct = False and numPrbPerSubband = 4 PRBs (5G\_L1\_IF\_14077\_replaced([11513492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxIxfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), value is 304.

---

#### 5.5.9.3.2 Thor HW

**5.5.9.3.2.0-4**  (ID: `11465540`)

Thor HW
When both SU-MIMO and BM UEs are active in a cell, the following capacity value are used:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  |  |  |  | Capacity value (per cell per SRS symbol) |  |  |  |
| Frame structure | SRS Delay budget (ms) | SRS Processing budget per cell (μs) | Cells per Half Thor | Subband size (PRBs) | SU-MIMO case | BM case | mixed SU-MIMO+BM case (resources are pooled within a cell) |  |
| Max Num of SU-MIMO UEs (Note 3) | Max Num of L1 BM resource | Baseline target Num of SU-MIMO UEs (Note 3) | Max Num of L1 BM resource |  |  |  |  |  |
| 5GC001070 | 1 | 2000 | 3 | >=4 | 8 | When pSRSBwvAct = Fase: 136 When pSRSBwvAct = True: 80 | 2 | When pSRSBwvAct = Fase: 136 When pSRSBwvAct = True: 80 |
| 5GC001208 | 1.5 | 3000 | 3 | >=4 | 8 | 136 | 4 | 136 |
| 5GC001116 | 1.785 | 3570 | 3 | >=4 | 8 | 304 | 4 | 304 |
| CB008406 | 1 | 2000 | 3 | >=4 | 8 | When pSRSBwvAct = Fase: 136 When pSRSBwvAct = True: 80 | 2 | When pSRSBwvAct = Fase: 136 When pSRSBwvAct = True: 80 |
| [CB009422-B] CB009422 [End CB009422-B] | 1 |  | 3 | >=4 | 8 | When pSRSBwvAct = Fase: 136 When pSRSBwvAct = True: up to 80 for Comb 2 and 4 | 2 | When pSRSBwvAct = Fase: 136 When pSRSBwvAct = True: 80 |

SRS Delay budget:  time from first NDSM SRS job triggering to next UL slot start boundary. Also, SRS Delay Budget=SRS Processing budget/numberOfAllocatedDSPCores.

SRS Processing budget: time to process I/Q samples and send response to L2PS with 1 allocated DSP core.

numberOfAllocatedDSPCores=2. Up to 28 DSP cores can be used (shared by all cells)

SU-MIMO case: only SU-MIMO UEs are allocated in a particular SRS symbol. No BM processing.

BM case: only L1 BM resources present in a particular SRS symbol. No SU-MIMO calculations.

Note:

1. Minimal SRS subband size is 4 PRB for comb2 and 8 for comb4, respectively. For larger SRS subband size (e.g., 8PRB, 16PRB), the maximum number of L1 BM resource is limited by both L1 capacity and SRS configuration. For example, (272/8) subbands \* 2 combs \* 4 cyclic shifts \* 1 symbol = 272 BM resources.
2. Different delay budgets for different frame structures lead to different SRS capacity results.
3. SRS capacity splits into two parts. The first part is dedicated for SU MIMO case, while the second part is reserved for both SU MIMO and BM cases (mixed case). From E2E point of view, the maximum number of SU MIMO UEs (RI/PMI for an 2 SRS AP UE) is always 8 regardless of frame structure and SRS configuration. See max number of SU-MIMO UEs column. However, the capacity of the first part (SU MIMO case only) is defined in baseline target num of SU-MIMO UEs column. Taking frame structure 5GC001070 for example, baseline target number of SU MIMO UEs is just 2 and the other 6 UEs shall consume the capacity reserved for both SU MIMO and BM cases (mixed case). This is achieved by the relationship 1 SU-MIMO UE = 6 L1 BM resources.
4. CP and L2PS ensure that L1 capacity numbers are never exceeded. In case NDM SRS Pooling activated, the maximum capacity of NDM SRS per L1 pool is still 3 cells. If more than 3 cells, NDM SRS are divided into two cell groups and distributed in special slots according to the cell group. Look also 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_5804.
5. In case of short term subband beamforming is activated (pSrsBwvAct = True in 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), half comb SRS resources will be reserved for it. Only the other half resource can be used for long term BF. Refer to 5G\_UP\_3297 and 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_6070.
6. In case NDM SRS Pooling deactivated: for L1 normal pool size, maximum capacity of NDM SRS per L1 pool is maximum capacity per cell \* 3 (cells), [PR809280] for L1 large pool size (one L1 pool with 3 suppools or 4 subpools), maximum capacity of NDM SRS per L1 pool is maximum capacity per cell \* 6 (cells) [End PR809280].

---

### 5.5.9.4 SRS capacity for Subband Beamforming

#### 5.5.9.4.0-1 SRS capacity for Subband Beamforming NDM SRS capacity for short term subband beamforming is defined as per subcell per slot. (ID: 11465548)

#### 5.5.9.4.1 Loki HW

**5.5.9.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `11465570`)

Loki HW
When pSRSBwvAct = True (5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the NDM SRS capacity for short term subband beamforming is as below:

* 2 UEs for one single SRS symbol and 2\*3 = 6 per L1 pool.
* Up to 6 CS processing capability (I.e., 3 2T4R wideband UEs or 6 1T4R wideband UEs) for BF subband size >= 8 PRBs per subcell per slot and 18 CS processing capability per L1 pool.
* Up to 4 CS processing capability (I.e., 2 2T4R wideband UEs or 4 1T4R wideband UEs) for BF subband size = 4 PRBs per subcell per slot and 12 CS processing capability per L1 pool.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Frame structure | Comb | BF subband Size - PRBs | max CS per slot per cell | total CS per UL Pool | max numOf BF Subband UE to calc weight per Cell per Slot | max Total numOf BF Subband UE to calc weight per UL Pool per Slot |
| 5GC001208 5GC001116 5GC001070 CB008406 | 2 | 4 | 4 | 12 | 2 | 6 |
| >= 8 | 4 | 12 | 2 | 6 |  |  |
| 4 | 4 | 4 | 12 | 2 | 6 |  |
| >= 8 | 4 | 12 | 3 | 9 |  |  |

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Frame structure | Comb | BF subband Size - PRBs | max CS per slot per cell | total CS per UL Pool | max numOf BF Subband UE to calc weight per Cell per Slot | max Total numOf BF Subband UE to calc weight per UL Pool per Slot |
| 5GC001208 5GC001116 | 2 | 4 | 4 | 18 | 2 | 6 |
| >= 8 | 4 | 18 | 2 | 6 |  |  |
| 4 | 4 | 4 | 18 | 2 | 6 |  |
| >= 8 | 6 4 | 18 | 3 | 9 |  |  |
| 5GC001070 CB008406 [CB009422-B] CB009422 [End CB009422-B] | 2 | 4 | 4 | 12 | 2 | 6 |
| >= 8 | 4 | 12 | 2 | 6 |  |  |
| 4 | 4 | 4 | 12 | 2 | 6 |  |
| >= 8 | 4 | 12 | 2 | 6 |  |  |

Note:

1. half Comb SRS resource is reserved for short term subband beamforming and the other half Comb SRS resource is used for long term beamforming. L1 processing capability also splits into LT BF and ST BF. Refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_6070.
2. CP and L2PS ensure that L1 capacity numbers are never exceeded.

---

**SRS Delay budget:  time from first NDM SRS job triggering to next UL slot start boundary.**

Rationale of SRS delay budget in case of C4S: since no other channels, 5G-L1-UL (BB) can use the full time until the first symbol of receiving NDM SRS in Downlink Slot for the subsequent NDM SRS steam.

before the first symbol of receving NDM SRS in Downlink Slot for the subsequent NDM SRS steam.

The maximum number of SU-MIMO UEs (PMI/RI for an 2 SRS AP UE) is 4 (per cell per SRS symbol) regardless of frame structure and configuration.

CP and L2PS ensure that L1 capacity numbers are never exceeded.

Only one symbol per slot can be used for SRS with SU-MIMO purpose.

Maximum capacity of precise positioning UEs for L1 pool is maximum capacity per cell \* number of Cells per L1 pool.

**Note:** For multiple sequenceId(s) on the same symbol/slot/subcell, see [12874461: Multiple sequenceId(s) on the same symbol](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_6irooa_ZEfCkGp-OQxzvvQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).\*\*\*\*

**Note: The capacity will be updated once SRS benchmark results are available.**

## 5.5.10 Robustness
